<div id="page-803">
<h3><a name="page-803">Wednesday, February 19, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A beautiful day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/67' title='Willie Mayhew'>Willie Mayhew</a> and <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben Brumfield</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> started to <a href='../subjects/446' title='South Boston'>South Boston</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening with <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul Bennetts</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/128' title='tobacco sale'>tobacco</a> and some for <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin Smith</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> That is all the tobacco that<span class='line-break'> </span> they have to sell.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/162' title='wood cutting'>cut wood</a> all day. <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> went to see <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie Reynolds</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> has been <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>feeling bad</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to day. <a href='../subjects/7651' title='Janie Brumfield'>Janie Brumfield</a> come<span class='line-break'> </span> with <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> home to night<span class='line-break'> </span> from <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>. They are having<span class='line-break'> </span> a big time tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I had a <a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a> from <a href='../subjects/209' title='John Brumfield'>John <span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield</a> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8:30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-804">
<h3><a name="page-804">Thursday, February 20, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/13' title='cold'>colde</a> <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a>. <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/162' title='wood cutting'>cut wood</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> come from <a href='../subjects/446' title='South Boston'>South Boston</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening. He his is not feeling<span class='line-break'> </span> well tonight. He <a href='../subjects/128' title='tobacco sale'>solde</a> <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Pauls</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> to day. I don't know<span class='line-break'> </span> what it brought. He has not tolde<span class='line-break'> </span> me. <a href='../subjects/242' title='Irvin Lewis'>Irvin Lewis</a> come this morning<span class='line-break'> </span> and got my <a href='../subjects/87' title='calves'>calf</a>. I paid him<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7482' title='money'>one dollar</a> to carrie it.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> carried <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kates</a> <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chickens</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7203' title='Long Island, Virginia'>Long Island</a> this morning.  Virginia<span class='line-break'> </span> went with him.  Marvin brought<span class='line-break'> </span> Jims <a href='../subjects/370' title='pigs'>pigs</a> from <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Lewis brought them from <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a><span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to Kates today and to<span class='line-break'> </span> see <a href='../subjects/335' title='Margaret Brumfield'>Mag</a>.  She was not at home.<span class='line-break'> </span> I come home with Marvin on the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-805">
<h3><a name="page-805">Friday, February 21, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A bad day.  There was more<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/2' title='snow'>snow</a> on the ground than had<span class='line-break'> </span> bin this winter.  It is all gone<span class='line-break'> </span> to night.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr. Owen</a> &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7559' title='Board Dews'>Board Dews</a> went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7678' title='Jessie Mays'>Mr. Jessie Mays</a> <a href='../subjects/7437' title='farm sale'>sale</a>.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin<span class='line-break'> </span> Smith</a> bought <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a><span class='line-break'> </span> two <a href='../subjects/370' title='pigs'>pigs</a> to day.  He bought<span class='line-break'> </span> them from <a href='../subjects/7283' title='Bob Starkey'>Robert Starkey</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am so glad that he could <span class='line-break'> </span> get them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> is <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a> I am afraid.<span class='line-break'> </span> He is so cross.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> did not go to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a> to<span class='line-break'> </span> day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-806">
<h3><a name="page-806">Saturday, February 22, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A very <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rainy</a> day. <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/7547' title='hauling wood'>hauled</a><span class='line-break'> </span> two loads of <a href='../subjects/36' title='wood'>wood</a>. Had to quit it <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rained</a><span class='line-break'> </span> so hard. <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/162' title='wood cutting'>cut some wood</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7217' title='Glenland, Virginia'>Glenland</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to a <a href='../subjects/380' title='trustee meeting'>trustee meeting</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <a href='../subjects/52' title='Irvin Harvey'>Irvin Harvey</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come and brought us some<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chicken</a>.  We certainly did enjoy it.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I made me an <a href='../subjects/70' title='apron'>apron</a> and <a href='../subjects/182' title='mending'>mended</a><span class='line-break'> </span> some things.  I cut and <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> some rag strings to night.  <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a><span class='line-break'> </span> wound the ball for me.  She loves<span class='line-break'> </span> to wind the balls.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> There is a <a href='../subjects/314' title='thunder cloud'>thunder cloud</a> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie made some <a href='../subjects/42' title='candy'>candy</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9:10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-807">
<h3><a name="page-807">Sunday, February 23, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/7644' title='clearing land'>cleared</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> walked a round most<span class='line-break'> </span> all day.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> She is bad off with <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>colde</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am uneasy a bout her.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George Blairs</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  The young folks<span class='line-break'> </span> was gone to church.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7450' title='Otho Blair'>Otho</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/393' title='Sallie Blair'>Sallie</a> come with<span class='line-break'> </span> them home.  They had a nice<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner.  Had a <a href='../subjects/140' title='turkey'>turkey</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/240' title='cake'>cake</a>.  I enjoyed it very much.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-808">
<h3><a name="page-808">Monday, February 24, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/162' title='wood cutting'>cut</a> and <a href='../subjects/7547' title='hauling wood'>hauled some wood</a> and <a href='../subjects/7531' title='sawing'>sawed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> it this evening.  <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> has bin <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> has a bad cough.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> was there.  She was <span class='line-break'> </span> pieceing a bed <a href='../subjects/8' title='quilting'>quilt</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Brought sewing she had<span class='line-break'> </span> done for <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Well I am a sleep.  Well qu [sic]<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-809">
<h3><a name="page-809">Tuesday, February 25, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A very bad day.  <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>Rained</a> a bout<span class='line-break'> </span> all day.  Some <a href='../subjects/7680' title='fox hunters'>fox hunters</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come by here this morning.  They<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7631' title='hunting'>hunted</a> all the morning.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> don't know a bout there catching<span class='line-break'> </span> anything or not.  I guess they<span class='line-break'> </span> got wet.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> all <a href='../subjects/946' title='playing cards'>played cards</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening a while.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The boys fix up the olde<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7681' title='cotton gin'>cotton gin</a> and gined some cotton.<span class='line-break'> </span> I had intended going to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7212' title='Richmond, Virginia'>Richmond</a> to morrow but will<span class='line-break'> </span> not go.  It has <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rained</a> so much<span class='line-break'> </span> that we could hardly get to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7682' title='depot'>the depo</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I comenced a cap for <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> that she intends to give<span class='line-break'> </span> to Ella Hubard.  Josie is bad off<span class='line-break'> </span> with a <a href='../subjects/445' title='weather'>colde</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-810">
<h3><a name="page-810">Wednesday, February 26, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> started<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7212' title='Richmond, Virginia'>Richmond</a> this morning.  I have<span class='line-break'> </span> felt disapointed all day but I think<span class='line-break'> </span> it is best that I did not go.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> is<span class='line-break'> </span> bad off with <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>colde</a> so she cant<span class='line-break'> </span> hardly go.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/162' title='wood cutting'>cut wood</a> all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> went to the <a href='../subjects/44' title='mill'>mill</a> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I have done most of the work<span class='line-break'> </span> today.  <a href='../subjects/393' title='Sallie Blair'>Sallie Blair</a> commenced to <span class='line-break'> </span> teach <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a> to day.  <a href='../subjects/242' title='Irvin Lewis'>Mr Lewis</a> carried<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a>.  I heard from my<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/87' title='calves'>calf</a> to day.  It brought me $20 12/cts.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-811">
<h3><a name="page-811">Thursday, February 27, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/162' title='wood cutting'>cut wood</a> this morning.  Hauled<span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/7301' title='hay'>hay</a> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> is in <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7212' title='Richmond, Virginia'>Richmond</a> I guess.  Hope he may have<span class='line-break'> </span> a good time.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> is still<span class='line-break'> </span> bad off with <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>colde</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Jim went to the store to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/376' title='Posey Reynolds'>Posie</a> <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Reynolds</a> brought <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> from <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> She got here just after <span class='line-break'> </span> dark.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/367' title='Odie Kellie'>Odie Kellie</a> come today<span class='line-break'> </span> and got a box to send some<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chickens</a> to market.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I finished <a href='../subjects/57' title='knitting'>knitting</a> <a href='../subjects/7452' title='Ella Hubbard'>Ella Hubards</a><span class='line-break'> </span> cap to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Jim has just come home.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 11 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>

<div id="page-812">
<h3><a name="page-812">Friday, February 28, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p><a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>Rain</a> to day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/162' title='wood cutting'>cut</a> some.  The <a href='../subjects/7680' title='fox hunters'>fox hunters</a><span class='line-break'> </span> caught <a href='../subjects/7685' title='foxes'>a fox</a> this evening near<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7686' title='Mr. Edmons&apos;s'>Mr. Edmons's</a>.  They run it all day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> There is a <a href='../subjects/48' title='party'>party</a> at the <a href='../subjects/194' title='school house'>school<span class='line-break'> </span> house</a> selling boxes.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> with <a href='../subjects/183' title='Mr Mayhew'>Mr Mayhew</a> &amp; Owen. <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> got home from <a href='../subjects/7212' title='Richmond, Virginia'>Richmond</a> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> met him at <a href='../subjects/7941' title='Mr Bailiss'>Mr. Bailiss</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> is feeling some better to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie</a> has bin <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Henry has not come home yet<span class='line-break'> </span> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>

<div id="page-813">
<h3><a name="page-813">Saturday, March  1, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/162' title='wood cutting'>cut<span class='line-break'> </span> wood</a> all day.  They have gone to<span class='line-break'> </span> the store at <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/183' title='Mr Mayhew'>Mr Mayhew</a> come here tonight<span class='line-break'> </span> but did not stay as the boys<span class='line-break'> </span> was gone.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> is some better<span class='line-break'> </span> off at this time.  <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie</a> was<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a> to day.  Josie baked <a href='../subjects/170' title='pies'>pies</a><span class='line-break'> </span> for <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> today.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> went to Renan<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  Josie sent for <span class='line-break'> </span> Salmon.  This evening they went<span class='line-break'> </span> to the <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school house</a> after Sophia<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/986' title='dog'>dog</a>.  I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a><span class='line-break'> </span> a while this evening.  They were<span class='line-break'> </span> all well.  <a href='../subjects/7654' title='Eva Smith'>Eva</a> has commenced<span class='line-break'> </span> cralling.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>

<div id="page-815">
<h3><a name="page-815">Monday, March  3, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/162' title='wood cutting'>cut</a><span class='line-break'> </span> half the day in the pines.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben went this evening to a <a href='../subjects/261' title='cutting match'>cutting<span class='line-break'> </span> match</a> at <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George Blairs</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> worked on the <a href='../subjects/7246' title='orchard'>orchard</a> all<span class='line-break'> </span> day &amp; did not finish it.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> is feeling some better of her<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>colde</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7688' title='Bettie Rosser'>Bettie Rosser</a> washed for<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie to day.  She washes fine.<span class='line-break'> </span> Heard to day that <a href='../subjects/7636' title='Elsie East'>Elsie East</a> has<span class='line-break'> </span> a new boy.  I hope they get<span class='line-break'> </span> on well.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-816">
<h3><a name="page-816">Tuesday, March  4, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/162' title='wood cutting'>cut<span class='line-break'> </span> wood</a> this morning &amp; <a href='../subjects/298' title='corn shucking'>shucked some<span class='line-break'> </span> corn</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> worked on the <a href='../subjects/7246' title='orchard'>orchard</a> all day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> and went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>, got knocked in<span class='line-break'> </span> a mud hole, and had to come<span class='line-break'> </span> home to change his clothes.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Tonight <a href='../subjects/104' title='Tom Edmonds'>Tom</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7689' title='Claude Edmonds'>Claud Edmons</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come up here a few minutes <span class='line-break'> </span> to see Jim and talk a<span class='line-break'> </span> bout <a href='../subjects/7219' title='West Virginia'>West Virginia</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Jim &amp; Ben has gone to <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-817">
<h3><a name="page-817">Wednesday, March  5, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p><a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>Clear</a> this morning at five<span class='line-break'> </span> oclock then clouded up and has <span class='line-break'> </span> bin a very <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rainy</a> day. <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The men folks <a href='../subjects/298' title='corn shucking'>shucked</a> some <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7208' title='Altavista, Virginia'>Altavista</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> with his <a href='../subjects/115' title='wagon'>waggon</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and came home through the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a>.  <a href='../subjects/183' title='Mr Mayhew'>Mr Mayhew</a> is here <span class='line-break'> </span> now.  He eat <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a> with us <span class='line-break'> </span> and they are <a href='../subjects/946' title='playing cards'>playing cards</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> now.  I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a>     <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9: oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-818">
<h3><a name="page-818">Thursday, March  6, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p><a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>Cloudy</a> most of the day.  No<span class='line-break'> </span> rain yet. The men folks <a href='../subjects/162' title='wood cutting'>cut wood</a><span class='line-break'> </span> in the <a href='../subjects/65' title='woods'>woods</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a>. I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> come and eat with<span class='line-break'> </span> us. She worked some <a href='../subjects/91' title='button holes'>button holes</a><span class='line-break'> </span> in <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese Smiths</a> <a href='../subjects/9095' title='waist'>waists</a><span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I made a <a href='../subjects/418' title='canvas'>canvas</a> for <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got a <a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a> from <a href='../subjects/7921' title='Fannie Emerson'>Fanny <span class='line-break'> </span> Emerson</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 15 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-819">
<h3><a name="page-819">Friday, March  7, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p><a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>Cloudy</a> this morning.  <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>Clear</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening. <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went with<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/419' title='Travis Dews'>Mr Dews</a> to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a> after his<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a>. They had some trouble in<span class='line-break'> </span> getting it home. I do hope that<span class='line-break'> </span> they will be pleased with it.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> helped <a href='../subjects/68' title='John Hutcherson'>John Hutcherson</a> <a href='../subjects/332' title='barn raising'>raise<span class='line-break'> </span> a barn</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> &amp; the children went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> this evening. I went a<span class='line-break'> </span> few minutes then cut a mess<span class='line-break'> </span> of Salit I <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fished</a> a few<span class='line-break'> </span> minutes this evening.  Caught three<span class='line-break'> </span> minows.  No one here found it out<span class='line-break'> </span> but <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a>. I think he saw<span class='line-break'> </span> me. Josie had a <a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a> from<span class='line-break'> </span> her mother this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-820">
<h3><a name="page-820">Saturday, March  8, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day and <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>raining</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to night. The men folks <a href='../subjects/162' title='wood cutting'>cut</a> until<span class='line-break'> </span> twelve then <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> hauled<span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/11' title='tobacco stalks'>stalks</a> and <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> &amp; Ben and <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7240' title='Jim Power'>Jim Powers</a>. <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> I staid at home all the morning<span class='line-break'> </span> then Henry went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owens</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> To night Ben &amp; Marvin has<span class='line-break'> </span> gone to the <a href='../subjects/85' title='lodge'>lodge</a> at <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait<span class='line-break'> </span> Stone</a> I know they will get<span class='line-break'> </span> wet. Josie says she has never seen<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/233' title='roads'>roads</a> as bad as they were<span class='line-break'> </span> today. <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese Smith</a> has bought<span class='line-break'> </span> him a <a href='../subjects/422' title='bicycle'>bycicle</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johnson Reynolds</a> has gone to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7218' title='Norfolk, Virginia'>Norfork</a> to see <a href='../subjects/7224' title='Julia Ferguson'>Julia Fergerson</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I feel like I know how glad<span class='line-break'> </span> she will be to see him.<span class='line-break'> </span> I hope he will see <a href='../subjects/209' title='John Brumfield'>John B</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10: oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-821">
<h3><a name="page-821">Sunday, March  9, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p><a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>Cloudy</a> this morning.  <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>Clear</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  We all staid at home until<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> then <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to <a href='../subjects/419' title='Travis Dews'>Mr Dews</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to try to run his new <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> <a href='../subjects/153' title='Ren Worsham'>Wren<span class='line-break'> </span> Worsham</a> &amp; some of the children <span class='line-break'> </span> come to Marvins.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/424' title='Doris Brumfield'>Doris</a> and <a href='../subjects/7649' title='Emmett Brumfield'>Emit</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7650' title='Aubrey Brumfield'>Aubrey<span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/427' title='Floyd Reynolds'>Floyd Reynols</a> was<span class='line-break'> </span> here a while today.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We heard today that <a href='../subjects/428' title='Ola Bennett Jefferson'>Ola Jeferson</a><span class='line-break'> </span> has <a href='../subjects/7646' title='Carey James Jefferson'>a daughter</a><span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-822">
<h3><a name="page-822">Monday, March 10, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The men folks<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/162' title='wood cutting'>cut wood</a> until twelve.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> carried <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> to <a href='../subjects/7203' title='Long Island, Virginia'>Long Island</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening,  Her mother met her<span class='line-break'> </span> and they started for <a href='../subjects/7219' title='West Virginia'>W Virginia</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/982' title='Max Carr'>Max Carr</a> was going with them part<span class='line-break'> </span> of the way.  <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> went to <span class='line-break'> </span> Marvins this evening. I went and <span class='line-break'> </span> come with them back.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went to school.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben says that the <a href='../subjects/233' title='roads'>roads</a> is very<span class='line-break'> </span> bad.  <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johnson</a> and <a href='../subjects/7386' title='Christine Reynolds'>Christinia<span class='line-break'> </span> Reynols</a> come from <a href='../subjects/7218' title='Norfolk, Virginia'>Norfork</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening. <a href='../subjects/7497' title='Reuben Reynolds'>Reubin</a> met<span class='line-break'> </span> them at <a href='../subjects/7203' title='Long Island, Virginia'>the Island</a><span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-823">
<h3><a name="page-823">Tuesday, March 11, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/274' title='cool'>cool</a> <a href='../subjects/61' title='wind'>windy</a> day the men<span class='line-break'> </span> folks put on the <a href='../subjects/418' title='canvas'>canvas</a> for their<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/238' title='plantbeds'>plant beds</a> this morning and <a href='../subjects/162' title='wood cutting'>cut</a> &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/985' title='mauling'>mauled</a> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come a few minutes to day.  She eat<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> with us.  She brought me<span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/7690' title='hominy'>homony</a>.  I went with her<span class='line-break'> </span> part the way home.  I carried <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> looked after them while I<span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/376' title='Posey Reynolds'>Posie Reynolds</a> and got some<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7379' title='turnips'>turnip salit</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We heard to day that<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7691' title='Tom Lumpkins'>Tom  Lumpkins</a> and <a href='../subjects/7692' title='Tom Johnson'>Tom Johnson</a><span class='line-break'> </span> was <a href='../subjects/96' title='death'>dead</a>, one of them at <a href='../subjects/973' title='Danville, Virginia'>Danville</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and one at <a href='../subjects/7693' title='Newport News, Virginia'>New Port News</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johnson Reynolds</a> went to Danville<span class='line-break'> </span> to be at Lumpkins <a href='../subjects/118' title='burial'>burial</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> got a <a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a> from <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie</a> telling <span class='line-break'> </span> him that <a href='../subjects/7694' title='Mr Walker'>Mr Walker</a> is very<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Jim &amp; Ben walked over<span class='line-break'> </span> to the store at <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/242' title='Irvin Lewis'>Mr Lewis</a> was not there so they<span class='line-break'> </span> come home soon and went to bed.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I finished pickin the 1919 crop of <a href='../subjects/7695' title='cotton'>cotton</a> to night.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-824">
<h3><a name="page-824">Wednesday, March 12, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/445' title='weather'>colde</a> morning.  <a href='../subjects/3' title='ice'>Ice</a> plenty by<span class='line-break'> </span> twelve.  It was pleasant.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The men folks <a href='../subjects/298' title='corn shucking'>shucked some corn</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and hauled it up.  Hauled the storks[sic]<span class='line-break'> </span> and cut them up.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a> after <a href='../subjects/113' title='oil'>oil</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> went with <span class='line-break'> </span> him.  Ben had a <a href='../subjects/7696' title='postcard'>card</a> from<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a>.  She was on her way<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7219' title='West Virginia'>W Va</a>.  I hope she may<span class='line-break'> </span> have a good time.  We certainly<span class='line-break'> </span> do miss her &amp; will be so glad <span class='line-break'> </span> when she gets back.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-825">
<h3><a name="page-825">Thursday, March 13, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7547' title='hauling wood'>hauled wood</a>.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> cleaned up the <span class='line-break'> </span> brush in the <a href='../subjects/7246' title='orchard'>orchard</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> and I went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  I cut some <a href='../subjects/284' title='salad'>salit</a><span class='line-break'> </span> as I come home.  Marvin was<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowin</a>; the first time the land<span class='line-break'> </span> has bin dry enough in a <span class='line-break'> </span> long time.  Marvin &amp; <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a> yesterday.  They<span class='line-break'> </span> bought several things.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate</a> stayed with the little children<span class='line-break'> </span> while they were gone.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-826">
<h3><a name="page-826">Friday, March 14, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> <a href='../subjects/274' title='cool'>cool</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> fixed up the <a href='../subjects/7697' title='grape vines'>grape vines</a> at the <span class='line-break'> </span> garage and plowed over his<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>potatoe</a> patch.  <a href='../subjects/7688' title='Bettie Rosser'>Bettie Rosser</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> here today.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/419' title='Travis Dews'>Mr Dews</a> carried his <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a> to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben had a <a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a> from <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a>.  She<span class='line-break'> </span> wants to come home tomorrow.<span class='line-break'> </span> I wont be surprised if there is<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/2' title='snow'>snow</a> by morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lee</a> is in <a href='../subjects/973' title='Danville, Virginia'>Danville</a> with his<span class='line-break'> </span> last <a href='../subjects/128' title='tobacco sale'>tobacco</a>.  <a href='../subjects/367' title='Odie Kellie'>Otie Kellie</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> several others went to <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a><span class='line-break'> </span> today.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> has bin in<span class='line-break'> </span> doors all day today.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-827">
<h3><a name="page-827">Saturday, March 15, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>Cloudy all day &amp; rain<span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.  The men folks <a href='../subjects/298' title='corn shucking'>shucked<span class='line-break'> </span> some corn</a> this morning &amp; <a href='../subjects/7547' title='hauling wood'>hauled</a><span class='line-break'> </span> up the <a href='../subjects/11' title='tobacco stalks'>stalks</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7203' title='Long Island, Virginia'>the <span class='line-break'> </span> Island</a>.  Jim went on to <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben went to meet <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> He <a href='../subjects/158' title='telephones'>phoned</a> home that she had<span class='line-break'> </span> not come to <a href='../subjects/7211' title='Cedar Forest, Virginia'>Cedar Forest</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> He is down there somewhere<span class='line-break'> </span> now.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  He come home &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> got in the wood for to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We <a href='../subjects/131' title='feeding'>fed</a> the <a href='../subjects/133' title='horses'>horses</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cows</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/370' title='pigs'>pigs</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/87' title='calves'>calves</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chickens</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7698' title='dogs'>dogs</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> has bad <a href='../subjects/297' title='colds'>colds</a><span class='line-break'> </span> tonight and I am very sorry a<span class='line-break'> </span> bout it.  <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia</a> come to see me<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  I was glad that <span class='line-break'> </span> she come but was sorry to see<span class='line-break'> </span> [her]go home in the rain.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I am so afraid that something<span class='line-break'> </span> bad has happened to <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Car</a><span class='line-break'> </span> or Josie or both.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-828">
<h3><a name="page-828">Sunday, March 16, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day.  No rain.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7211' title='Cedar Forest, Virginia'>Cedar Forest</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning to meet <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a>.  She staid<span class='line-break'> </span> at <a href='../subjects/7208' title='Altavista, Virginia'>Altavista</a> last night on her<span class='line-break'> </span> way from <a href='../subjects/7219' title='West Virginia'>W Va</a>.  I think she had<span class='line-break'> </span> a good time and was glad to get<span class='line-break'> </span> home.  The children was so glad to<span class='line-break'> </span> see her and all the rest of us was<span class='line-break'> </span> glad.  There has not bin much<span class='line-break'> </span> traveling as the <a href='../subjects/233' title='roads'>roads</a> is so bad.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a few<span class='line-break'> </span> minutes this evening.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> was<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/81' title='complaining'>complaining</a> of the <a href='../subjects/375' title='headache'>head ache</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Hope she will be well soon.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8:30</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-829">
<h3><a name="page-829">Monday, March 17, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A partly <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> hauled <a href='../subjects/11' title='tobacco stalks'>tobacco<span class='line-break'> </span> stalks</a> and <a href='../subjects/298' title='corn shucking'>shucked</a> two shocks <span class='line-break'> </span> of corn. Ben went to the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/44' title='mill'>mill</a> got home after dark. <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> come down here <span class='line-break'> </span> a while. I went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> a few minutes <span class='line-break'> </span> then cut some salit. <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> staid at home all <span class='line-break'> </span> day. <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> tried to ride <span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/7222' title='tricycle'>tricicle</a> nearly all day. <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8092' title='Sallie Strange'>Miss Salie Strange</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7652' title='Effie Brumfield Cundiff'>Effie Brumfield</a> went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/67' title='Willie Mayhew'>Mr Willie Mayhews</a> tonight. <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a> to <span class='line-break'> </span> day.   9 oclock. </p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-830">
<h3><a name="page-830">Tuesday, March 18, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Had a hard rain<span class='line-break'> </span> last night.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to meet<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> this morning.  They helped<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> <a href='../subjects/332' title='barn raising'>raise a stable</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> We all was at <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie Reynols</a> was there.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> sent me some<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7379' title='turnips'>turnip salit</a> by <a href='../subjects/52' title='Irvin Harvey'>Irvin</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7649' title='Emmett Brumfield'>Emmit Brumfield</a> come with<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/325' title='Paul Smith'>Paul Smith</a> home this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/195' title='Henry Blair'>Henry Blair</a> is here tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> They are <a href='../subjects/946' title='playing cards'>playing cards</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> has a bad <a href='../subjects/7699' title='cough'>cough</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-831">
<h3><a name="page-831">Wednesday, March 19, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> <a href='../subjects/274' title='cool'>cool</a> day.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> helped to <a href='../subjects/332' title='barn raising'>rais a barn</a><span class='line-break'> </span> for <a href='../subjects/352' title='Jim Doss'>Mr Doss</a>.  He come home <span class='line-break'> </span> for <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr. Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> worked on<span class='line-break'> </span> one thing an other all day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I staid at <span class='line-break'> </span> home all day.  <a href='../subjects/7701' title='Bettie Davis'>Bettie Davis</a><span class='line-break'> </span> washed here to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a> to day.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> and her<span class='line-break'> </span> three babies come down this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  I was glad to see <span class='line-break'> </span> them.  I am so sorry for<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie.  She worries so and<span class='line-break'> </span> does have so much to do she<span class='line-break'> </span> dont know what to do first.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Jim &amp; Ben &amp; <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> worked <span class='line-break'> </span> on <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> <a href='../subjects/7310' title='pump'>pump</a> and got<span class='line-break'> </span> it to work this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-832">
<h3><a name="page-832">Thursday, March 20, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/61' title='wind'>windy</a> day and a little<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a>.  <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> all day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/7702' title='ditching'>ditched</a> some.  Ben went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a> twice after <a href='../subjects/7703' title='plow fixtures'>plow fixtures</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/205' title='Cordie Blair'>Cordie Blair</a> come a little while.<span class='line-break'> </span> She wanted <a href='../subjects/7704' title='flower bulbs'>flower bulbs</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia Blair</a> come as far as<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I went up<span class='line-break'> </span> there.  <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> come to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a little while.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I cut some <a href='../subjects/284' title='salad'>salit</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I want to write to <a href='../subjects/7672' title='Sarah Emerson'>Sarah</a> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-833">
<h3><a name="page-833">Friday, March 21, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/279' title='beautiful'>beautiful</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>planted</a> <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>potatoes</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7265' title='onions'>onions</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/355' title='peas'>peas</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and helped some.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I made some <a href='../subjects/7477' title='soap'>soap</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  This morning I cut<span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/284' title='salad'>salit</a> and carried<span class='line-break'> </span> it to <a href='../subjects/349' title='Minnie Owen'>Mrs Owen</a>.  We had<span class='line-break'> </span> salit for <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I cut that<span class='line-break'> </span> yesterday.  Josie cut salit to<span class='line-break'> </span> day for tomorrow.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> played out<span class='line-break'> </span> nearly all day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-834">
<h3><a name="page-834">Saturday, March 22, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>Cloudy most of the day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>planted</a> <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>potatoes</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> carried stalks to the <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cows</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> &amp; got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I washed a little.  I made the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/91' title='button holes'>button holes</a> in <a href='../subjects/222' title='Hazel Smith'>Hazel Smiths</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7706' title='cloak'>cloak</a> and carried it home.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> was busy fixin for<span class='line-break'> </span> tomorrow.  She is thinkin of going <span class='line-break'> </span> to meeting tomorrow.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7972' title='Lucius Gravely'>Lucius Gravely</a> come here tonight<span class='line-break'> </span> to go with Ben to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to night.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> carried<span class='line-break'> </span> them.  The lights on <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>Bens car</a><span class='line-break'> </span> would not work.  Josie and the<span class='line-break'> </span> children has all gone to bed.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-835">
<h3><a name="page-835">Sunday, March 23, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  We all staid <span class='line-break'> </span> at home and eat <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> We had <a href='../subjects/296' title='fried chicken'>fried chicken</a> for dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a>, <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> and I went to <a href='../subjects/7240' title='Jim Power'>Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> Powers</a>.  The first time I have<span class='line-break'> </span> bin on a <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a> this year.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin Smiths</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> was at <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/326' title='Fred Hutcherson'>Fred</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/327' title='Irvin Hutcherson'>Irvin Hutcherson</a> come<span class='line-break'> </span> here to day.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> was very<span class='line-break'> </span> glad.  I guess they had a good<span class='line-break'> </span> time.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-836">
<h3><a name="page-836">Monday, March 24, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> half<span class='line-break'> </span> the day then carried <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>the<span class='line-break'> </span> baby</a> and I to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a>.  They <span class='line-break'> </span> went to Strait Stone and I stoped<span class='line-break'> </span> at the <a href='../subjects/357' title='creek'>branch</a> and <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fished</a> while<span class='line-break'> </span> they were gone.  I did not catch but<span class='line-break'> </span> one fish.  We come home and<span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7581' title='Murphist Harvey'>Murphist Harvey</a><span class='line-break'> </span> was there at work on their <a href='../subjects/7609' title='house'>house</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7709' title='Jim White'>Jim White</a> washed the <a href='../subjects/7246' title='orchard'>apple<span class='line-break'> </span> trees</a> to day.  I think he has done<span class='line-break'> </span> a faithful days work and a nice<span class='line-break'> </span> job.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Today one year a go <a href='../subjects/23' title='Charles Brumfield'>Charles <span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield</a> was <a href='../subjects/118' title='burial'>buried</a>.  Don't know <span class='line-break'> </span> how soon it will be some of<span class='line-break'> </span> the rest of the family.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8:30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-837">
<h3><a name="page-837">Tuesday, March 25, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The men folks<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> nearly all day<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> and <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lees</a> today and <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a>ried a <a href='../subjects/986' title='dog'>dog</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George</a> Blains<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening. <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> &amp; Franklin<span class='line-break'> </span> started to go with me but<span class='line-break'> </span> Franklin would not walk<span class='line-break'> </span> so Josie and the baby stopped<span class='line-break'> </span> at <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Marvin went to [Altavista]<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning for <a href='../subjects/171' title='lumber'>lumber</a> but<span class='line-break'> </span> could not get it.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Edna untied my shoes to<span class='line-break'> </span> night. Franklin has a very <span class='line-break'> </span> bad <a href='../subjects/13' title='cold'>cold</a> tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 o'clock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-838">
<h3><a name="page-838">Wednesday, March 26, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/7710' title='grubbing'>grubed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> all day. <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> &amp; I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>. Josie baked<span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/240' title='cake'>cake</a> and <a href='../subjects/160' title='tea cakes'>tea cakes</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> carried me to <a href='../subjects/7206' title='White Falls, Virginia'>White<span class='line-break'> </span> Falls</a>. <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> and the children<span class='line-break'> </span> went as far as <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kates</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am so glad to get to go.<span class='line-break'> </span> When I got home <a href='../subjects/206' title='Nettie Blair'>Nettie</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/39' title='Helen Brumfield'>Hellen</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/1630' title='Virginia Harvey'>Virginia</a> were here. I was <span class='line-break'> </span> glad that they came.<span class='line-break'> </span> I had a <a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a> from <a href='../subjects/7224' title='Julia Ferguson'>Julia<span class='line-break'> </span> Furgerson</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am always glad to hear<span class='line-break'> </span> from her.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 o'clock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-839">
<h3><a name="page-839">Thursday, March 27, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rainy</a> day most of the time<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> tonight and the <a href='../subjects/61' title='wind'>wind</a> is<span class='line-break'> </span> blowing. <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> carried <a href='../subjects/1630' title='Virginia Harvey'>Virginia</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7711' title='Helen'>Helling</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/206' title='Nettie Blair'>Nettie</a> as far as<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kates</a>. It <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rained</a> so hard they<span class='line-break'> </span> stopped at Kates.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> set by the <a href='../subjects/14' title='fire'>fire</a> all that<span class='line-break'> </span> we could. <a href='../subjects/244' title='Mrs Mayhew'>Mrs Mayhew</a> came<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening and wanted Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7531' title='sawing'>saw</a> some <a href='../subjects/36' title='wood'>wood</a> for him.<span class='line-break'> </span> I do hope the wind won't<span class='line-break'> </span> blow to hard all night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 o'clock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-840">
<h3><a name="page-840">Friday, March 28, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>colde</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/162' title='wood cutting'>cut</a>.  <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/7547' title='hauling wood'>hauled</a> some.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/67' title='Willie Mayhew'>Willie Mayhews</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/162' title='wood cutting'>cut some wood</a> and to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/262' title='Tom Peak'>Tom Peaks</a>. To night Ben &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> Jim has gone to <a href='../subjects/7712' title='Lewis&apos;s Store'>Lewis's Store</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sowed</a> on<span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/8' title='quilting'>quilt</a> that I commenced<span class='line-break'> </span> some time a go.  I finished to<span class='line-break'> </span> day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> come a few <span class='line-break'> </span> minutes this morning.  She come<span class='line-break'> </span> on <a href='../subjects/349' title='Minnie Owen'>Mrs Owens</a> <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a> &amp; walked <span class='line-break'> </span> home.  Josie went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a><span class='line-break'> </span> a little while this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> cut his finger to night<span class='line-break'> </span> and fainted while <a href='../subjects/230' title='Lizzie Bennett'>his mother</a><span class='line-break'> </span> wrapped it up.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9:10 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-841">
<h3><a name="page-841">Saturday, March 29, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A bright <a href='../subjects/274' title='cool'>cool</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7531' title='sawing'>sawed</a> <a href='../subjects/36' title='wood'>wood</a> for <a href='../subjects/7713' title='Mr Peak'>Mr Peak</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> set up wood in the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/65' title='woods'>woods</a>.  <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I set <span class='line-break'> </span> by the <a href='../subjects/14' title='fire'>fire</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/325' title='Paul Smith'>Paul<span class='line-break'> </span> Smith</a> come and ask Ben to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/953' title='hair cutting'>cut their hair</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7561' title='Gladys Brumfield'>Gladis Brumfield</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7714' title='Myrtle Shelton'>Myrtle Shelton</a> come<span class='line-break'> </span> and got some flowers.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben put a <a href='../subjects/7572' title='yoke'>yoke</a> on the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cow</a> this evening.  I hope<span class='line-break'> </span> she wont kill her self with<span class='line-break'> </span> it.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-842">
<h3><a name="page-842">Sunday, March 30, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/7715' title='changeable'>changeable</a> day.  Some times<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7716' title='sunshine'>sunshine</a> and then <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a>.  It is raining<span class='line-break'> </span> now.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> and I staid at home all<span class='line-break'> </span> day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; family went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7717' title='Mr Powers'>Mr Powers</a>.  We had <a href='../subjects/170' title='pies'>pies</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7622' title='sausage'>sausage</a> for <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I intended to<span class='line-break'> </span> go to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> but they were<span class='line-break'> </span> not at home this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I <a href='../subjects/7718' title='Daylight Savings Time'>turned up my clock</a> tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> I dont like that a bit<span class='line-break'> </span> but every one will have to do it.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-843">
<h3><a name="page-843">Monday, March 31, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/445' title='weather'>colde</a> <a href='../subjects/61' title='wind'>windy</a> day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> all day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> helped<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7503' title='Jim Emerson'>Jim Emerson</a> work on his <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a><span class='line-break'> </span> all day.  <a href='../subjects/349' title='Minnie Owen'>Mrs Owen</a> is <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a> did not work to<span class='line-break'> </span> day.  Heard tonight that<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8085' title='Juanita Owen'>Dr Owens baby</a> has croup.<span class='line-break'> </span> Hope she may soon get well.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> They were all well.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a><span class='line-break'> </span> was workin in his <a href='../subjects/290' title='garden'>garden</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> He is good hand in a garden.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a><span class='line-break'> </span> today.  To night Edna put her<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/199' title='stockings'>stockins</a> on some <a href='../subjects/36' title='wood'>wood</a> by the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/14' title='fire'>fire</a> and they <a href='../subjects/7699' title='cough'>cough</a> afire<span class='line-break'> </span> and burnt the feet off.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9:30 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Heard to day that <a href='../subjects/7972' title='Lucius Gravely'>Lucius<span class='line-break'> </span> Gravelys</a> wife has a daughter.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-844">
<h3><a name="page-844">Tuesday, April  1, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
