<p>A very <a href='../subjects/13' title='cold'>colde</a> <a href='../subjects/61' title='wind'>windy</a> day.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a>.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> cleaned up on the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/357' title='creek'>branch</a>.  <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a> staid at home.<span class='line-break'> </span> He has <a href='../subjects/7828' title='Benjamin Franklin Owen'>a new baby</a> born this morning<span class='line-break'> </span> at three oclock.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Betty Davis washed here today.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  She cooked <a href='../subjects/304' title='beans'>beans</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and baked <a href='../subjects/170' title='pies'>coconut pies</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I did not do much of any<span class='line-break'> </span> thing.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie went to <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  Carried some <a href='../subjects/249' title='eggs'>eggs</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and bought a few things.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> come a few<span class='line-break'> </span> minutes this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I walked with her as far<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7654' title='Eva Smith'>Carries baby</a> was<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>not well</a>.  Hope she may soon<span class='line-break'> </span> be well.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-845">
<h3><a name="page-845">Wednesday, April  2, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>colde</a> day.  There was<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/3' title='ice'>ice</a> plentiful this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> cleaned up the <a href='../subjects/357' title='creek'>branch</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> until <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a><span class='line-break'> </span> then <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr. Owen</a> plowed until<span class='line-break'> </span> night.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and got <a href='../subjects/284' title='salad'>salit</a> for dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> She got dinner.  I went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owens</a> and bathed <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7828' title='Benjamin Franklin Owen'>the little baby</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollies</a>, and <span class='line-break'> </span> got salit from <a href='../subjects/376' title='Posey Reynolds'>Posies</a> <a href='../subjects/290' title='garden'>garden</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/252' title='Mrs Hutcherson'>Mrs Hutcherson</a> was there.  She<span class='line-break'> </span> had bin to the store.  <a href='../subjects/8085' title='Juanita Owen'>Dr Owens<span class='line-break'> </span> baby</a> is very sick.  I hope she<span class='line-break'> </span> may soon be well.  <a href='../subjects/376' title='Posey Reynolds'>Posie Reynolds</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come down here this evening<span class='line-break'> </span> and got <a href='../subjects/7719' title='sycamores'>cickamore bushes</a> to<span class='line-break'> </span> plant.  I heard to day a bout<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7720' title='Clifton Reynolds, Jr.'>Cliftons boy</a>.  Jim &amp; Ben has<span class='line-break'> </span> gone to night to <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a> to get<span class='line-break'> </span> some cottens[coulters?] to work with<span class='line-break'> </span> tomorrow.  Hope they will soon be <span class='line-break'> </span> back.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-846">
<h3><a name="page-846">Thursday, April  3, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> cleaned<span class='line-break'> </span> up on the <a href='../subjects/357' title='creek'>spring branch</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> some then got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I ironed while<span class='line-break'> </span> she got the dinner.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.  I went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owens</a> and bathed <a href='../subjects/7828' title='Benjamin Franklin Owen'>the baby</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening I went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> and cut some <a href='../subjects/284' title='salad'>salit</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> We looked for <a href='../subjects/348' title='Mrs Edmonds'>Mrs Edmons</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> She did not come.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie went to see <a href='../subjects/349' title='Minnie Owen'>Mrs Owens</a><span class='line-break'> </span> baby this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-847">
<h3><a name="page-847">Friday, April  4, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day and <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a> all<span class='line-break'> </span> the evening.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> worked<span class='line-break'> </span> on the <a href='../subjects/357' title='creek'>branch</a> until it <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rained</a> so<span class='line-break'> </span> they had to quit or get wet.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> some this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning and went to the <a href='../subjects/44' title='mill'>mill</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  Guess he got<span class='line-break'> </span> wet.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I went to <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owens</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> bathed <a href='../subjects/7828' title='Benjamin Franklin Owen'>the baby</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7884' title='Willie Wooding'>Miss Willie Wooding</a> come a few<span class='line-break'> </span> minutes this morning.  She<span class='line-break'> </span> looks feeble.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a> at <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a> closed to day.  I think<span class='line-break'> </span> most every one was glad.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-848">
<h3><a name="page-848">Saturday, April  5, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/298' title='corn shucking'>shucked<span class='line-break'> </span> some corn</a> this morning &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7721' title='hauling stalks'>hauled some stalks</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben carried <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and I the <a href='../subjects/7722' title='Moons Mill'>Moons Mill</a>.  We<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fished</a> some.  Did not catch<span class='line-break'> </span> any thing that was worth<span class='line-break'> </span> having. <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  She<span class='line-break'> </span> baked <a href='../subjects/390' title='bread'>light bread</a>.  Boiled over<span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/7723' title='molasses'>molasses</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Jim &amp; Ben &amp; <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> come<span class='line-break'> </span> after us.  Reuben &amp; <a href='../subjects/325' title='Paul Smith'>Paul</a> come<span class='line-break'> </span> a few minutes.  <a href='../subjects/7497' title='Reuben Reynolds'>Reubin</a> drove<span class='line-break'> </span> up the <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cows</a> for me.  He brought<span class='line-break'> </span> me his <a href='../subjects/7724' title='photograph'>picture</a>.  I was glad<span class='line-break'> </span> to see the boys.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/153' title='Ren Worsham'>Ren Worsham</a> &amp; 4 of the <span class='line-break'> </span> children was at <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> He would of brought us part<span class='line-break'> </span> the way home if Ben had not<span class='line-break'> </span> come as soon as he did.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-849">
<h3><a name="page-849">Sunday, April  6, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> staid at home all day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got most of the <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr. Owens</a> twice.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went &amp; dressed <a href='../subjects/7828' title='Benjamin Franklin Owen'>the baby</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and come home.  Then <a href='../subjects/349' title='Minnie Owen'>Mrs Owen</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7725' title='fainting'>fainted</a> and I went back a while.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a> carried his neice home<span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lee</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7636' title='Elsie East'>Elsie</a> come and<span class='line-break'> </span> eat dinner with us.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Elsie had her new baby with<span class='line-break'> </span> her.  I think he is a fine baby.<span class='line-break'> </span> I was very glad that they<span class='line-break'> </span> came.  It is the first time<span class='line-break'> </span> that Lee has bin here this year<span class='line-break'> </span> or Elsie for that <a href='../subjects/163' title='mat'>mat</a>ter.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I have not seen or heard<span class='line-break'> </span> from <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> to day.  Hope they<span class='line-break'> </span> are all well.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went to <a href='../subjects/335' title='Margaret Brumfield'>Mag Brumfields</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  Said he had a fine time.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-850">
<h3><a name="page-850">Monday, April  7, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The men folks <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> until twelve then [?] this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owens</a>.  I <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and dodged a round most of the<span class='line-break'> </span> day.  I went to <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> a few<span class='line-break'> </span> minutes this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/205' title='Cordie Blair'>Cordie</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/206' title='Nettie Blair'>Nettie Blair</a> and <a href='../subjects/7535' title='Ada Hutcherson'>Ada<span class='line-break'> </span> Hutcherson</a> come this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> They said that <a href='../subjects/64' title='Lottie Craddock'>Lottie Craddock</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7727' title='Edith Ardena Craddock'>has a daughter</a>.  <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia Blair</a><span class='line-break'> </span> has gone up there to see her.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> caught a <a href='../subjects/7726' title='turtles'>turtle</a><span class='line-break'> </span> in the <a href='../subjects/357' title='creek'>branch</a>.  I dressed it for<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a>.  The Owen boyes has<span class='line-break'> </span> bin here most all day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-851">
<h3><a name="page-851">Tuesday, April  8, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The men folks<span class='line-break'> </span> worked on the <a href='../subjects/357' title='creek'>branch</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> comenced washin this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7688' title='Bettie Rosser'>Bettie Rosser</a> come and finished<span class='line-break'> </span> washin and washed some of<span class='line-break'> </span> the floors.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> There was a <a href='../subjects/7728' title='demonstration'>demonstration</a> of <a href='../subjects/7729' title='machinery'>machinery</a><span class='line-break'> </span> at <a href='../subjects/92' title='Mr Hutcherson'>Mr Hutchersons</a> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span> None of us went.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> and I went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7730' title='Creasy&apos;s pond'>Creasys fish pond</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> carried us.  We walked<span class='line-break'> </span> home.  We caught some little<span class='line-break'> </span> fish.  <a href='../subjects/7731' title='Mrs Millam'>Mrs Millam</a> and <a href='../subjects/7732' title='Giles'>Giles</a><span class='line-break'> </span> was  there most of the time<span class='line-break'> </span> that we were.  I was glad <span class='line-break'> </span> to be with her.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9:15 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Got a <a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a> from <a href='../subjects/7205' title='Effie Thornton Brumfield'>Effie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield to day.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-852">
<h3><a name="page-852">Wednesday, April  9, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a><span class='line-break'> </span> worked on the <a href='../subjects/357' title='creek'>branch</a> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7733' title='Lovel Witcher'>Lovel Witcher</a> come here to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr. Owens</a> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7652' title='Effie Brumfield Cundiff'>Effie Brumfield</a> and <a href='../subjects/308' title='Hugh Brumfield'>Hugh</a> and I<span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7206' title='White Falls, Virginia'>White Falls</a>.  We had <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lee<span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfields</a> <a href='../subjects/133' title='horses'>horse</a> and <a href='../subjects/268' title='buggy'>buggy</a>.  I was<span class='line-break'> </span> glad to get to go.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> and went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  Josie went to <a href='../subjects/376' title='Posey Reynolds'>Posie<span class='line-break'> </span> Reynols's</a> for <a href='../subjects/7379' title='turnips'>turnip</a> greens this<span class='line-break'> </span> mornin.  We enjoy them so much.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/376' title='Posey Reynolds'>Posie</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/409' title='Nannie Reynolds'>Nanie</a> intends startin<span class='line-break'> </span> to see <a href='../subjects/7224' title='Julia Ferguson'>Julia Ferguson</a> tomorow.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got a <a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a> from <a href='../subjects/209' title='John Brumfield'>John</a> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-853">
<h3><a name="page-853">Thursday, April 10, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The men <a href='../subjects/7736' title='hauling feed'>hauled</a><span class='line-break'> </span> in the <a href='../subjects/7475' title='pea hay'>pea hay</a> this mornin<span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7737' title='hauling manure'>hauled manure</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Commenced to use the <a href='../subjects/7738' title='spreader'>spreader</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> helped to <span class='line-break'> </span> get <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> to day and has<span class='line-break'> </span> got the dinner for ten days<span class='line-break'> </span> she says.  I went to <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr<span class='line-break'> </span> Owens</a> and dressed <a href='../subjects/7828' title='Benjamin Franklin Owen'>the baby</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> While we were eating <span class='line-break'> </span> dinner <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> called me and<span class='line-break'> </span> ask if I wanted to go<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fishing</a>.  Of course I said<span class='line-break'> </span> I wanted to go so he carried<span class='line-break'> </span> me to <a href='../subjects/7211' title='Cedar Forest, Virginia'>Cedar Forest</a>.  I did <span class='line-break'> </span> not catch many fish.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I was glad of the trip.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got a <a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a> from <a href='../subjects/203' title='Alma Bennett'>Alma</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  Ben &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> has gone to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/67' title='Willie Mayhew'>Willie Mayhews</a> to night to get<span class='line-break'> </span> him to haul a load of <a href='../subjects/154' title='guano'>guano</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-854">
<h3><a name="page-854">Friday, April 11, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rainy</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> could<span class='line-break'> </span> not do much of any thing.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a>.  I helped some and<span class='line-break'> </span> helped a bout the <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> &amp; washing<span class='line-break'> </span> the dishes.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Got nearly wet attending<span class='line-break'> </span> to my <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chickens</a>.  It has bin a<span class='line-break'> </span> bad day on them.  <a href='../subjects/401' title='Virginia Dews'>Mrs. Dews</a><span class='line-break'> </span> intended to go <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fishing</a> and take<span class='line-break'> </span> me but it was so bad she<span class='line-break'> </span> did not go.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/242' title='Irvin Lewis'>Mr. Lewis</a> sent Ben five nice<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a> by <a href='../subjects/75' title='William Gilbert'>William Gilbert</a>.  Don't<span class='line-break'> </span> know what they will cost<span class='line-break'> </span> him.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-855">
<h3><a name="page-855">Saturday, April 12, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  I went<span class='line-break'> </span> with <a href='../subjects/419' title='Travis Dews'>Mr Dews</a> to <a href='../subjects/7211' title='Cedar Forest, Virginia'>Cedar<span class='line-break'> </span> Forest</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7740' title='Mrs Lewis'>Mrs Lewis</a> went also.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim Brumfield</a> carried me as<span class='line-break'> </span> far as Dews home.  We <span class='line-break'> </span> then went on a <a href='../subjects/115' title='wagon'>waggon</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/67' title='Willie Mayhew'>Mr Mayhew</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7741' title='Robert Mayhew'>Robert</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went on Mayhews <a href='../subjects/219' title='truck'>truck</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I never saw as many people<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fishing</a> on one day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7349' title='Evelyn Brumfield'>Evylin</a> come to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr. Owen</a> went after<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/154' title='guano'>guano</a>.  There was lots of<span class='line-break'> </span> people hauling <a href='../subjects/253' title='fertilizer'>fertilizer</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/153' title='Ren Worsham'>Wren</a> come over to the <span class='line-break'> </span> river where I was and talked<span class='line-break'> </span> with me a while.  I certainly<span class='line-break'> </span> did appreciate his comeing.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I left everything for <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> to do to<span class='line-break'> </span> day.  <a href='../subjects/15' title='milking'>Milkin</a> and <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churning</a> &amp; cookin.<span class='line-break'> </span> I would like to do what I think is right<span class='line-break'> </span> a bout the work but cant do<span class='line-break'> </span> enough to suit them not if I stay <span class='line-break'> </span> at home and work all the time.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-856">
<h3><a name="page-856">Sunday, April 13, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> &amp; I got the <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owens</a> and dressed <a href='../subjects/7828' title='Benjamin Franklin Owen'>the baby</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie</a> and <a href='../subjects/7349' title='Evelyn Brumfield'>Evylin</a> went home this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> They went on <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>Bens car</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7446' title='Mary Christine Craddock Towler'>Sister Mary</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7747' title='Mintie Motley'>Minty Motley</a> come<span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  <a href='../subjects/7743' title='Claud Debs?'>Claud Debs?</a> brough them.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am very glad that they come.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> &amp; family come a few<span class='line-break'> </span> minutes this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 11 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-857">
<h3><a name="page-857">Monday, April 14, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr. Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/93' title='hauling guano'>hauled</a><span class='line-break'> </span> a load of <a href='../subjects/154' title='guano'>guano</a> from the island.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/67' title='Willie Mayhew'>Mr Mayhew</a> hauled four loads.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got a mess of <a href='../subjects/7379' title='turnips'>turnip</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/284' title='salad'>salit</a> from <a href='../subjects/376' title='Posey Reynolds'>Posie Reynols</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and got the most of the <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went to the store this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening <a href='../subjects/7446' title='Mary Christine Craddock Towler'>Mary Towler</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7747' title='Mintie Motley'>Minty Motley</a> and I went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George Blairs</a> and had a<span class='line-break'> </span> nice time.  <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia</a> was not at <span class='line-break'> </span> home.  <a href='../subjects/153' title='Ren Worsham'>Wren Worsham</a> was<span class='line-break'> </span> at <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>Georges</a>.  Him and three<span class='line-break'> </span> children.  He brought us most<span class='line-break'> </span> of the way home.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-858">
<h3><a name="page-858">Tuesday, April 15, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a><span class='line-break'> </span> worked on their <a href='../subjects/7221' title='tobacco land'>tobacco land</a>.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> some in the <a href='../subjects/290' title='garden'>garden</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7688' title='Bettie Rosser'>Bettie Rosser</a> washed.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7446' title='Mary Christine Craddock Towler'>Mary</a> and <a href='../subjects/7747' title='Mintie Motley'>Mintie</a> and I and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went to <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johnsons</a>.  <a href='../subjects/409' title='Nannie Reynolds'>Nannie<span class='line-break'> </span> Kate Reynols</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7600' title='Charlotte Reynolds'>her baby</a> come<span class='line-break'> </span> over there.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> baked some<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/170' title='pies'>pies</a> for <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I cut <a href='../subjects/284' title='salad'>salit</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a>.  Paid <a href='../subjects/242' title='Irvin Lewis'>Lewis</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7745' title='debt'>what I owed him</a>.  Bought some<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7746' title='prunes'>prunes</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/42' title='candy'>candy</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> My <a href='../subjects/7577' title='shoes'>shoes</a> that Josie ordered<span class='line-break'> </span> come.  I got a little check<span class='line-break'> </span> interest on my <a href='../subjects/7481' title='Liberty Bonds'>bonds</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-859">
<h3><a name="page-859">Wednesday, April 16, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> morning and <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a><span class='line-break'> </span> before twelve oclock.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The men folks could not do<span class='line-break'> </span> much of any thing.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7446' title='Mary Christine Craddock Towler'>Mary Towler</a> and <a href='../subjects/7747' title='Mintie Motley'>Mintie Motley</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went from here this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> carried them to <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George<span class='line-break'> </span> Blairs</a> and <a href='../subjects/301' title='Frank Blair'>Frank Blair</a><span class='line-break'> </span> carried them home and brought<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>his mother</a> home.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> today.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> made <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> a <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a> and finished<span class='line-break'> </span> it some time before night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a few<span class='line-break'> </span> minutes this evening.  I got<span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/199' title='stockings'>stockings</a> by <a href='../subjects/7530' title='mail'>mail</a> that<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie ordered for me.  Am very<span class='line-break'> </span> well pleased with them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> has bin cross and mean<span class='line-break'> </span> all day.  I think because he could<span class='line-break'> </span> not <a href='../subjects/448' title='play'>play</a> out doors.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-860">
<h3><a name="page-860">Thursday, April 17, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/274' title='cool'>cool</a> <a href='../subjects/61' title='wind'>windy</a> day.  The men<span class='line-break'> </span> folks <a href='../subjects/7531' title='sawing'>sawed</a> <a href='../subjects/36' title='wood'>wood</a> here &amp; at <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owens</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> some and got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening she <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewed</a> on <a href='../subjects/90' title='pants'>pants</a><span class='line-break'> </span> for <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7650' title='Aubrey Brumfield'>Aubrey Brumfield</a> come here this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening for <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>potatoes</a>.  I did not<span class='line-break'> </span> have them for him.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> made a <a href='../subjects/7748' title='hot bed'>hot bed</a> Tuesday<span class='line-break'> </span> and used all the potatoes that<span class='line-break'> </span> was fit to bed.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I have mised <a href='../subjects/7446' title='Mary Christine Craddock Towler'>sister Mary</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7747' title='Mintie Motley'>Mintie</a> to day.  Hope they<span class='line-break'> </span> got home ok.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I <a href='../subjects/455' title='weeding'>cut some grass</a> out of the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7749' title='strawberry patch'>straw berrie patch</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Molly Reynolds's</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> They did not stay but a <span class='line-break'> </span> little while.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9:30 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Today was <a href='../subjects/212' title='Roy Smith'>Roy Smiths</a> birthday.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-861">
<h3><a name="page-861">Friday, April 18, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/274' title='cool'>cool</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/7531' title='sawing'>sawed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7547' title='hauling wood'>wood</a> for <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> this morning<span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/298' title='corn shucking'>shucked</a> corn this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin &amp; <a href='../subjects/75' title='William Gilbert'>William</a> helped them.<span class='line-break'> </span> They finished getting up<span class='line-break'> </span> the corn &amp; <a href='../subjects/7547' title='hauling wood'>hauled</a> the <a href='../subjects/11' title='tobacco stalks'>stalks</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/162' title='wood cutting'>cut</a> them up<span class='line-break'> </span> then cut down the cickamore<span class='line-break'> </span> tree.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> bought some <a href='../subjects/259' title='meal'>meal</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> from <a href='../subjects/68' title='John Hutcherson'>John Hutcherson</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> a peice of <a href='../subjects/260' title='meat'>meat</a> from <a href='../subjects/218' title='George Hutcherson'>George<span class='line-break'> </span> Hutcherson</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> &amp; starched the<span class='line-break'> </span> clothes.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening <a href='../subjects/205' title='Cordie Blair'>Cordie</a> and <a href='../subjects/206' title='Nettie Blair'>Nettie<span class='line-break'> </span> Blair</a> and <a href='../subjects/7535' title='Ada Hutcherson'>Ada Hutcherson</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come and <a href='../subjects/416' title='Beatrice Owen'>Beatriss Owen</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and several children. Three<span class='line-break'> </span> of <a href='../subjects/67' title='Willie Mayhew'>Willie Mayhews</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7751' title='Gladys Owen'>Gladis<span class='line-break'> </span> Owen</a>.  I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a><span class='line-break'> </span> a little while this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> was makeing <a href='../subjects/7654' title='Eva Smith'>Eva</a> a<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a>.  Marvin went to <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-862">
<h3><a name="page-862">Saturday, April 19, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/279' title='beautiful'>beautiful</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a>.  Ben <span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; Josie got home a bout night.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim staid up there.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> and I said[sic] at home<span class='line-break'> </span> until twelve.  Eat our <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> then went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  Marvin<span class='line-break'> </span> carried <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> &amp; Henry and I to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7206' title='White Falls, Virginia'>White Falls</a>.  We caught a <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a> a<span class='line-break'> </span> piece.  They would not bite.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/367' title='Odie Kellie'>Odie</a> and <a href='../subjects/7752' title='Lottie Kellie'>Lottie Kellie</a> and <a href='../subjects/7636' title='Elsie East'>Elsie<span class='line-break'> </span> East</a> was there.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7329' title='Mrs Johnson'>Mrs Johnson</a> come down there<span class='line-break'> </span> where I was a few minutes.<span class='line-break'> </span> There was plenty of <a href='../subjects/7544' title='frost'>frost</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> mornin.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-863">
<h3><a name="page-863">Sunday, April 20, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>Easter Sunday.  A good day.<span class='line-break'> </span> We all staid at home until<span class='line-break'> </span> after <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  We had <a href='../subjects/240' title='cake'>cake</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7753' title='pimento pepper'>pimento pepper</a> for dinner<span class='line-break'> </span> that <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> bought at <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and family<span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7240' title='Jim Power'>Jim Powers</a>.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George Blairs</a>.  <a href='../subjects/230' title='Lizzie Bennett'>Lizzie<span class='line-break'> </span> Bennett</a> was there for dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/153' title='Ren Worsham'>Ren Worsham</a> and family<span class='line-break'> </span> come this evening.  Ren and<span class='line-break'> </span> George and <a href='../subjects/7534' title='Dorothea Worsham'>Doratha</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7755' title='Ruth Worsham'>Ruth</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7756' title='Edge Hill, Virginia'>Edge Hill</a> <a href='../subjects/7228' title='preaching'>preaching</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin Smith</a> &amp; family<span class='line-break'> </span> come to <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>Georges</a>.  Marvin<span class='line-break'> </span> brought Lizzie and I home.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr. Owen</a> had a <a href='../subjects/133' title='horses'>horse</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/268' title='buggy'>buggy</a> and went for his<span class='line-break'> </span> sister.  She was at <a href='../subjects/7757' title='Mrs Myers'>Mrs<span class='line-break'> </span> Myers</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> made the <a href='../subjects/14' title='fire'>fire</a> in the cook<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/45' title='stove'>stove</a> this morning for the first time<span class='line-break'> </span> in his life that I know any thing<span class='line-break'> </span> a bout.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-864">
<h3><a name="page-864">Monday, April 21, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/230' title='Lizzie Bennett'>Lizzie</a> was here<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  She went to <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and eat <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  Ben &amp; family<span class='line-break'> </span> and I went to <a href='../subjects/7730' title='Creasy&apos;s pond'>Creasys fish<span class='line-break'> </span> pond</a>.  They drewed the <a href='../subjects/123' title='water'>water</a> off.<span class='line-break'> </span> They caugh several nice <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and a lot of <a href='../subjects/7726' title='turtles'>turtles</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I came back to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> and eat<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> come up there &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> the children.  They had an <a href='../subjects/7758' title='Easter egg hunt'>egg<span class='line-break'> </span> hunt</a> and had some nice<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/42' title='candy'>candy</a>.  Lizzie and I went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johnson Reynols</a>.  <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie</a> was<span class='line-break'> </span> not at home.  She &amp; <a href='../subjects/63' title='Robert Reynolds'>Robert</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7386' title='Christine Reynolds'>Christenie</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7651' title='Janie Brumfield'>Janie Brumfield</a><span class='line-break'> </span> had gone to <a href='../subjects/379' title='Jim Thompson'>Jim Thomsons</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We went to see <a href='../subjects/7444' title='Nannie Bennett'>Nanie</a> a while.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/410' title='Mrs Yeatts'>Mrs Yeats</a> was at <a href='../subjects/376' title='Posey Reynolds'>Posies</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim Brumfield</a> come home<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben &amp; <a href='../subjects/67' title='Willie Mayhew'>Mr Mayhew</a> went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a> this evening and got<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Bens</a> wire for a <a href='../subjects/414' title='fence'>fence</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-865">
<h3><a name="page-865">Tuesday, April 22, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  There was<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7544' title='frost'>frost</a> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The men folks worked on their<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7221' title='tobacco land'>tobacco land</a> all day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> some.  I put <a href='../subjects/249' title='eggs'>eggs</a><span class='line-break'> </span> under two <a href='../subjects/282' title='hens'>hens</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>planted</a> some <a href='../subjects/250' title='tomatoes'>tomato plants</a><span class='line-break'> </span> right at night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/212' title='Roy Smith'>Roy</a> and <a href='../subjects/325' title='Paul Smith'>Paul</a> has bin here<span class='line-break'> </span> all the evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> and three of<span class='line-break'> </span> the children went to <a href='../subjects/7208' title='Altavista, Virginia'>Altavista</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  I guess <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate</a> &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1630' title='Virginia Harvey'>Virginia Harvey</a> went with<span class='line-break'> </span> them.  <a href='../subjects/7759' title='Mr Pagget'>Mr</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7760' title='Mrs Pagget'>Mrs Pagget</a> passed <span class='line-break'> </span> here this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie scraped the grass out<span class='line-break'> </span> of the walke way to the<span class='line-break'> </span> front gate walk.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Well I will quit.  I went<span class='line-break'> </span> to sleep before I finished.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9:30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-866">
<h3><a name="page-866">Wednesday, April 23, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day most all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> most of the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/93' title='hauling guano'>hauled</a> straw and<span class='line-break'> </span> [?] Jims <a href='../subjects/7761' title='potato patch'>potato patch</a><span class='line-break'> </span> then worked on the <a href='../subjects/7221' title='tobacco land'>tobacco land</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim and I <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>planted</a> some <a href='../subjects/7265' title='onions'>onions</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>--most of it.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia</a> &amp; Corrdie come this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  Josie and <a href='../subjects/205' title='Cordie Blair'>Cordie</a> ordered<span class='line-break'> </span> some flower <a href='../subjects/363' title='seeds'>seed</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7762' title='bulbs'>bulbs</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> and the children come<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/7503' title='Jim Emerson'>Jim Emerson</a><span class='line-break'> </span> passed going down the way.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben has a bad <a href='../subjects/445' title='weather'>colde</a> &amp; is<span class='line-break'> </span> very much <a href='../subjects/81' title='complaining'>complaining</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9:10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-867">
<h3><a name="page-867">Thursday, April 24, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> <a href='../subjects/61' title='wind'>windy</a> day.  Some <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a> last night.  The men folks<span class='line-break'> </span> worked on their <a href='../subjects/7221' title='tobacco land'>tobacco land</a><span class='line-break'> </span> all day.  <a href='../subjects/7763' title='Robert Vaden'>Mr Robert Vaden</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7390' title='Smith'>Smith</a> of <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a> was<span class='line-break'> </span> here today.  They wanted the<span class='line-break'> </span> use of the <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school house</a> for<span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/7498' title='speaking'>speakin</a> Sat night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I both had a hand<span class='line-break'> </span> in gettin <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evenin I went to <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owens</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/401' title='Virginia Dews'>Mrs Dews</a> was there.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> come home and Josie and the<span class='line-break'> </span> children all went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> showed us her new things<span class='line-break'> </span> that she got at <a href='../subjects/7208' title='Altavista, Virginia'>Altavista</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin had made him a <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7748' title='hot bed'>hot bed</a>.  Mr Owen made one<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9:15 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-868">
<h3><a name="page-868">Friday, April 25, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> day and very <a href='../subjects/445' title='weather'>colde</a><span class='line-break'> </span> for this time of the year.<span class='line-break'> </span> The men folks worked on their<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7764' title='corn land'>corn land</a> all day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got some <a href='../subjects/238' title='plantbeds'>plant bed</a> <a href='../subjects/284' title='salad'>salit</a><span class='line-break'> </span> for the first time this year.<span class='line-break'> </span> She bake some ginger <a href='../subjects/37' title='cakes'>cakes</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  Light <a href='../subjects/390' title='bread'>bread</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  I washed some today.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7765' title='hiving'>Hived</a> a swarm of <a href='../subjects/7245' title='bees'>bees</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  They were so colde they<span class='line-break'> </span> could hardly fly.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I am a fraid that there will be <span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/7543' title='killing frost'>killing frost</a> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-869">
<h3><a name="page-869">Saturday, April 26, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> <a href='../subjects/274' title='cool'>cool</a> day.  There was<span class='line-break'> </span> plenty of <a href='../subjects/7544' title='frost'>frost</a> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> In some places the land was<span class='line-break'> </span> frozen.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> fixed some<span class='line-break'> </span> land for a <a href='../subjects/7766' title='sweet potato patch'>sweet potato patch</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7767' title='Chalk Level, Virginia'>Chalk Level</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning for some work that<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7768' title='Sam Switz'>Sam Switz</a> done for him.<span class='line-break'> </span> Worked the balance of the<span class='line-break'> </span> day on <a href='../subjects/7503' title='Jim Emerson'>Jim Emersons</a> <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and did not get it so he could<span class='line-break'> </span> use it.  Jim Emerson &amp; Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield and <a href='../subjects/7972' title='Lucius Gravely'>Lucius Gravely</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and Ben has gone to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait <span class='line-break'> </span> Stone</a> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> cooked <a href='../subjects/7237' title='butter beans'>butter beans</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> little <a href='../subjects/7770' title='white beans'>white beans</a> and baked<span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/240' title='cake'>cake</a> and fried some<span class='line-break'> </span> fresh <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a> for <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> a few things this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning and <a href='../subjects/182' title='mending'>mended</a> some<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-870">
<h3><a name="page-870">Sunday, April 27, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> <a href='../subjects/274' title='cool'>cool</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/7544' title='frost'>Frost</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> come home from<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a> a bout twelve oclock<span class='line-break'> </span> last night.  <a href='../subjects/7503' title='Jim Emerson'>Jim Emerson</a> come with<span class='line-break'> </span> him and staid all night and until <span class='line-break'> </span> some time this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben brough <a href='../subjects/55' title='ice cream'>ice cream</a> with him<span class='line-break'> </span> more than <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I could eat.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim Brumfield</a> and Ben staid<span class='line-break'> </span> at home all day.  Josie and the<span class='line-break'> </span> children and I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie got most of the <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> We had a <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chicken</a> for dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> The olde hog eat one of my<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/282' title='hens'>hens</a> this morning.  I am very<span class='line-break'> </span> sorry.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Heard to day that <a href='../subjects/7599' title='Mildred Ferguson'>Julia<span class='line-break'> </span> Fergersons baby</a> has bin very<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a>.  I do hope she will soon<span class='line-break'> </span> be well.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-871">
<h3><a name="page-871">Monday, April 28, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day and <a href='../subjects/159' title='warm'>warmer</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> worked<span class='line-break'> </span> on some <a href='../subjects/7764' title='corn land'>corn land</a> all the <span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  This evening Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> carried <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and I to <a href='../subjects/7211' title='Cedar Forest, Virginia'>Cedar Forest</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie done some dealing at<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7407' title='Mrs Hendricks'>Mrs Hendricks</a> then went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7240' title='Jim Power'>Jim Powers</a>.  I <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fished</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Did not <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>catch any</a> much.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben paid <a href='../subjects/153' title='Ren Worsham'>Ren Worsham</a> for<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/154' title='guano'>guano</a> this evenin.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie got <a href='../subjects/284' title='salad'>salit</a> for <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollies</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  Guess we will go<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7216' title='Portsmouth, Virginia'>Portsmoth</a> tomorrow.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The <a href='../subjects/134' title='hogs'>olde hog</a> eat my<span class='line-break'> </span> hen today that had some<span class='line-break'> </span> little <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chickens</a>.  I am so sorry<span class='line-break'> </span> that she will eat chickins.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-872">
<h3><a name="page-872">Tuesday, April 29, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  I was at home<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7772' title='Mrs Farmer'>Mrs<span class='line-break'> </span> Farmer</a> and went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7216' title='Portsmouth, Virginia'>Portsmoth</a>.  Had a good trip.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7224' title='Julia Ferguson'>Julia Fergerson</a> met us<span class='line-break'> </span> at the station.  <a href='../subjects/7223' title='Howard Ferguson'>Howard</a><span class='line-break'> </span> met us at the <a href='../subjects/463' title='boat'>boat</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/209' title='John Brumfield'>John</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7771' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield (b 1878)'>Henry Brumfield</a><span class='line-break'> </span> met us at Howards.<span class='line-break'> </span> I was glad to see them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-873">
<h3><a name="page-873">Wednesday, April 30, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day and some<span class='line-break'> </span> rain.  <a href='../subjects/7224' title='Julia Ferguson'>Julia</a> and <a href='../subjects/7599' title='Mildred Ferguson'>the baby</a>. <a href='../subjects/7772' title='Mrs Farmer'>Mrs Farmer</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie</a> and I went to the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7773' title='city park'>citty park</a>.  It <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rained</a> so that Julia<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; the baby staid under a shelter.  The<span class='line-break'> </span> rest of us looked a round.  There was<span class='line-break'> </span> a lot to look at.  Fowls &amp; flowers &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> animals.  We got back to <a href='../subjects/7223' title='Howard Ferguson'>Howards</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and eat <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.  <a href='../subjects/209' title='John Brumfield'>John</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7771' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield (b 1878)'>Henry<span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield</a> come.  Then we went<span class='line-break'> </span> to a <a href='../subjects/7774' title='picture show'>picture show</a>.  While we<span class='line-break'> </span> were waiting for a <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a> the <a href='../subjects/14' title='fire'>fire</a><span class='line-break'> </span> bell rang.  We went to see <span class='line-break'> </span> them throw <a href='../subjects/123' title='water'>water</a> with their <a href='../subjects/7310' title='pump'>pump</a><span class='line-break'> </span> It is all a show for them<span class='line-break'> </span> that dont live in town.<span class='line-break'> </span> I certainly do wish that <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> could be there and<span class='line-break'> </span> hear &amp; see for a while.  Julias baby<span class='line-break'> </span> cried a heap.  I am a fraid it is<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>not well</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This is wrote Thursday evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I for got to write last night.<span class='line-break'> </span> Having such a big time.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-874">
<h3><a name="page-874">Thursday, May  1, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day and a hard <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a> this evening.  We went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7218' title='Norfolk, Virginia'>Norfork</a> shopping did not get <span class='line-break'> </span> wet.  <a href='../subjects/209' title='John Brumfield'>John</a> and <a href='../subjects/7771' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield (b 1878)'>Henry</a> come again <span class='line-break'> </span> to night.  John brought some <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/42' title='candy'>candy</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7780' title='Mrs Barker'>Mrs. Barker</a> kept <a href='../subjects/7599' title='Mildred Ferguson'>Julias<span class='line-break'> </span> baby</a>.  This is wrote Friday <span class='line-break'> </span> morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-875">
<h3><a name="page-875">Friday, May  2, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  We are<span class='line-break'> </span> at <a href='../subjects/7224' title='Julia Ferguson'>Julias</a> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We have bin to <a href='../subjects/7218' title='Norfolk, Virginia'>Norfolk</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to see <a href='../subjects/7412' title='a show'>a show</a>.  We have <span class='line-break'> </span> bin to <a href='../subjects/7775' title='Virginia Beach, Virginia'>Virginia Beach</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  Julia went with<span class='line-break'> </span> us.  We had a nice<span class='line-break'> </span> time.  <a href='../subjects/209' title='John Brumfield'>John</a> treated us to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/55' title='ice cream'>ice cream</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7771' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield (b 1878)'>Henry</a> did <span class='line-break'> </span> not come to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I don't know <span class='line-break'> </span> what time it is.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-876">
<h3><a name="page-876">Saturday, May  3, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  I staid at<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7223' title='Howard Ferguson'>Howard Fergersons</a> all day.  <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7779' title='Mr Farmer'>Mr Farmer</a> went over to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7218' title='Norfolk, Virginia'>Norfolk</a> to day.  All three of us<span class='line-break'> </span> went to see <a href='../subjects/7780' title='Mrs Barker'>Mrs Barker</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7781' title='Mr Lewis Johnson'>Mr Lewis Johnson</a> come with<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/209' title='John Brumfield'>John Brumfield</a> to see me to<span class='line-break'> </span> nigh.  <a href='../subjects/7771' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield (b 1878)'>Henry</a> was here two.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7599' title='Mildred Ferguson'>Little Mildred</a> has cried a<span class='line-break'> </span> lot to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-877">
<h3><a name="page-877">Sunday, May  4, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/7772' title='Mrs Farmer'>Mrs Farmer</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7224' title='Julia Ferguson'>Julia</a> &amp; I and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/209' title='John Brumfield'>John</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7771' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield (b 1878)'>Henry</a> all went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7782' title='Williamsburg, Virginia'>Williams Burg</a>.  We <a href='../subjects/7531' title='sawing'>saw</a> lots <span class='line-break'> </span> of things that was curiosities<span class='line-break'> </span> to us.  It was a tiresome<span class='line-break'> </span> trip but we enjoyed it<span class='line-break'> </span> so much.  I hope that we<span class='line-break'> </span> may get home all right.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-878">
<h3><a name="page-878">Monday, May  5, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/7772' title='Mrs Farmer'>Mrs Farme</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie<span class='line-break'> </span> Reynolds</a> and come from <a href='../subjects/7223' title='Howard Ferguson'>Howard<span class='line-break'> </span> Fergersons</a> at <a href='../subjects/7216' title='Portsmouth, Virginia'>Portsmoth</a> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7224' title='Julia Ferguson'>Julia Fergerson</a> went with us to the<span class='line-break'> </span> depot.  Our fare a peice was $5 84 cts.<span class='line-break'> </span> We had a good trip up to <a href='../subjects/7203' title='Long Island, Virginia'>Long Island</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Julia gave us a nice lunch to take with<span class='line-break'> </span> us and <a href='../subjects/7779' title='Mr Farmer'>Mr Farmer</a> bough some<span class='line-break'> </span> fruit so we had plenty to eat and that<span class='line-break'> </span> was good.  <a href='../subjects/406' title='Bruce Reynolds'>Bruce Reynolds</a><span class='line-break'> </span> met us at <a href='../subjects/7682' title='depot'>the depot</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> brought us home.  I do thank them<span class='line-break'> </span> for carrieing and bringin me home.<span class='line-break'> </span> I found them all well.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> and her little ones was<span class='line-break'> </span> here.  I was glad to see them<span class='line-break'> </span> all.  I have felt troubled ever<span class='line-break'> </span> since I got home a bout <a href='../subjects/7329' title='Mrs Johnson'>Mrs<span class='line-break'> </span> Johnson</a> and <a href='../subjects/252' title='Mrs Hutcherson'>Mrs Hutcherson</a><span class='line-break'> </span> being so <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a>.  I want to go <span class='line-break'> </span> and see Mrs Hutcherson soon.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I am so glad I am at home<span class='line-break'> </span> a gain.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-879">
<h3><a name="page-879">Tuesday, May  6, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day and <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a><span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>planted</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a> all day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening I went to <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>Georges<span class='line-break'> </span> Blairs</a>.  <a href='../subjects/64' title='Lottie Craddock'>Lottie Blair</a> was there<span class='line-break'> </span> with <a href='../subjects/7727' title='Edith Ardena Craddock'>her little baby</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I was glad to see Lottie lookin<span class='line-break'> </span> as well as she does.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/204' title='Isla Blair'>Isla</a> was makeing Lottie a <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/205' title='Cordie Blair'>Cordie</a> was making her a <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8' title='quilting'>quilt</a>.  I came home and found<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>Jersey cow</a> with a<span class='line-break'> </span> new <a href='../subjects/87' title='calves'>calf</a>.  Ben is makeing my<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7783' title='clocks'>clock</a> strike right.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-880">
<h3><a name="page-880">Wednesday, May  7, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day.  No rain to<span class='line-break'> </span> stop any one from work.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> hung the <a href='../subjects/7784' title='spring house'>spring house</a> door<span class='line-break'> </span> and cleaned out the spring house.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening Josie and all the<span class='line-break'> </span> children went to <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>Georg Blairs</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I choped some in the <a href='../subjects/7785' title='flower garden'>flower<span class='line-break'> </span> garden</a> and helped <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> take<span class='line-break'> </span> off two <a href='../subjects/418' title='canvas'>canveses</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>planted</a> <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> some.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-881">
<h3><a name="page-881">Thursday, May  8, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Finish <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>planted</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a> and commence putting in<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/253' title='fertilizer'>ferterlizer</a> for <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> come here a little while.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> My <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>Jersey cow</a> <a href='../subjects/96' title='death'>died</a> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am very sorry but am glad <span class='line-break'> </span> it is no worse.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Have not seen any of <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a><span class='line-break'> </span> people to day.  All ways mis<span class='line-break'> </span> them if I dont see any of<span class='line-break'> </span> them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> is both<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/81' title='complaining'>complaining</a> this evening.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> hope they will get well soon.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> has had the <a href='../subjects/66' title='toothache'>tooth ache</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-882">
<h3><a name="page-882">Friday, May  9, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day and <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>some rain</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> The men folks <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>planted</a> a little<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a>.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> worked all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
