<p> I planted some <a href='../subjects/7265' title='onions'>onions</a>.  The <span class='line-break'> </span> latest that we planted<span class='line-break'> </span> any.  I planted them in<span class='line-break'> </span> the olde <a href='../subjects/7786' title='ice house'>ice house</a> hole.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening I <a href='../subjects/182' title='mending'>mended</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Bens</a> overalls<span class='line-break'> </span> then went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and staid a few minutes.<span class='line-break'> </span> Come home and <a href='../subjects/131' title='feeding'>fed</a> the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chickens</a> and <a href='../subjects/15' title='milking'>milked</a> the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cow</a> and fed the <a href='../subjects/87' title='calves'>calf</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie went to the <a href='../subjects/238' title='plantbeds'>plant<span class='line-break'> </span> bed</a> and got some <a href='../subjects/284' title='salad'>salit</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> She liked to got wet<span class='line-break'> </span> comeing home.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-883">
<h3><a name="page-883">Saturday, May 10, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>Some rain</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  They <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>planted</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> all the evening.  <a href='../subjects/349' title='Minnie Owen'>Mrs Owens</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/401' title='Virginia Dews'>Mrs Dews</a> and I <a href='../subjects/7787' title='drawing plants'>drawed<span class='line-break'> </span> plants</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We had a few <a href='../subjects/312' title='strawberries'>straw berries</a><span class='line-break'> </span> for <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> has gone to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span> All of the rest has gone<span class='line-break'> </span> to bed and a sleep.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-884">
<h3><a name="page-884">Sunday, May 11, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  We all staid<span class='line-break'> </span> at home until <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate</a> &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/52' title='Irvin Harvey'>Irvin Harvey</a> come and eat dinner<span class='line-break'> </span> with us.  When Kate started <span class='line-break'> </span> home <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I walked with<span class='line-break'> </span> her as far as <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7497' title='Reuben Reynolds'>Reubin Reynolds</a> come<span class='line-break'> </span> while we were gone.  <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johnson</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/406' title='Bruce Reynolds'>Bruce Reynolds</a> come to <span class='line-break'> </span> Marvins.  Bruce brought me home.<span class='line-break'> </span> I sent Reubin some <a href='../subjects/7788' title='roses'>roses</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> The <a href='../subjects/7245' title='bees'>bees</a> <a href='../subjects/7789' title='swarming'>swarmed</a> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-885">
<h3><a name="page-885">Monday, May 12, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The men folks<span class='line-break'> </span> worked on <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> land most of<span class='line-break'> </span> the day.  Late this evening<span class='line-break'> </span> they <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>planted</a> some tobacco<span class='line-break'> </span> but it is so <a href='../subjects/445' title='weather'>colde</a> that things<span class='line-break'> </span> cant grow.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/349' title='Minnie Owen'>Mrs. Owen</a> and I <a href='../subjects/7787' title='drawing plants'>drawed plants</a>.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> got so colde that I quit<span class='line-break'> </span> and come to the <a href='../subjects/7609' title='house'>house</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I washed some<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  Josie got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7651' title='Janie Brumfield'>Janie Brumfield</a> and <a href='../subjects/441' title='Delma Owen'>Delma<span class='line-break'> </span> Owen</a> come to see the<span class='line-break'> </span> children this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I started <a href='../subjects/7224' title='Julia Ferguson'>Julia Fergerson</a><span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I am so near a sleep that<span class='line-break'> </span> I cant hardly write.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The children found my Lady<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cow</a> with a nice little <a href='../subjects/87' title='calves'>calf</a>.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-886">
<h3><a name="page-886">Tuesday, May 13, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day and <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a><span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.  The men worked on their<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7221' title='tobacco land'>tobacco land</a> most of the day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went to the meeting of the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/221' title='school board'>school board</a> late this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  This evening<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johnsons</a>.  <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7386' title='Christine Reynolds'>Christenia</a> was at home.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/410' title='Mrs Yeatts'>Mrs Yeats</a> went from <a href='../subjects/376' title='Posey Reynolds'>Posies</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/7600' title='Charlotte Reynolds'>Nannies baby</a><span class='line-break'> </span> is <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>not well</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 11 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-887">
<h3><a name="page-887">Wednesday, May 14, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>Cloudy most of the day.<span class='line-break'> </span> The men <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>planted tobacco</a> all<span class='line-break'> </span> day.  <a href='../subjects/349' title='Minnie Owen'>Mrs Owen</a> and I <a href='../subjects/7787' title='drawing plants'>drawed<span class='line-break'> </span> plantes</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  We <span class='line-break'> </span> all certainly did enjoy it.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> <a href='../subjects/7790' title='dropping plants'>dropped plantes</a> some.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie &amp; <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> went to<span class='line-break'> </span> see <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> a little while.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening the weather is<span class='line-break'> </span> so <a href='../subjects/274' title='cool'>cool</a> that we have <a href='../subjects/14' title='fire'>fires</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to sit by when we<span class='line-break'> </span> get a chance to sit down.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-888">
<h3><a name="page-888">Thursday, May 15, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The men folks<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>planted tobacco</a> this morning.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7787' title='drawing plants'>drawed plants</a> until twelve.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/150' title='Dr. Anderson Owen'>Dr Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/8086' title='Jennie Owen'>and wife</a> ask me to <span class='line-break'> </span> go <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fishing</a>.  Their <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a> got so it<span class='line-break'> </span> would not work.  They left it<span class='line-break'> </span> on the road.  <a href='../subjects/68' title='John Hutcherson'>John Hutcherson</a><span class='line-break'> </span> let the Dr have his and<span class='line-break'> </span> we went to <a href='../subjects/7791' title='Moons Pond'>Moons Pond</a>.  Did<span class='line-break'> </span> not <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>catch any</a> fish to speak<span class='line-break'> </span> of.  I thank them for takein<span class='line-break'> </span> me with them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  She made<span class='line-break'> </span> vegetable <a href='../subjects/155' title='soup'>soup</a>.  I thought it<span class='line-break'> </span> was very good.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We heard to day that <a href='../subjects/7329' title='Mrs Johnson'>Mrs<span class='line-break'> </span> Johnson</a> <a href='../subjects/96' title='death'>died</a> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am sorry for the family.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-889">
<h3><a name="page-889">Friday, May 16, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The men<span class='line-break'> </span> worked on <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> land<span class='line-break'> </span> until twelve.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a> to meet <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie<span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield</a>.  <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> &amp; I<span class='line-break'> </span> went with him.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/242' title='Irvin Lewis'>Irvin Lewis</a> carried my<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/87' title='calves'>calf</a> to Gretna this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  <a href='../subjects/195' title='Henry Blair'>Henry Blair</a><span class='line-break'> </span> was up there.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 <a href='../subjects/7783' title='clocks'>clock</a></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-890">
<h3><a name="page-890">Saturday, May 17, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>Cloudy most of the day &amp; a<span class='line-break'> </span> little <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a>.  I woke up at three<span class='line-break'> </span> oclock this morning.  Got up at<span class='line-break'> </span> half passed four.  Made a <a href='../subjects/14' title='fire'>fire</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and went to the spring and<span class='line-break'> </span> then got <a href='../subjects/26' title='breakfast'>breakfast</a> fried <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/248' title='ham'>ham</a>.  After breakfast I<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/15' title='milking'>milked</a> two <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cows</a> and <a href='../subjects/131' title='feeding'>fed</a> the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/87' title='calves'>calf</a> then put on another <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> carried me to <a href='../subjects/419' title='Travis Dews'>Mr Dews</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> They carried me with them to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7203' title='Long Island, Virginia'>Long Island</a> <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fishing</a>.  We did not<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>catch any</a> thing worth haveing.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/401' title='Virginia Dews'>Mrs Dews</a> had a nice <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> They were all as nice &amp; good to<span class='line-break'> </span> me as any one could ask.  Brought<span class='line-break'> </span> me as far as <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owens</a> on my<span class='line-break'> </span> way home.  I certainly do thank<span class='line-break'> </span> them for their kindness.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie</a> was here to get<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner and attend to things.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben went to the <a href='../subjects/44' title='mill'>mill</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> [Ink smear] I went to sleep.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-891">
<h3><a name="page-891">Sunday, May 18, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day <a href='../subjects/274' title='cool'>cool</a> for May.<span class='line-break'> </span> We all staid at home until<span class='line-break'> </span> after <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie Brumfield</a><span class='line-break'> </span> was here.  We had <a href='../subjects/296' title='fried chicken'>fried chicken</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/170' title='pies'>coconut pies</a> for dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> and <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> went with Nellie<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a>.  They were gone three<span class='line-break'> </span> hours.  I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a><span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Maggie Brumfield and two<span class='line-break'> </span> children was there.  I was glad<span class='line-break'> </span> to see them<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-892">
<h3><a name="page-892">Monday, May 19, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The men folks<span class='line-break'> </span> worked on their <a href='../subjects/7764' title='corn land'>corn land</a> on the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/357' title='creek'>branch</a> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> carried<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7792' title='Mrs Moris of Altavista'>Mrs Moris of Altavista</a> to <a href='../subjects/7203' title='Long Island, Virginia'>Long Island</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> He was two late.  Her train had<span class='line-break'> </span> gone.  She went to <a href='../subjects/7793' title='Bill Owens'>Mr Bill <span class='line-break'> </span> Owens</a> to stay all night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  This evening<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie Smith</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come a little while.<span class='line-break'> </span> While they were here the <a href='../subjects/87' title='calves'>calves</a><span class='line-break'> </span> got in the <a href='../subjects/290' title='garden'>garden</a>.  I was <span class='line-break'> </span> mad and I am a fraid I<span class='line-break'> </span> made some of the rest of them<span class='line-break'> </span> mad.  I am very sorry that<span class='line-break'> </span> I got mad.  It is two late<span class='line-break'> </span> now.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> was <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  I do hope he is better <span class='line-break'> </span> by now.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got a <a href='../subjects/7794' title='check'>check</a> for<span class='line-break'> </span> my little <a href='../subjects/87' title='calves'>calf</a> to day.  It <span class='line-break'> </span> did not amount to much.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am glad of that if it is little.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-893">
<h3><a name="page-893">Tuesday, May 20, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>Rain</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>planted</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a> on the <a href='../subjects/357' title='creek'>branch</a> land<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  This evening Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> finished ceiling <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> room<span class='line-break'> </span> then they planted some <a href='../subjects/7324' title='watermelons'>water<span class='line-break'> </span> mellon</a> <a href='../subjects/363' title='seeds'>seed</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> I helped some.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I picked a few <a href='../subjects/312' title='strawberries'>straw<span class='line-break'> </span> berries</a> for <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> is very <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span> I do hope he may be better<span class='line-break'> </span> by morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-894">
<h3><a name="page-894">Blank</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-895">
<h3><a name="page-895">Thursday, May 22, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day and very <a href='../subjects/274' title='cool'>cool</a><span class='line-break'> </span> for May.  The men folks<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>replanted</a> their <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a>.  <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a><span class='line-break'> </span> planted some <a href='../subjects/304' title='beans'>beans</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7795' title='Dr Wigginton'>Dr Wigginton</a> was here today <span class='line-break'> </span> to see <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a>.  Said <span class='line-break'> </span> he did not have diptheria<span class='line-break'> </span> He is much better off than<span class='line-break'> </span> he was last night I<span class='line-break'> </span> think.  This evening I went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7581' title='Murphist Harvey'>Murphist Harvey</a><span class='line-break'> </span> was there.  He hung their<span class='line-break'> </span> screen doors to day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-896">
<h3><a name="page-896">Friday, May 23, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A very <a href='../subjects/274' title='cool'>cool</a> day for May.<span class='line-break'> </span> We begin to need rain.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> <a href='../subjects/7249' title='working tobacco'>worked tobacco</a><span class='line-break'> </span> all day.  <a href='../subjects/7796' title='John Bailey'>Mr John Baily</a> eat <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> here to day.  Ben &amp; Jim &amp; Henry<span class='line-break'> </span> has gone to the <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school house</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to night.  A <a href='../subjects/7797' title='patrons meeting'>patrons meeting</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> this morning.  This<span class='line-break'> </span> evening she went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/206' title='Nettie Blair'>Nettie Blair</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/424' title='Doris Brumfield'>Doris Brumfield</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7535' title='Ada Hutcherson'>Ada Hutcherson</a> come here<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  Doris wanted<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7324' title='watermelons'>water mellon</a> <a href='../subjects/363' title='seeds'>seed</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We heard to day that <a href='../subjects/7798' title='Lucie Peak'>Mrs<span class='line-break'> </span> Lucie Peak</a> started to the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7799' title='hospital'>hospitle</a> at <a href='../subjects/7800' title='Roanoke, Virginia'>Roanoke</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I am glad that <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> is<span class='line-break'> </span> a most well a gain.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-897">
<h3><a name="page-897">Saturday, May 24, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> morning and<span class='line-break'> </span> a little <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> We have a plenty of rain.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> worked on their<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco until <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  Ben &amp; Jim <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a>.  <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate<span class='line-break'> </span> Harvey</a> went with them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> &amp; I went with<span class='line-break'> </span> them as far as <a href='../subjects/379' title='Jim Thompson'>Jim Thompsons</a><span class='line-break'> </span> the we walked to <a href='../subjects/7206' title='White Falls, Virginia'>White Falls<span class='line-break'> </span> mills</a> [and] <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fished</a>.  We caught a<span class='line-break'> </span> few fish.  We walked back<span class='line-break'> </span> as far <a href='../subjects/7541' title='Mt. Airy, Virginia'>Mt Airy</a><span class='line-break'> </span> Ben brought us home.<span class='line-break'> </span> I paid Ben for the trouble<span class='line-break'> </span> that we were.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> most of the <span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  This evening Josie<span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> staid here<span class='line-break'> </span> by them selves.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I <a href='../subjects/15' title='milking'>milked</a> by the light of<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/7801' title='lantern'>lantern</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10:50 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-898">
<h3><a name="page-898">Sunday, May 25, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> come home<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to meet <span class='line-break'> </span> him.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/376' title='Posey Reynolds'>Posie</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/409' title='Nannie Reynolds'>Nannie</a> and <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie<span class='line-break'> </span> Reynolds</a> come this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I was at <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a><span class='line-break'> </span> was there.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> staid at home all day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> and <a href='../subjects/222' title='Hazel Smith'>Hazel Smith</a><span class='line-break'> </span> is <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a>.  I do hope that they<span class='line-break'> </span> will soon get well.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul Bennett</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/231' title='Earl Bennett'>Earl</a> was<span class='line-break'> </span> at Marvins to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-899">
<h3><a name="page-899">Monday, May 26, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The men folks<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>planted tobacco</a> all day.  I<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7787' title='drawing plants'>drawed plants</a> all the time<span class='line-break'> </span> that I could.  <a href='../subjects/349' title='Minnie Owen'>Mrs. Owen</a><span class='line-break'> </span> drawed this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/416' title='Beatrice Owen'>Beatriss Owen</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7203' title='Long Island, Virginia'>Long<span class='line-break'> </span> Island</a> to meet her cousin.<span class='line-break'> </span> She did not come.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> and <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> She picked <a href='../subjects/312' title='strawberries'>straw berries</a> for<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Two of <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a><span class='line-break'> </span> children are <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a>.  I am so<span class='line-break'> </span> sorry.  Hope they may be well<span class='line-break'> </span> soon.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul Bennett</a> commenced<span class='line-break'> </span> to work at <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span> I do hope that they may<span class='line-break'> </span> make a good crop.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/205' title='Cordie Blair'>Cordie</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/206' title='Nettie Blair'>Nettie Blair</a> come<span class='line-break'> </span> here this evening.  I did not<span class='line-break'> </span> see them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-900">
<h3><a name="page-900">Tuesday, May 27, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p><a href='../subjects/187' title='cloudy'>Cloudy</a> most of the day &amp; some<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a>.  The men finished planting<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>replanted</a> some.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> She went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We had <a href='../subjects/355' title='peas'>peas</a> for dinner<span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/296' title='fried chicken'>fried chicken</a>.  Had<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/312' title='strawberries'>strawberries</a> for <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> All of us are able to eat<span class='line-break'> </span> most any thing that we cook.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9:15 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-901">
<h3><a name="page-901">Wednesday, May 28, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  They <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>replanted</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> this morning and worked<span class='line-break'> </span> it this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening Josie and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> and I <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7802' title='Hubbards Bridge'>Hubbards Bridge</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fished</a> a little while.<span class='line-break'> </span> I caught 4 fish.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie got several things.<span class='line-break'> </span> She carried 10-1/2 dozen<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/249' title='eggs'>eggs</a> to the store and<span class='line-break'> </span> solde them.  They alowed her<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7482' title='money'>35 cts</a> per dozen<span class='line-break'> </span> for them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 ocloc</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-902">
<h3><a name="page-902">Thursday, May 29, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The men worked<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> this morning.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> worked<span class='line-break'> </span> in the <a href='../subjects/290' title='garden'>garden</a> this evening and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>planted</a> <a href='../subjects/7264' title='sweet potatoes'>sweet potatoes</a>.  I went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Reynols's</a> and got some slips.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> went to <a href='../subjects/68' title='John Hutcherson'>John Hutchersons</a><span class='line-break'> </span> twise to day after <a href='../subjects/259' title='meal'>meal</a>.  She<span class='line-break'> </span> got some this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie <a href='../subjects/7396' title='pickling'>made some pickle</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning and washed up her<span class='line-break'> </span> floor this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> worked all day in the<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco.  <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> was<span class='line-break'> </span> at <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> all the evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I have not seen <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul Bennett</a><span class='line-break'> </span> yet.  I begin to want to see<span class='line-break'> </span> him. <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-903">
<h3><a name="page-903">Friday, May 30, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The men<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7249' title='working tobacco'>worked tobacco</a> all day.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a><span class='line-break'> </span> helped them this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> all the morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> I <a href='../subjects/7233' title='irrigation'>watered</a> and covered<span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>potatoe slips</a> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got most of the <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> We had <a href='../subjects/355' title='peas'>peas</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7345' title='beets'>beets</a><span class='line-break'> </span> for dinner to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening Josie and I<span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie staid with the<span class='line-break'> </span> children.  <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> and I went<span class='line-break'> </span> for <a href='../subjects/312' title='strawberries'>straw berries</a>.  Did not<span class='line-break'> </span> find many.  I have bin <span class='line-break'> </span> cappin some to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10:30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-904">
<h3><a name="page-904">Saturday, May 31, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> worked on the tobacco<span class='line-break'> </span> until they finished.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> baked a <a href='../subjects/240' title='cake'>cake</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning and made a few<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/251' title='preserves'>preserves</a>.  I dressed 4 <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chickens</a> and capped a few<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/312' title='strawberries'>berries</a>.  This evening Josie<span class='line-break'> </span> scrubed the dining room<span class='line-break'> </span> floor.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> very kindly let<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul Bennett</a> carrie <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/325' title='Paul Smith'>Paul</a> and <a href='../subjects/212' title='Roy Smith'>Roy</a> and I to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7206' title='White Falls, Virginia'>White Falls</a> <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fishing</a>.  We<span class='line-break'> </span> caught several fish.<span class='line-break'> </span> I was so glad that <span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin helped us to go.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-905">
<h3><a name="page-905">Sunday, June  1, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day &amp; very <a href='../subjects/159' title='warm'>warm</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> staid at home and<span class='line-break'> </span> gathered some <a href='../subjects/311' title='cherries'>cherries</a> and <a href='../subjects/7804' title='straw berries'>straw<span class='line-break'> </span> berries</a>. <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> did not go to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben &amp; I and <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/416' title='Beatrice Owen'>Beatalis Owen</a> wen on the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a> with us.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> They had a big crowd<span class='line-break'> </span> and a plenty to eat.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7349' title='Evelyn Brumfield'>Evylin</a> came<span class='line-break'> </span> down. Sunday got to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Straight Stone</a> in time for <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> They came back by here.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Nellie staid and Evylin<span class='line-break'> </span> and Edna went back to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-906">
<h3><a name="page-906">Monday, June  2, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A little <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>shower</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning. Carried <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> with him.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie</a> went home.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben brought <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> home. She<span class='line-break'> </span> was very much pleased with<span class='line-break'> </span> her trip to Chatham.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> gathered a bucket of<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/311' title='cherries'>cheries</a> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie Reynolds</a><span class='line-break'> </span> came to the currant bushes.<span class='line-break'> </span> I met her. We gathered<span class='line-break'> </span> nearly two gallons of <a href='../subjects/383' title='currants'>currants</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> nearly all day<span class='line-break'> </span> on the patches.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 clock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-907">
<h3><a name="page-907">Tuesday, June  3, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7203' title='Long Island, Virginia'>Long Island</a> and got<span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/384' title='beet pulp'>beet pulp</a>. <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>planted</a> some <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>potatoes</a> slips.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> helped me.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening <a href='../subjects/7636' title='Elsie East'>Elsie</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/39' title='Helen Brumfield'>Hellen</a><span class='line-break'> </span> came. Elsie brought her baby.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie kept it while Elsie<span class='line-break'> </span> gathered some <a href='../subjects/311' title='cherries'>cherries</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am sorry that I was<span class='line-break'> </span> not at home.I would of bin<span class='line-break'> </span> if I had knowed they were<span class='line-break'> </span> coming. <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie Reynolds</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> I and Henry went after<span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/312' title='strawberries'>strawberries</a>. We found<span class='line-break'> </span> some.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I have not seen any of<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> people to day. I allways<span class='line-break'> </span> miss them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-908">
<h3><a name="page-908">Wednesday, June  4, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> in the <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a>.  Ben carried<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> and <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> to Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> Powers at twelve.  <a href='../subjects/7771' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield (b 1878)'>Henry</a> &amp; I went<span class='line-break'> </span> as far as the crossin at Starkeys.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fished</a> until Ben come back<span class='line-break'> </span> then come home.  Then I went to<span class='line-break'> </span> where <a href='../subjects/7805' title='Booker Callums'>Booker Callums</a> lives on <a href='../subjects/7806' title='Mrs Haley'>Mrs<span class='line-break'> </span> Haleys</a> land.  <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie Reynolds</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> I hunted <a href='../subjects/312' title='strawberries'>strawberries</a>.  Did not<span class='line-break'> </span> find many.  I <a href='../subjects/15' title='milking'>milked</a> by<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7801' title='lantern'>lantern</a> light to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We had <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>new Irish potatoes</a><span class='line-break'> </span> for <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> to day.  They was<span class='line-break'> </span> fine.  I made a few<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/251' title='preserves'>preserves</a> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10:15 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-909">
<h3><a name="page-909">Thursday, June  5, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A very <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rainy</a> day.  The <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/357' title='creek'>branch</a> was out of the <span class='line-break'> </span> banks.  The men <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> in the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a> a little while this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> I was here by my self<span class='line-break'> </span> except <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> in and out.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>potatoes</a> for <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> The <a href='../subjects/87' title='calves'>calf</a> got in the corn<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  Henry and I<span class='line-break'> </span> got it out &amp; <a href='../subjects/182' title='mending'>mended</a> the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/414' title='fence'>fence</a>.  I <a href='../subjects/79' title='letter writing'>wrote a letter</a> to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7205' title='Effie Thornton Brumfield'>Effie</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10:30 ocl</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-910">
<h3><a name="page-910">Friday, June  6, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7240' title='Jim Power'>Jim Powers</a> and got some<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7269' title='tobacco plants'>tobacco plants</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> come home<span class='line-break'> </span> with him.  I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>replanted</a> tobacco.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/205' title='Cordie Blair'>Cordie Blair</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7534' title='Dorothea Worsham'>Doratha</a> and <a href='../subjects/7755' title='Ruth Worsham'>Ruth<span class='line-break'> </span> Worsham</a> come this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-911">
<h3><a name="page-911">Saturday, June  7, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The men<span class='line-break'> </span> folks finished <a href='../subjects/8436' title='replanting tobacco'>replanting<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> She had <a href='../subjects/296' title='fried chicken'>fried chicken</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/355' title='peas'>peas</a> and <a href='../subjects/7345' title='beets'>beets</a>.  This evening<span class='line-break'> </span> she scrubed the cook<span class='line-break'> </span> room floor.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7240' title='Jim Power'>Mr Jim Power</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; wife come up here after<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/311' title='cherries'>cherries</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fishing</a>.  <a href='../subjects/307' title='Grace Brumfield'>Grace B</a><span class='line-break'> </span> carried me.  We got a mighty<span class='line-break'> </span> nice string of fish.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/308' title='Hugh Brumfield'>Hugh Brumfield</a> come a while<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  Got as many<span class='line-break'> </span> cherries as he could eat.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Jim and <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> has gone <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7231' title='Ethel Worsham'>Ethel Worsham</a> <a href='../subjects/7807' title='Paul Dewey Worsham'>has a son</a><span class='line-break'> </span> born this morning that is the 19th<span class='line-break'> </span> grand childe.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kates</a> <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cow</a> has a <a href='../subjects/87' title='calves'>calf</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Came last night.  I was so<span class='line-break'> </span> glad to see Kate this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-912">
<h3><a name="page-912">Sunday, June  8, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  We all staid<span class='line-break'> </span> at home until <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> then<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; family went to <a href='../subjects/7240' title='Jim Power'>Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> Powers</a>.  Jim and I staid at<span class='line-break'> </span> home.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> and family come<span class='line-break'> </span> all but <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a>.  I certainly was<span class='line-break'> </span> glad that they come.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I got dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> We had <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>new Irish potatoes</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/296' title='fried chicken'>fried chicken</a>, <a href='../subjects/7345' title='beets'>beets</a>, and <a href='../subjects/170' title='pies'>chocolate<span class='line-break'> </span> pies</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I stopped <a href='../subjects/7972' title='Lucius Gravely'>Lucius</a> &amp; his<span class='line-break'> </span> wife and had a look at their<span class='line-break'> </span> little daughter.  She is a fine<span class='line-break'> </span> child.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-913">
<h3><a name="page-913">Monday, June  9, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  They <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>replanted</a><span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> this morning &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7808' title='thinning corn'>thined corn</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> has bin <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a> most all<span class='line-break'> </span> day.  I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> then<span class='line-break'> </span> washed some.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Aunt Mollies</a> &amp; got some<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>potatoe slips</a>.  Henry and I<span class='line-break'> </span> planted them.  We have finished<span class='line-break'> </span> planting all that we want.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-914">
<h3><a name="page-914">Tuesday, June 10, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The men folks<span class='line-break'> </span> worked on their <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> all day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I washed a little this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  She had<span class='line-break'> </span> croped [?] <a href='../subjects/7809' title='greens'>greens</a> and <a href='../subjects/7345' title='beets'>beets</a>, <a href='../subjects/7265' title='onions'>onions</a> &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>potatoes</a> and <a href='../subjects/250' title='tomatoes'>tomatoes</a> and <a href='../subjects/170' title='pies'>pies</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> It was all good but<span class='line-break'> </span> worked her two hard.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening I went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George Blairs</a>.  The girls were<span class='line-break'> </span> seeding <a href='../subjects/311' title='cherries'>cherries</a>.  <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/252' title='Mrs Hutcherson'>Mrs<span class='line-break'> </span> Hutcherson</a> was gone to see<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7231' title='Ethel Worsham'>Ethel Worsham</a>.  I come by<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a>.  Josie was there.  We seeded<span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/311' title='cherries'>cheries</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-915">
<h3><a name="page-915">Wednesday, June 11, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A little <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span> The men folks worked in the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> most all day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I worked<span class='line-break'> </span> in the <a href='../subjects/290' title='garden'>garden</a> a while.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie gathered some <a href='../subjects/7277' title='green beans'>snaps</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening and we<span class='line-break'> </span> strung them tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/75' title='William Gilbert'>William Gilbert</a> gathered<span class='line-break'> </span> two gallons <a href='../subjects/311' title='cherries'>cheries</a> for<span class='line-break'> </span> us to day.  Josie and I<span class='line-break'> </span> seeded them this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-916">
<h3><a name="page-916">Thursday, June 12, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  We had a <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>very<span class='line-break'> </span> hard rain</a> just before day this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> The men <a href='../subjects/7810' title='cutting wheat'>cut some wheat</a> to<span class='line-break'> </span> day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> was<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a>.  We had our first mess of<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7277' title='green beans'>snaps</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> and I went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/153' title='Ren Worsham'>Ren Worsham's</a>.  Found them<span class='line-break'> </span> all well as could be expected.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7550' title='Jesse Hutcherson'>Mr Jessie Hutcherson</a> &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/68' title='John Hutcherson'>John Hutcherson</a> was <a href='../subjects/7388' title='tobacco cutting'>cutting</a><span class='line-break'> </span> wheat.  Also Ren was cutting <span class='line-break'> </span> two.  Workeing 4 <a href='../subjects/133' title='horses'>horses</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Edna and I walked.  Ren<span class='line-break'> </span> insisted that we let him<span class='line-break'> </span> bring us home.  I would not<span class='line-break'> </span> let him.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-917">
<h3><a name="page-917">Friday, June 13, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The men<span class='line-break'> </span> folks <a href='../subjects/7810' title='cutting wheat'>cut wheat</a> the most<span class='line-break'> </span> of the day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed to night.<span class='line-break'> </span> She has the <a href='../subjects/66' title='toothache'>tooth ache</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening I went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a>.  She was boiling<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7811' title='dewberries'>dew berries</a> to make some<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7373' title='jelly'>jellie</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henrys</a> duck <a href='../subjects/249' title='eggs'>eggs</a> hatched<span class='line-break'> </span> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie made <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> two<span class='line-break'> </span> little <a href='../subjects/8112' title='petticoats'>peticoats</a>.  I think they<span class='line-break'> </span> are pretty.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7208' title='Altavista, Virginia'>Altavista</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening for <a href='../subjects/7581' title='Murphist Harvey'>Murphist<span class='line-break'> </span> Harvey</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-918">
<h3><a name="page-918">Saturday, June 14, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Some <a href='../subjects/187' title='cloudy'>clouds</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this morning but no rain here.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> finished <a href='../subjects/7810' title='cutting wheat'>cutting wheat</a><span class='line-break'> </span> at <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> and at home.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> has had the <a href='../subjects/66' title='toothache'>tooth ache</a><span class='line-break'> </span> all day.  I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening Marvin let <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul<span class='line-break'> </span> Bennett</a> carrie me &amp; <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7206' title='White Falls, Virginia'>White Falls</a>.  We come<span class='line-break'> </span> with <a href='../subjects/63' title='Robert Reynolds'>Robert Reynolds</a> as<span class='line-break'> </span> far as <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a>.  Paul brough<span class='line-break'> </span> me home.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/273' title='Gordon Bennett'>Gordon</a> and <a href='../subjects/7508' title='Frances Bennett'>Frances</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/231' title='Earl Bennett'>Earl</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/230' title='Lizzie Bennett'>Lizzie Bennett</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come down here this evening.  Lizzie<span class='line-break'> </span> is with us tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Henry and I had a good<span class='line-break'> </span> time if we did not catch<span class='line-break'> </span> many <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a>.  Robert stopped at<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/378' title='Alice Thompson'>Alice Thomsons</a> and got the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7813' title='ice cream freezer'>ice cream freezer</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I had two invatations from<span class='line-break'> </span> the grand children to be at<span class='line-break'> </span> their <a href='../subjects/7814' title='graduation'>graduations</a>, one in <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and one in <a href='../subjects/7212' title='Richmond, Virginia'>Richmond</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben and Josie went to Renan tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 11 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-919">
<h3><a name="page-919">Sunday, June 15, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <a href='../subjects/230' title='Lizzie Bennett'>Lizzie Bennett</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George Blairs</a> for <span class='line-break'> </span> dinner.  <a href='../subjects/273' title='Gordon Bennett'>Gordon</a> &amp; his wife and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/231' title='Earl Bennett'>Earl</a> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul Bennett</a> all was<span class='line-break'> </span> there for dinner.  They had a <span class='line-break'> </span> good dinner.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> family and <a href='../subjects/52' title='Irvin Harvey'>Irvin</a> and <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate<span class='line-break'> </span> Harvey</a> all come here a while<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  I would of liked <span class='line-break'> </span> to of bin here two.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7408' title='Johnsons'>Johnsons</a> a<span class='line-break'> </span> while this evening.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> staid at home all day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>his mother</a> has<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/66' title='toothache'>tooth ache</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-920">
<h3><a name="page-920">Monday, June 16, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The men <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> all day.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> picked two<span class='line-break'> </span> gallons of <a href='../subjects/7811' title='dewberries'>dew berries</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning and some this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> She went to <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I worked some in the <a href='../subjects/290' title='garden'>garden</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening a bout the most<span class='line-break'> </span> that I have done in the garden<span class='line-break'> </span> this year.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> has worked it<span class='line-break'> </span> a bout all this year.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie boiled some <a href='../subjects/7816' title='berries'>berries</a> to<span class='line-break'> </span> make <a href='../subjects/7373' title='jelly'>jellie</a>.  Left it to drip<span class='line-break'> </span> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-921">
<h3><a name="page-921">Tuesday, June 17, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The men<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> all day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> to the <a href='../subjects/44' title='mill'>mill</a> mightty a gainst<span class='line-break'> </span> his will.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> made <a href='../subjects/7373' title='jelly'>jellie</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/251' title='preserves'>preserves</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  We had <a href='../subjects/236' title='cabbage'>cabbage</a><span class='line-break'> </span> for <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> the first time <span class='line-break'> </span> this spring.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/7408' title='Johnsons'>Johnsons</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  I went with<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lee B</a><span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/228' title='Clifton Reynolds'>Clifton Reynolds</a> come<span class='line-break'> </span> home this evening on<span class='line-break'> </span> a visit.  He is on his way<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7817' title='North Carolina'>North Carlina</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-922">
<h3><a name="page-922">Wednesday, June 18, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/7378' title='sowing'>sowed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/355' title='peas'>peas</a>.  Ben went to <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lee B</a><span class='line-break'> </span> after them and carried all the<span class='line-break'> </span> children.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> carried two doz<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/249' title='eggs'>eggs</a>.  He bought <a href='../subjects/7818' title='matches'>match</a> and <a href='../subjects/7819' title='fly powder'>fly<span class='line-break'> </span> powder</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7820' title='chewing gum'>chewing gum</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Henry done his first <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowing</a> to<span class='line-break'> </span> day.  <a href='../subjects/7821' title='Dr Bennett'>Dr Bennett</a> and <a href='../subjects/7822' title='Henry Bennett'>Henry<span class='line-break'> </span> Bennett</a> come to see Jim &amp; Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> today.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> this morning.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  This evening I ironed<span class='line-break'> </span> some &amp; then went to the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7761' title='potato patch'>sweet potatoe patch</a>.  They are<span class='line-break'> </span> lookin well.  I come through<span class='line-break'> </span> Jims <a href='../subjects/7337' title='tobacco ground'>tobacco ground</a>.  The<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco is growing some.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10:15 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-923">
<h3><a name="page-923">Thursday, June 19, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>shower</a> this morning<span class='line-break'> </span> but a <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/7668' title='sowing tobacco'>sowed</a> <a href='../subjects/355' title='peas'>peas</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  This evening Ben <a href='../subjects/7810' title='cutting wheat'>cut</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7263' title='wheat'>wheat</a> for <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lee Brumfield</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Oskar Brumfield <a href='../subjects/7808' title='thinning corn'>thined<span class='line-break'> </span> corn</a> for Ben.  <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> and I<span class='line-break'> </span> thined 26 rows this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> made Ben two <a href='../subjects/7606' title='shirts'>shirts</a><span class='line-break'> </span> today.  I <a href='../subjects/7371' title='canning'>caned</a> some <a href='../subjects/7345' title='beets'>beets</a>.  The<span class='line-break'> </span> first that I ever caned.<span class='line-break'> </span> I choped a little in the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/290' title='garden'>garden</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>replanted</a> some<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7250' title='cucumber'>cucumber</a> hills.  Put up some<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7265' title='onions'>onions</a>.  We are getting plenty<span class='line-break'> </span> vegatables now.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10:15 oclock </p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-924">
<h3><a name="page-924">Friday, June 20, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day and very <a href='../subjects/159' title='warm'>warm</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> all day <a href='../subjects/7295' title='laying by'>laying by</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a>.  <a href='../subjects/951' title='Oscar Brumfield'>Oscar</a> and <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry Brumfield</a><span class='line-break'> </span> finished thining corn this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> Oscar plowed this evening.  Henry &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/308' title='Hugh Brumfield'>Hugh</a> played all the evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry went with Hugh home<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to the meeting of the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/221' title='school board'>school board</a> at <a href='../subjects/7823' title='Greenfield Baptist Church'>Green field</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> and I went to <a href='../subjects/7206' title='White Falls, Virginia'>White<span class='line-break'> </span> Falls</a>.  Ben carried us and<span class='line-break'> </span> come and brought us home.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  She cooked<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/236' title='cabbage'>cabbage</a> and <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>potatoes</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> baked <a href='../subjects/7398' title='apples'>apples</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-925">
<h3><a name="page-925">Saturday, June 21, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good morning.  It <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rained</a><span class='line-break'> </span> a nice <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>shower</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> finished <a href='../subjects/7810' title='cutting wheat'>cutting wheat</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> at <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lees</a> this morning.  <a href='../subjects/951' title='Oscar Brumfield'>Oscar<span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield</a> brought the <a href='../subjects/7824' title='binder'>binder</a><span class='line-break'> </span> home this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben carried <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> a part<span class='line-break'> </span> of the way to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7825' title='John Ramsey'>Mr John<span class='line-break'> </span> Ramsey</a> carried him to Gretna.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben did not go to the <a href='../subjects/85' title='lodge'>Lodge</a><span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> gathered some <a href='../subjects/7826' title='dew berries'>dew<span class='line-break'> </span> berries</a> this morning.  <a href='../subjects/7371' title='canning'>Caned</a><span class='line-break'> </span> them this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I was at <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> a few minutes<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-926">
<h3><a name="page-926">Sunday, June 22, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> staid at home all day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We <a href='../subjects/296' title='fried chicken'>fried chicken</a> for <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and had <a href='../subjects/170' title='pies'>berrie pie</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went to <a href='../subjects/335' title='Margaret Brumfield'>Mags</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went with<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> to <a href='../subjects/391' title='Sunday School'>Sunday School</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/153' title='Ren Worsham'>Ren Worshams</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to see <a href='../subjects/7600' title='Charlotte Reynolds'>Posies baby</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> She is <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>not well</a>.  The <a href='../subjects/293' title='doctor'>dr</a> was<span class='line-break'> </span> to see her Friday.<span class='line-break'> </span> I do hope she may get well<span class='line-break'> </span> soon.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
