<p> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/378' title='Alice Thompson'>Alace Thomson</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and the children was at<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7408' title='Johnsons'>Johnsons</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-927">
<h3><a name="page-927">Monday, June 23, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>Rain</a> tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/7827' title='cutting oats'>cut his oats</a> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> come home from<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a> to night.  He come<span class='line-break'> </span> with <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johnson Reynolds</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/349' title='Minnie Owen'>Mrs. Owen</a> come a while<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  Brought her new<span class='line-break'> </span> baby <a href='../subjects/7828' title='Benjamin Franklin Owen'>Benjamine Franklin</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George Blairs</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  They were getting<span class='line-break'> </span> up their <a href='../subjects/7263' title='wheat'>wheat</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7675' title='Charlie Hutcherson'>Mr Charley Hutcherson</a><span class='line-break'> </span> was planting <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a> this evening<span class='line-break'> </span> on <a href='../subjects/7478' title='wheat land'>wheat land</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/204' title='Isla Blair'>Isla Blair</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/205' title='Cordie Blair'>Cordie</a> was<span class='line-break'> </span> gone to <a href='../subjects/153' title='Ren Worsham'>Ren Worshams</a><span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben bought a sack of<span class='line-break'> </span> ship [?] stuff from <a href='../subjects/242' title='Irvin Lewis'>Irvin Lewis</a>.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-928">
<h3><a name="page-928">Tuesday, June 24, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A very <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rainy</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> got out a few <a href='../subjects/355' title='peas'>peas</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewed</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Made <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> some <a href='../subjects/110' title='under waist'>under waist</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/210' title='drawers'>drawers</a> and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> a pair<span class='line-break'> </span> of drawers.  I <a href='../subjects/158' title='telephones'>phoned</a> to night<span class='line-break'> </span> to hear from <a href='../subjects/7423' title='Mrs. Edmons'>Mrs. Edmons</a> &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/336' title='Alice Wooding'>Miss Alice Wooding</a>.  They are very<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a> yet. I want to go to see<span class='line-break'> </span> them soon.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-929">
<h3><a name="page-929">Wednesday, June 25, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day and <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>raining</a><span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.  The men folks cant<span class='line-break'> </span> do any thing much.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sowed</a> some this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening she went <span class='line-break'> </span> to see <a href='../subjects/7423' title='Mrs. Edmons'>Mrs. Edmons</a> &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/336' title='Alice Wooding'>Miss Alice Wooding</a>.  Did <span class='line-break'> </span> not see Miss Alice as they <span class='line-break'> </span> dont let any one go in<span class='line-break'> </span> to see her.  I hope that they<span class='line-break'> </span> both may soon be better.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got a <a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a> from<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7224' title='Julia Ferguson'>Julia Fergerson</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Was glad to hear from her.<span class='line-break'> </span> I <a href='../subjects/79' title='letter writing'>wrote</a> <a href='../subjects/209' title='John Brumfield'>John Brumfield</a> a <span class='line-break'> </span> letter today.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul Bennett</a><span class='line-break'> </span> is very much <a href='../subjects/81' title='complaining'>complaining</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim Brumfield</a><span class='line-break'> </span> carried some <a href='../subjects/7261' title='rye'>rye</a> to Charley<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7323' title='Hutcherson'>Hutcherson</a> for him to grind.<span class='line-break'> </span> Walked and carried it<span class='line-break'> </span> rather than hitch a <a href='../subjects/133' title='horses'>horse</a> to a <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/268' title='buggy'>buggy</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-930">
<h3><a name="page-930">Thursday, June 26, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rainy</a> day.  The <a href='../subjects/357' title='creek'>branch</a> was<span class='line-break'> </span> as high as it most ever gets.<span class='line-break'> </span> It has <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rained</a> three nights nearly<span class='line-break'> </span> all night.  We had fried <a href='../subjects/7398' title='apples'>apples</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/249' title='eggs'>eggs</a> for <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George Blairs</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  They had to wade<span class='line-break'> </span> the branch to get a cross.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Jim bought some <a href='../subjects/223' title='butter'>butter</a> from <a href='../subjects/393' title='Sallie Blair'>Sallie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> Blair.  He would insist on going<span class='line-break'> </span> home so Ben carried him to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7203' title='Long Island, Virginia'>Long Island</a>.  When Ben got to the <span class='line-break'> </span> creek at <a href='../subjects/7342' title='Cedar Forest'>Cedar Forest</a> it was<span class='line-break'> </span> up so that he would not cross<span class='line-break'> </span> with the <a href='../subjects/268' title='buggy'>buggy</a>.  He put his <a href='../subjects/133' title='horses'>horse</a><span class='line-break'> </span> up at <a href='../subjects/7829' title='Mr Johnsons'>Mr Johnsons</a> and come <span class='line-break'> </span> over on a <a href='../subjects/463' title='boat'>boat</a> and walked<span class='line-break'> </span> home.  He brough some <a href='../subjects/7530' title='mail'>mail</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> for several people.  The carrier did<span class='line-break'> </span> not make his round on account<span class='line-break'> </span> of <a href='../subjects/7447' title='flooding'>high water</a>.  I am very<span class='line-break'> </span> glad that things are not worse<span class='line-break'> </span> than they are.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-931">
<h3><a name="page-931">Friday, June 27, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>Some <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7342' title='Cedar Forest'>Cedar Forest</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> for his <a href='../subjects/133' title='horses'>horse</a> that he left<span class='line-break'> </span> yesterday.  The river did not get<span class='line-break'> </span> very high.  Not like it was<span class='line-break'> </span> expected to.  Ben come to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a> and <a href='../subjects/7830' title='seining'>helped to sein</a><span class='line-break'> </span> some.  Brought home 4 nice<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7288' title='catfish'>cat fish</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> cleaned up <span class='line-break'> </span> the cupboard some.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>Potatoes</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/355' title='peas'>peas</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7345' title='beets'>beets</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr. Owen</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> to see his brother to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-932">
<h3><a name="page-932">Saturday, June 28, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  A <a href='../subjects/274' title='cool'>cool</a> east <a href='../subjects/61' title='wind'>wind</a><span class='line-break'> </span> all day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> choped a<span class='line-break'> </span> little in the <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a>.  The land two<span class='line-break'> </span> wet to work.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I did not do<span class='line-break'> </span> much of any thing.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening Ben &amp; the children<span class='line-break'> </span> and I and <a href='../subjects/416' title='Beatrice Owen'>Beatriss Owen</a> went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a> to a lawn<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/48' title='party'>party</a>.  They solde <a href='../subjects/55' title='ice cream'>ice cream</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I enjoyed it all.  <a href='../subjects/7759' title='Mr Pagget'>Mr</a>s. Car<span class='line-break'> </span> was there.  They had a big<span class='line-break'> </span> crowd.  Could of solde as much<span class='line-break'> </span> more cream if they had it.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> and his crowd was<span class='line-break'> </span> there.  We got home about sundown.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie got <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.  I <a href='../subjects/15' title='milking'>milked</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/52' title='Irvin Harvey'>Irvin Harvey</a> rode <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Bens</a> <a href='../subjects/289' title='colt'>colte</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to Strait Stone.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-933">
<h3><a name="page-933">Sunday, June 29, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Cool north<span class='line-break'> </span> east <a href='../subjects/61' title='wind'>wind</a> blowing.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7831' title='Mr Hankins'>Mr Hankins</a> and got<span class='line-break'> </span> three of his little <a href='../subjects/7833' title='ducks'>ducks</a> that<span class='line-break'> </span> got a way when the <a href='../subjects/357' title='creek'>branch</a><span class='line-break'> </span> was so high.  We all eat <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> at home.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben went this evening to<span class='line-break'> </span> meet <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a>.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> went with <span class='line-break'> </span> him.  I went as far as <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lee Brumfields</a>.  Spent a pleasant<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> is in<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7800' title='Roanoke, Virginia'>Roanoake</a> to see <a href='../subjects/360' title='Pearl Harvey'>Pearl Wigginton</a><span class='line-break'> </span> in the <a href='../subjects/7799' title='hospital'>hospitle</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/41' title='Beulah Brumfield'>Beaula Brumfield</a> is staying<span class='line-break'> </span> with <a href='../subjects/1630' title='Virginia Harvey'>Virginia Harvey</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Jim is here Ok tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> children was here<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-934">
<h3><a name="page-934">Monday, June 30, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The men chopped<span class='line-break'> </span> in the tobacco.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and washed this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/7206' title='White Falls, Virginia'>White Falls</a> <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fishin</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/307' title='Grace Brumfield'>Grace Brumfield</a> carried me<span class='line-break'> </span> from <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a> &amp; brought me<span class='line-break'> </span> that far back.  I walked home.<span class='line-break'> </span> I <a href='../subjects/7592' title='saw'>saw</a> five plows going<span class='line-break'> </span> in one field at <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johnson<span class='line-break'> </span> Reynolds</a> and mowing at<span class='line-break'> </span> the same time.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-935">
<h3><a name="page-935">Tuesday, July  1, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> in their <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed a big washin of clothes.  I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  Was <span class='line-break'> </span> late a bout it.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia Blair</a> come and eat <span class='line-break'> </span> dinner with us.  I was glad <span class='line-break'> </span> that she come. <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> I walked to <a href='../subjects/7422' title='Mr. Edmons'>Mr. Edmons</a> to <span class='line-break'> </span> see <a href='../subjects/7423' title='Mrs. Edmons'>Mrs. Edmons</a>.  <a href='../subjects/401' title='Virginia Dews'>Mrs. Dews</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/349' title='Minnie Owen'>Mrs. Owen</a> was there.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7559' title='Board Dews'>Board Dews</a> come for his <span class='line-break'> </span> mother and <a href='../subjects/349' title='Minnie Owen'>Aunt Minnie</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> in the <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a>.  He brought <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia</a> and I as far as <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owens</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7429' title='Mrs. Coats'>Mrs. Coats</a> <a href='../subjects/96' title='death'>died</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> today.  She was <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josies</a> aunt.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7898' title='Evelyn Edmonds'>Miss Evylin Edmons</a> made <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7834' title='lemonaide'>lemmon aid</a> as good as <span class='line-break'> </span> I ever drank.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>

<div id="page-936">
<h3><a name="page-936">Wednesday, July  2, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> this morning.  This evening<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim mowed.  Ben &amp; <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7429' title='Mrs. Coats'>Mrs Coats</a> <a href='../subjects/118' title='burial'>burial</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> and <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  Henry carried<span class='line-break'> </span> his <a href='../subjects/7833' title='ducks'>ducks</a> with him up there to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/448' title='play'>play</a> with.  I went to <a href='../subjects/92' title='Mr Hutcherson'>Mr<span class='line-break'> </span> Hutchersons</a>.  <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia</a> and <a href='../subjects/393' title='Sallie Blair'>Sallie<span class='line-break'> </span> Blair</a> was there.  <a href='../subjects/7836' title='Anna Mayhew'>Anna Mayhew</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and two of her children<span class='line-break'> </span> was there.  <a href='../subjects/252' title='Mrs Hutcherson'>Mrs Hutcherson</a><span class='line-break'> </span> in tends going to <a href='../subjects/7212' title='Richmond, Virginia'>Richmond</a><span class='line-break'> </span> tomorrow for to see the <a href='../subjects/373' title='Dr'>Dr</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I hope she may get well.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 O Clock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>

<div id="page-937">
<h3><a name="page-937">Thursday, July  3, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day and very hot.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> raked up his <a href='../subjects/7301' title='hay'>hay</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> this morning.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come this evening and brought<span class='line-break'> </span> all the children.  Josie &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie went after <a href='../subjects/7816' title='berries'>berries</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Found the <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cow</a> in the <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> They got some berries &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> lots of <a href='../subjects/7837' title='chiggers'>chickers</a> (dont know<span class='line-break'> </span> how to spell them).  Josie made<span class='line-break'> </span> plum <a href='../subjects/7373' title='jelly'>jellie</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got up the <a href='../subjects/7265' title='onions'>onions</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> helped<span class='line-break'> </span> me put them in the <a href='../subjects/7838' title='carriage house'>buggy<span class='line-break'> </span> house</a> up stairs.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/252' title='Mrs Hutcherson'>Mrs Hutcherson</a> started to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7212' title='Richmond, Virginia'>Richmond</a> this morning.  I do<span class='line-break'> </span> hope she may come home a<span class='line-break'> </span> gain.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-938">
<h3><a name="page-938">Friday, July  4, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The men folks<span class='line-break'> </span> all <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  She<span class='line-break'> </span> cooked <a href='../subjects/7277' title='green beans'>snaps</a> and <a href='../subjects/7336' title='cymblins'>cymblins</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>potatoes</a> and <a href='../subjects/7345' title='beets'>beets</a> and baked<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7398' title='apples'>apples</a>.  This evening I went with<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7561' title='Gladys Brumfield'>Gladdis</a> and <a href='../subjects/308' title='Hugh Brumfield'>Hugh</a> and <a href='../subjects/7650' title='Aubrey Brumfield'>Aubry<span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield</a> <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fishing</a>.  We caught <span class='line-break'> </span> a lot of little fish.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I come by <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Blairs</a>.  The men<span class='line-break'> </span> folks was stackin <a href='../subjects/7301' title='hay'>hay</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7292' title='oats'>oats</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Several of the people a round<span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7208' title='Altavista, Virginia'>Altavista</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and some to <a href='../subjects/446' title='South Boston'>South Boston</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>planted</a> some <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/304' title='beans'>beans</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 30 O <a href='../subjects/7783' title='clocks'>clock</a></p>
</div>
</div>

<div id="page-939">
<h3><a name="page-939">Saturday, July  5, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> some to day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim helped <a href='../subjects/68' title='John Hutcherson'>John Hutcherson</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7308' title='threshing'>thrash</a> <a href='../subjects/7263' title='wheat'>wheat</a> this morning<span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>planted</a> him some <a href='../subjects/7839' title='pink beans'>pink<span class='line-break'> </span> beans</a> this evening after<span class='line-break'> </span> they got up the <a href='../subjects/7301' title='hay'>hay</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>

<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> &amp; got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a> and washed a <span class='line-break'> </span> few things this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening I worked some<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/91' title='button holes'>button holes</a> and <a href='../subjects/182' title='mending'>mended</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> a few things.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7972' title='Lucius Gravely'>Lucius Gravely</a> come here<span class='line-break'> </span> tonight on his way to the <a href='../subjects/85' title='lodge'>lodge</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> He had forgot that last Sunday<span class='line-break'> </span> was a fifth Sundy.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10:30:oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>

<div id="page-940">
<h3><a name="page-940">Sunday, July  6, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good morning.  We all staid<span class='line-break'> </span> at home.  <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7349' title='Evelyn Brumfield'>Evylin</a> come<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  <a href='../subjects/7840' title='Tup Walker'>Mr Tup Walker</a><span class='line-break'> </span> brought them.  <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie Smith</a> and the little <span class='line-break'> </span> children come a little while.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to the <a href='../subjects/357' title='creek'>creek</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Had to hurry back on account<span class='line-break'> </span> of a cloud.  We have had the<span class='line-break'> </span> hardest <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a> I most ever <a href='../subjects/7592' title='saw'>saw</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> The <a href='../subjects/357' title='creek'>branch</a> is as high as I <span class='line-break'> </span> ever saw it.  Washed the <a href='../subjects/414' title='fence'>fence</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> a way below the <a href='../subjects/7841' title='spring'>spring</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Oh I am so sorry a bout the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7447' title='flooding'>high water</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Evylin is playing the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7320' title='piano'>piano</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>

<div id="page-941">
<h3><a name="page-941">Monday, July  7, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day.  This morning <span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/414' title='fence'>fences</a> <a href='../subjects/7447' title='flooding'>washed down</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> away.  I lost a 4 galons of<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7286' title='milk'>milk</a> besides lots of other damage.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sowed</a> some on <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josies</a> <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7349' title='Evelyn Brumfield'>Evylin</a> straitened up the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/318' title='parlor'>parlor</a>.  I <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a>.  It was a <span class='line-break'> </span> hard matter to get a <a href='../subjects/14' title='fire'>fire</a><span class='line-break'> </span> a bout eleven oclock.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7842' title='Mr Glass'>Mr Glass</a> and <a href='../subjects/7843' title='Mr Vonwagner'>Mr Vonwagner</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come.  They eat dinner here.<span class='line-break'> </span> Nell &amp; Evylin went with<span class='line-break'> </span> them to <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The boys killed the <a href='../subjects/7245' title='bees'>bees</a> in <span class='line-break'> </span> two hives this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> There has bin three or four<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>cars</a> passed here today.<span class='line-break'> </span> The <a href='../subjects/233' title='roads'>roads</a> are very bad.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie &amp; the children and I<span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul Bennett</a> got the car in the <a href='../subjects/357' title='creek'>creek</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and never got home until twelve to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10: o clock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-942">
<h3><a name="page-942">Tuesday, July  8, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> fixed up the <a href='../subjects/414' title='fence'>fence</a> that <a href='../subjects/7447' title='flooding'>washed down</a><span class='line-break'> </span> Sunday night.  This evening Jim <span class='line-break'> </span> went &amp; helped <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George Blair</a> <a href='../subjects/7308' title='threshing'>thrash</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7263' title='wheat'>wheat</a>.  Ben and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/7844' title='hauling wheat'>hauled up<span class='line-break'> </span> wheat</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  She cooked<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/236' title='cabbage'>cabbage</a> and <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>potatoes</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7336' title='cymblins'>symblings</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> carried <a href='../subjects/7561' title='Gladys Brumfield'>Gladys</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7652' title='Effie Brumfield Cundiff'>Effie Brumfield</a> to <a href='../subjects/7206' title='White Falls, Virginia'>White Falls</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fishin</a>.  We caught several small<span class='line-break'> </span> fish.  They finished mending the <span class='line-break'> </span> race &amp; commenced <a href='../subjects/7845' title='grinding wheat'>grinding<span class='line-break'> </span> new wheat</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I droped my knife in the <span class='line-break'> </span> river.  The <a href='../subjects/123' title='water'>water</a> was mudy<span class='line-break'> </span> so that I could not see it.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got down and felt for it and<span class='line-break'> </span> found it.  I know it is foolish to<span class='line-break'> </span> to write about it but I keep<span class='line-break'> </span> thinkin a bout the surprize<span class='line-break'> </span> that I found it.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10:30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-943">
<h3><a name="page-943">Wednesday, July  9, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owens</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7844' title='hauling wheat'>hauled up wheat</a>.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> turned<span class='line-break'> </span> some land for a <a href='../subjects/7379' title='turnips'>turnip</a> patch<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  Jim helped <a href='../subjects/7308' title='threshing'>thrash</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7263' title='wheat'>wheat</a> at <a href='../subjects/7309' title='Hutchersons'>Hutchersons</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  This evening<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie &amp; <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> worked a little <span class='line-break'> </span> in the <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> and I went to <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George<span class='line-break'> </span> Blairs</a> then <a href='../subjects/204' title='Isla Blair'>Isla</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/205' title='Cordie Blair'>Cordie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/206' title='Nettie Blair'>Nettie</a> and I and Edna<span class='line-break'> </span> went to the <a href='../subjects/357' title='creek'>creek</a> at<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7846' title='Kellies Bridge'>Kellies Bridge</a>.  We caught<span class='line-break'> </span> caught a few <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia</a> baked some <a href='../subjects/160' title='tea cakes'>tea cakes</a><span class='line-break'> </span> while we were gone.  I certainly<span class='line-break'> </span> did enjoy them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-944">
<h3><a name="page-944">Thursday, July 10, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  They <a href='../subjects/7308' title='threshing'>thrashed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7263' title='wheat'>wheat</a> here and at <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a><span class='line-break'> </span> today.  <a href='../subjects/7215' title='William Brumfield'>Willie Brumfield</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7847' title='Dr Cutor'>Dr Cutor</a> come to day.<span class='line-break'> </span> They eat <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> here.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> picked 3 gallons<span class='line-break'> </span> of <a href='../subjects/7299' title='black berries'>black berries</a> and <a href='../subjects/7371' title='canning'>caned</a><span class='line-break'> </span> them.  I picked a few<span class='line-break'> </span> beries this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> They are plentiful this <span class='line-break'> </span> year.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10:15 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-945">
<h3><a name="page-945">Friday, July 11, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went to help <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johnson Reynolds</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7308' title='threshing'>thrash</a> <a href='../subjects/7263' title='wheat'>wheat</a>.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> in<span class='line-break'> </span> his <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> all day.  Jim <span class='line-break'> </span> helped him this evening.  To night<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben &amp; Jim has gone to nail up<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/414' title='fence'>the gate</a>.  The <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cows</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/133' title='horses'>horses</a> got in<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a> last night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  This evening<span class='line-break'> </span> she picked a bucket full<span class='line-break'> </span> of <a href='../subjects/7299' title='black berries'>black berries</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I though I would pick <span class='line-break'> </span> some berries but did not get <span class='line-break'> </span> many.  I felt so bad that <span class='line-break'> </span> I did not get many berries.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10:30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-946">
<h3><a name="page-946">Saturday, July 12, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to<span class='line-break'> </span> the meeting of the <a href='../subjects/221' title='school board'>school board</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and a meeting of some sort a<span class='line-break'> </span> gain to night.  He has gone to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a> to the meeting of <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7362' title='Odd Fellows'>odd fellows</a>.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7972' title='Lucius Gravely'>Lucius Gravely</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went with him.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> worked all day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a> went to the <a href='../subjects/44' title='mill'>mill</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  She baked<span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/170' title='pies'>pies</a> for Sundays dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> was finishing <span class='line-break'> </span> up the little girls <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dresses</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10:10 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-947">
<h3><a name="page-947">Sunday, July 13, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  It <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rained</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning at two oclock this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning. We all staid at home <span class='line-break'> </span> until after <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> time.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; family went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7276' title='Robert Hubbard'>Rob Hubards</a>.  Come back<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7240' title='Jim Power'>Jim Powers</a>.  They got<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a> there.  They had <a href='../subjects/248' title='ham'>ham</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/55' title='ice cream'>ice cream</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7231' title='Ethel Worsham'>Ethel<span class='line-break'> </span> Worsham</a> and all of her<span class='line-break'> </span> family.  They have a nice<span class='line-break'> </span> lot of children.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7562' title='Stuart Owen'>Dr Owens son</a> and <a href='../subjects/7849' title='Mr Rucker'>Mr Ruckers<span class='line-break'> </span> son</a> was there.  I come home<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/15' title='milking'>milked</a> the <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cows</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> got supper for <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> and I.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 11 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-948">
<h3><a name="page-948">Monday, July 14, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>shower</a> this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Clear this evening.  The men<span class='line-break'> </span> commenced to <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plow</a> but the rain<span class='line-break'> </span> stoped them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> carried me <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7211' title='Cedar Forest, Virginia'>Cedar Forest</a>.  We caught<span class='line-break'> </span> a few <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a>.  Stoped at <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait<span class='line-break'> </span> Stone</a> and got a few things.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie</a> come today.  Her &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> picked <a href='../subjects/7299' title='black berries'>black berries</a> all the evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate</a> come this evening.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; Jim went with her home.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1630' title='Virginia Harvey'>Virginia</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7851' title='Brookneal, Virginia'>Brookneal</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  She went to <a href='../subjects/7852' title='Ed Harvey'>Ed<span class='line-break'> </span> Harveys</a> to visit.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/203' title='Alma Bennett'>Alma Bennett</a> come to <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a><span class='line-break'> </span> yesterday.  She is doing some <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewing</a>.  I want to go and <span class='line-break'> </span> see her soon.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10:30 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-949">
<h3><a name="page-949">Tuesday, July 15, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good morning.  <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>Rain</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening and tonight.  The <a href='../subjects/357' title='creek'>branch</a><span class='line-break'> </span> has bin out of the banks and<span class='line-break'> </span> washed a way the <a href='../subjects/7853' title='foot bridge'>foot bridge</a><span class='line-break'> </span> the third time in the last <span class='line-break'> </span> month.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> in their <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie</a> made <a href='../subjects/251' title='preserves'>preserves</a> and <a href='../subjects/7371' title='canning'>caned</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7816' title='berries'>berries</a> all the morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I <a href='../subjects/15' title='milking'>milked</a> two<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cows</a> and Josie one.  She helped me<span class='line-break'> </span> milk.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/153' title='Ren Worsham'>Wren Worsham</a> carried me<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and <a href='../subjects/204' title='Isla Blair'>Isla Blair</a> to <a href='../subjects/7854' title='Worshams pond'>Worshams<span class='line-break'> </span> pond</a> to <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a>.  I caught 4 small carp.<span class='line-break'> </span> I was glad to get them.  We got<span class='line-break'> </span> back as far as <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George Blairs</a> before<span class='line-break'> </span> it <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rained</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7855' title='George William Blair'>George Jr</a> brought us home.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am glad that they are so good to me.<span class='line-break'> </span> I eat dinner with Wren &amp; Isla at a good<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7841' title='spring'>spring</a> on the hill.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7856' title='Suiter? Blair'>Suiter? Blair</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and wife &amp; son come to George Blairs<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  I wanted to see <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia</a> but she was at <a href='../subjects/7231' title='Ethel Worsham'>Ethels</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I milked the cows after <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10:30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-950">
<h3><a name="page-950">Wednesday, July 16, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> morning.  A hard <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  The <a href='../subjects/357' title='creek'>branch</a> was all out of<span class='line-break'> </span> the banks a gain.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> started to <a href='../subjects/7203' title='Long Island, Virginia'>the Island</a>.  They had got as<span class='line-break'> </span> far as Arch Moons when the rain<span class='line-break'> </span> began to <a href='../subjects/120' title='falling'>fall</a>.  When [it] quit so that they<span class='line-break'> </span> could, they come back home.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  Josie made <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> a<span class='line-break'> </span> blouse.  I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/203' title='Alma Bennett'>Alma</a> was makeing <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> a<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a>.  Marvin went to the <a href='../subjects/44' title='mill'>mill</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  Did not get his <span class='line-break'> </span> grain ground.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Jim brought the <a href='../subjects/134' title='hogs'>olde hog</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-951">
<h3><a name="page-951">Thursday, July 17, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rainy</a> day.  We could<span class='line-break'> </span> not get any <a href='../subjects/123' title='water'>water</a> out of the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7841' title='spring'>spring</a> that would do to use until<span class='line-break'> </span> nearly night.  The men folks<span class='line-break'> </span> cant do anything in the crop.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to <a href='../subjects/419' title='Travis Dews'>Mr Dews</a> to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7229' title='croquet'>play croquet</a>.  It <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rained</a> so<span class='line-break'> </span> hard that they had to quit.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We had <a href='../subjects/296' title='fried chicken'>fried chicken</a> for <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  Did not try to get vegetables.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sowed</a> some.  Made <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a><span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/7606' title='shirts'>shirt</a>.  <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie</a> worked some<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/91' title='button holes'>button holes</a> in <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklins</a><span class='line-break'> </span> clothes.  Henry &amp; <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George Blairs</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> They are trying to learn to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/448' title='play'>recite some pieces</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9: oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-952">
<h3><a name="page-952">Friday, July 18, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rainy</a> day.  It has <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rained</a> some for<span class='line-break'> </span> five days.  Every thing is nearly drowned.<span class='line-break'> </span> The men folks has not done anything<span class='line-break'> </span> much to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie</a> washed <span class='line-break'> </span> and dried and <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> some of her<span class='line-break'> </span> clothes this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I <a href='../subjects/15' title='milking'>milk</a> and churn.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewed</a> some this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/104' title='Tom Edmonds'>Tom Edmons</a> has <a href='../subjects/7354' title='curing'>cured</a> a<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>house</a> of <a href='../subjects/7347' title='primings'>primings</a>, the first <span class='line-break'> </span> that has bin cured a bout here.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9:30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-953">
<h3><a name="page-953">Saturday, July 19, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rainy</a> morning and it is<span class='line-break'> </span> raining to night.  Did not rain all day<span class='line-break'> </span> but the most of it.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a>ried <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie</a> to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  To day she<span class='line-break'> </span> is <a href='../subjects/81' title='complaining'>complaining</a> is hardly <span class='line-break'> </span> able to go.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The children and I went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  <a href='../subjects/203' title='Alma Bennett'>Alma Bennett</a><span class='line-break'> </span> was makeing <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> a <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie got early <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim did not get any dinner <span class='line-break'> </span> today.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9:30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-954">
<h3><a name="page-954">Sunday, July 20, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rainy</a> morning.  Has not <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rained</a><span class='line-break'> </span> so much to day.  We all staid<span class='line-break'> </span> at home until after <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to <a href='../subjects/67' title='Willie Mayhew'>Mayhews</a>.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George Blair</a> come<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  I was so sorry<span class='line-break'> </span> that the boys was not at<span class='line-break'> </span> home.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got dinner.  <span class='line-break'> </span> She cooked <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7237' title='butter beans'>butter beans</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and made a <a href='../subjects/46' title='pudding'>pudding</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> We all enjoyed our dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Heard tonight that <a href='../subjects/51' title='Jack Harvey'>Jack Harvey</a> &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7858' title='Bob Booker'>Bob Booker</a> got home this evening.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-955">
<h3><a name="page-955">Monday, July 21, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p><a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>Rain</a> a gain to day.  The boys<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7316' title='topping'>toped</a> some <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed some this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning and went to <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to see <a href='../subjects/335' title='Margaret Brumfield'>Mag</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  They were all<span class='line-break'> </span> well.  <a href='../subjects/424' title='Doris Brumfield'>Doris</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7859' title='Fannie'>Fannie</a> had gone<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/316' title='Mrs Kellie'>Mrs Kellies</a>.  I come by<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kates</a> to see <a href='../subjects/51' title='Jack Harvey'>Jack</a> but did<span class='line-break'> </span> not see him.  <a href='../subjects/52' title='Irvin Harvey'>Irvin</a> &amp; Jack had <span class='line-break'> </span> gone to <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lee Brumfields</a> for<span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/7398' title='apples'>aples</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I started to walk up there.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went by <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a><span class='line-break'> </span> wanted to take me and they<span class='line-break'> </span> let him.  I am mighty glad<span class='line-break'> </span> that they did as it <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rained</a> so<span class='line-break'> </span> hard that I could of hardly<span class='line-break'> </span> got home.  <a href='../subjects/205' title='Cordie Blair'>Cordie</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/206' title='Nettie Blair'>Nettie</a> was<span class='line-break'> </span> at the store.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-956">
<h3><a name="page-956">Tuesday, July 22, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p><a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>Rain</a> a gain to day.  Old as I am<span class='line-break'> </span> I don't think I ever saw such<span class='line-break'> </span> a time.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> an <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul Bennett</a><span class='line-break'> </span> all started to <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> We have not heard a word from <span class='line-break'> </span> them yet.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> &amp; the children <span class='line-break'> </span> staid here all day and they are<span class='line-break'> </span> here tonight.  <a href='../subjects/51' title='Jack Harvey'>Jack Harvey</a> come <span class='line-break'> </span> to see us today.  He is lookin<span class='line-break'> </span> well.  Heard to day that <a href='../subjects/252' title='Mrs Hutcherson'>Mrs Hutcherson</a><span class='line-break'> </span> had come home.  Hope she may get well.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I had a <a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a> from <a href='../subjects/209' title='John Brumfield'>John</a> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/203' title='Alma Bennett'>Alma Bennett</a> made me a <a href='../subjects/7861' title='bonnets'>bonnet</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-957">
<h3><a name="page-957">Wednesday, July 23, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p><a href='../subjects/187' title='cloudy'>Cloudy</a> most of the day but<span class='line-break'> </span> no rain.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to Strait<span class='line-break'> </span> Stone this evening and got<span class='line-break'> </span> roofing for the <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barns</a> and <a href='../subjects/7813' title='ice cream freezer'>ice cream freezer</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> went some where and got<span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/370' title='pigs'>pigs</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johnson Reynolds</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7224' title='Julia Ferguson'>Julia Fergerson</a><span class='line-break'> </span> was there and <a href='../subjects/7333' title='Jane Reynolds'>Cliftons wife</a> <a href='../subjects/7720' title='Clifton Reynolds, Jr.'>&amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> baby</a> came this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie Reynolds</a> went to see<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/252' title='Mrs Hutcherson'>Mrs Hutcherson</a>.  She is mighty<span class='line-break'> </span> feeble.  <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul Bennett</a> come from<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a> to day.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> did not<span class='line-break'> </span> come.  <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait<span class='line-break'> </span> Stone</a> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese Smith</a><span class='line-break'> </span> carried her.  I walked to<span class='line-break'> </span> Reynolds and walke most every<span class='line-break'> </span> where else that I can.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Oh that I could help my self.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-958">
<h3><a name="page-958">Thursday, July 24, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/7316' title='topping'>toped some<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco</a> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening I went to see<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/252' title='Mrs Hutcherson'>Mrs Hutcherson</a>.  She is very<span class='line-break'> </span> feeble.  <a href='../subjects/7863' title='Mrs Peak'>Mrs Peak</a> &amp; children was<span class='line-break'> </span> there.  Mrs Hutcherson gave me<span class='line-break'> </span> a bucket of <a href='../subjects/7398' title='apples'>apples</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7864' title='Rena Mayhew'>Rena<span class='line-break'> </span> Mayhew</a> and <a href='../subjects/7535' title='Ada Hutcherson'>Ada Hutcherson</a><span class='line-break'> </span> brough them for me over half<span class='line-break'> </span> way home.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie &amp; <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> The Hutcherson and Worsham<span class='line-break'> </span> and Brumfield &amp; Smith <span class='line-break'> </span> children all met at<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Blairs</a> this evening to<span class='line-break'> </span> practice some pieces to say<span class='line-break'> </span> at church some day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-959">
<h3><a name="page-959">Friday, July 25, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> helped<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/18' title='Edmonds'>Edmons</a> build a <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> and <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> come<span class='line-break'> </span> from <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a> to day.  They<span class='line-break'> </span> had bin <a href='../subjects/7865' title='jury duty'>on a jurie</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> cooked a big pot of<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7277' title='green beans'>snaps</a>.  She <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> most<span class='line-break'> </span> of the day and is <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben carried <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> &amp; I<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7206' title='White Falls, Virginia'>White Falls</a>.  I caught<span class='line-break'> </span> several small <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a>.  <a href='../subjects/51' title='Jack Harvey'>Jack<span class='line-break'> </span> Harvey</a> come &amp; got the team <span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/115' title='wagon'>waggon</a> and went to the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/44' title='mill'>mill</a> for <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>his mother</a> and <a href='../subjects/7547' title='hauling wood'>hauled<span class='line-break'> </span> some wood</a>.  <a href='../subjects/203' title='Alma Bennett'>Alma</a> is at <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-960">
<h3><a name="page-960">Saturday, July 26, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7851' title='Brookneal, Virginia'>Brookneal</a> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/7378' title='sowing'>sowed</a> a <a href='../subjects/7379' title='turnips'>turnip patch</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  She killed<span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chicken</a> and baked <a href='../subjects/170' title='pies'>pies</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <a href='../subjects/203' title='Alma Bennett'>Alma Bennett</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> I staid with the children.<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin and <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a> to <a href='../subjects/7228' title='preaching'>preaching</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> The <a href='../subjects/7866' title='protracted meeting'>protracted meeting</a><span class='line-break'> </span> commenced to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/231' title='Earl Bennett'>Earl</a> and <a href='../subjects/230' title='Lizzie Bennett'>Lizzie Bennett</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come to <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Lizzie come with me home. <span class='line-break'> </span> I am glad that she came.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/92' title='Mr Hutcherson'>Mr Hutchersons</a> by themselves<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 12 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-961">
<h3><a name="page-961">Sunday, July 27, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> staid<span class='line-break'> </span> at home all day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7203' title='Long Island, Virginia'>Long Island</a> and brought<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/216' title='Mary Brumfield'>Mary Brumfield</a> home with him.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/230' title='Lizzie Bennett'>Lizzie Bennett</a> and [I] went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a> to <a href='../subjects/7228' title='preaching'>preaching</a>.  <a href='../subjects/231' title='Earl Bennett'>Earl<span class='line-break'> </span> Bennett</a> carried us and brough<span class='line-break'> </span> us home.  They had <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> on<span class='line-break'> </span> the ground and had a plenty<span class='line-break'> </span> for all hands.  Ben carried<span class='line-break'> </span> Lizzie to <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johnson Reynolds</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to night.  Mary &amp; <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> all went with him.<span class='line-break'> </span> They have not got back <span class='line-break'> </span> yet.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got dinner at <span class='line-break'> </span> home.  She cooked a <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chicken</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7237' title='butter beans'>butter beans</a> and <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> &amp; all of his family<span class='line-break'> </span> were there at preaching &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/153' title='Ren Worsham'>Ren</a> and his family.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-962">
<h3><a name="page-962">Monday, July 28, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>Clear this morning.  A <a href='../subjects/7868' title='thunder shower'>thunder sower</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  The men folks <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> some this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  This evening she<span class='line-break'> </span> kept <a href='../subjects/7654' title='Eva Smith'>Eva Carries baby</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/325' title='Paul Smith'>Paul</a> and <a href='../subjects/212' title='Roy Smith'>Roy</a> was here two.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/216' title='Mary Brumfield'>Mary Brumfield</a> was here all <span class='line-break'> </span> the evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went with <a href='../subjects/7652' title='Effie Brumfield Cundiff'>Effie Brumfield</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7206' title='White Falls, Virginia'>White Falls</a>.  We had <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lees</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/133' title='horses'>hors</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/268' title='buggy'>buggy</a>.  We caught<span class='line-break'> </span> several <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a>.  We got as far<span class='line-break'> </span> on our way home as <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate<span class='line-break'> </span> Harvey</a>.  Effie brought me as<span class='line-break'> </span> far on my way home as the<span class='line-break'> </span> forks of the road at <a href='../subjects/7408' title='Johnsons'>Johnsons</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barns</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7867' title='preachers'>The Preachers</a> come<span class='line-break'> </span> home with <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin Smith</a><span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10:30 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> comed my hair<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening while it was <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>raining</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-963">
<h3><a name="page-963">Tuesday, July 29, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> morning.  A <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>shower</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/7316' title='topping'>topped</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <a href='../subjects/216' title='Mary Brumfield'>Mary</a> dressed<span class='line-break'> </span> to go to meeting and <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a><span class='line-break'> </span> did not bring the children<span class='line-break'> </span> so she did not get to go.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7870' title='Dr ?aton'>Dr [?aton] </a> was here today<span class='line-break'> </span> him and his assistant.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7821' title='Dr Bennett'>Dr Bennett</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7871' title='Sam Bennett'>Sam Bennett</a><span class='line-break'> </span> was here to day.  They are<span class='line-break'> </span> anxious a bout the election.<span class='line-break'> </span> I want Bennett elected<span class='line-break'> </span> and don't know why.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben went to <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Rennan</a> today<span class='line-break'> </span> to talk to <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lee Brumfield</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Mary &amp; <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a>, <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> all went to <a href='../subjects/92' title='Mr Hutcherson'>Mr<span class='line-break'> </span> Hutchersons</a> for <a href='../subjects/7398' title='apples'>apples</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-964">
<h3><a name="page-964">Wednesday, July 30, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
