<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> some this morning.  This<span class='line-break'> </span> evening they went to <a href='../subjects/7872' title='Brutus, Virginia'>Brutus</a> to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7498' title='speaking'>a speakin</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7873' title='John L. Hunt'>John L. Hunt</a> done the<span class='line-break'> </span> talkin.  There is a meeting of<span class='line-break'> </span> men at <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a>.  The boys<span class='line-break'> </span> would not go.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I helped<span class='line-break'> </span> put up the dishes.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I chopped the grass out of the <span class='line-break'> </span> walk this evening then went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> a few minutes.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben brought two <a href='../subjects/7324' title='watermelons'>water mellons</a><span class='line-break'> </span> home this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/216' title='Mary Brumfield'>Mary Brumfield</a> went to <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Blairs</a> this morning.  She <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a>ed<span class='line-break'> </span> in some of the girls clothes<span class='line-break'> </span> and went to Strait Stone.<span class='line-break'> </span> She come back here tonight<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; I am glad to have<span class='line-break'> </span> her here.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10: oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-965">
<h3><a name="page-965">Thursday, July 31, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day but a hard<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/314' title='thunder cloud'>thunder cloud</a> and hard rain<span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> a little<span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to Greenfield<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7767' title='Chalk Level, Virginia'>Chalk Level</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr. Owen</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait<span class='line-break'> </span> Stone</a> to <a href='../subjects/7228' title='preaching'>preaching</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> staid at home and <span class='line-break'> </span> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  She cooked <a href='../subjects/7277' title='green beans'>snaps</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>potatoes</a> and <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I certainly did enjoy my<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> carried <a href='../subjects/216' title='Mary Brumfield'>Mary</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna Brumfield</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> I to <a href='../subjects/7854' title='Worshams pond'>Worshams pond</a>.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> caugh one nice <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Mary went to Preaching<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  To night she<span class='line-break'> </span> is at <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George Blairs</a>.  <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul<span class='line-break'> </span> Bennett</a> carried her.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am so glad that <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben got home before it<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rained</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9:30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-966">
<h3><a name="page-966">Friday, August  1, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7331' title='suckering'>suckered tobacco</a> most of the day.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr. Owen</a> went to meeting.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> commenced work on<span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/7356' title='curtains'>curtains</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening Josie kept <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a><span class='line-break'> </span> children.  They did well to<span class='line-break'> </span> be so small.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/216' title='Mary Brumfield'>Mary Brumfield</a> went to see<span class='line-break'> </span> her <a href='../subjects/335' title='Margaret Brumfield'>Aunt Mag</a>  this evening<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; come to <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Aunt Mollies</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7497' title='Reuben Reynolds'>Reubin <span class='line-break'> </span> Reynolds</a> brough her home.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> There was <a href='../subjects/7498' title='speaking'>speakin</a> at <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9:30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-967">
<h3><a name="page-967">Saturday, August  2, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7331' title='suckering'>suckered tobacco</a> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening Ben went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a> to meet <a href='../subjects/209' title='John Brumfield'>John</a> &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> his children.  They are<span class='line-break'> </span> all here to night.  <a href='../subjects/216' title='Mary Brumfield'>Mary</a><span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield went to <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lee Brumfield</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  Walked all the way<span class='line-break'> </span> up there.  <a href='../subjects/951' title='Oscar Brumfield'>Oscar</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/39' title='Helen Brumfield'>Hellen</a> come<span class='line-break'> </span> with her back home.  They would<span class='line-break'> </span> not come in and have <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a> with <span class='line-break'> </span> us.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> staid at home &amp; got <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I went to <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johnson</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Reynolds</a> to spend the day.  I eat<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner there.  <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie</a> had a good<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner.  <a href='../subjects/7497' title='Reuben Reynolds'>Reubin</a> brough me home<span class='line-break'> </span> as soon as I heard that John was <span class='line-break'> </span> comeing.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> went <span class='line-break'> </span> to meeting this morning.  Carrie &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> the children was here this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/203' title='Alma Bennett'>Alma Bennett</a> is at <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lees</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to night.  Jim brought home<span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/7250' title='cucumber'>cucumbers</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/250' title='tomatoes'>tomatoes</a><span class='line-break'> </span> from the tobacco ground this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-968">
<h3><a name="page-968">Sunday, August  3, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  We all staid<span class='line-break'> </span> at home.  <a href='../subjects/209' title='John Brumfield'>John</a> &amp; his children<span class='line-break'> </span> was here.  <a href='../subjects/216' title='Mary Brumfield'>Mary Brumfield</a> &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/424' title='Doris Brumfield'>Doris</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7651' title='Janie Brumfield'>Janie Brumfield</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7561' title='Gladys Brumfield'>Gladis</a> <a href='../subjects/427' title='Floyd Reynolds'>Floid<span class='line-break'> </span> Reynolds</a> and <a href='../subjects/52' title='Irvin Harvey'>Irvin Harvey</a> was all<span class='line-break'> </span> here this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  We had <span class='line-break'> </span> a nice <a href='../subjects/7501' title='roast beef'>roast of beef</a> <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie<span class='line-break'> </span> Reynolds</a> gave me.<span class='line-break'> </span> I think all enjoyed them<span class='line-break'> </span> selves.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Mary &amp; <a href='../subjects/7502' title='Edwin Brumfield'>Edwin</a> had quite<span class='line-break'> </span> an arguament a bout woman<span class='line-break'> </span> voteing.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10: oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-969">
<h3><a name="page-969">Monday, August  4, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/7331' title='suckering'>suckered</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> all day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> carried<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/216' title='Mary Brumfield'>Mary B</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7240' title='Jim Power'>Jim Powers</a>.  They spent<span class='line-break'> </span> the day.  He brough them home<span class='line-break'> </span> to night.  <a href='../subjects/7275' title='Fannie Power'>Fanny Power</a> come<span class='line-break'> </span> with them.  <a href='../subjects/209' title='John Brumfield'>John</a> &amp; his children<span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> this evening<span class='line-break'> </span> and from there to <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johnson<span class='line-break'> </span> Reynolds</a>.  <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went with<span class='line-break'> </span> them.  <a href='../subjects/7386' title='Christine Reynolds'>Christenia Reynols</a> &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7514' title='Ruth Barker'>Ruth Barker</a> come here<span class='line-break'> </span> a while this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1630' title='Virginia Harvey'>Virginia Harvey</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/39' title='Helen Brumfield'>Hellen<span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield</a> come to night.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7515' title='Mr Smith'>Mr Smith</a> brought them<span class='line-break'> </span> on a <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I gathered a few <a href='../subjects/304' title='beans'>beans</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening &amp; killed two <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chickens</a> for <a href='../subjects/26' title='breakfast'>breakfast</a><span class='line-break'> </span> in the morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 11 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-970">
<h3><a name="page-970">Tuesday, August  5, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> worked on the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> most of the day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> staid<span class='line-break'> </span> at <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a> all day as one of the<span class='line-break'> </span> judges of the <a href='../subjects/7546' title='election'>election</a>.  He has just<span class='line-break'> </span> come home.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/216' title='Mary Brumfield'>Mary</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7275' title='Fannie Power'>Fanny</a> has gone to <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lee<span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfields</a> and <a href='../subjects/7502' title='Edwin Brumfield'>Edwin</a> went two.<span class='line-break'> </span> They will come home to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  Mary &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> Fannie washed dishes after<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner.  I picked a few <a href='../subjects/304' title='beans'>beans</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and cut a few <a href='../subjects/7250' title='cucumber'>cucumbers</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and gathered some <a href='../subjects/250' title='tomatoes'>tomatoes</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Then I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a><span class='line-break'> </span> a few minutes.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> was fixin <a href='../subjects/250' title='tomatoes'>tomatoes</a> <a href='../subjects/7371' title='canning'>to can</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I helped her peel some<span class='line-break'> </span> tomatoes.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 11: oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-971">
<h3><a name="page-971">Wednesday, August  6, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A little <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a> this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Clear this evening.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/209' title='John Brumfield'>John</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/7894' title='pulling leaves'>pulled leaves</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> worked in <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Bens</a><span class='line-break'> </span> place while he carried <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/216' title='Mary Brumfield'>Mary Brumfield</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7275' title='Fannie Power'>Fanny Power</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7607' title='Mr Power'>Mr Powers</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7502' title='Edwin Brumfield'>Edwin</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin<span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield</a> went with him.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7514' title='Ruth Barker'>Ruth Barker</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7386' title='Christine Reynolds'>Christenia<span class='line-break'> </span> Reynolds</a> eat <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> with <span class='line-break'> </span> us and spent the evening<span class='line-break'> </span> with us.  <a href='../subjects/7224' title='Julia Ferguson'>Julia Fergerson</a><span class='line-break'> </span> was at <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got dinner.  This evening<span class='line-break'> </span> she went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We heard to day that <a href='../subjects/7874' title='Miss Moon'>Miss<span class='line-break'> </span> Moon</a> was <a href='../subjects/96' title='death'>dead</a> that was staying<span class='line-break'> </span> at <a href='../subjects/8608' title='Mr Bookers'>Bookers</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7502' title='Edwin Brumfield'>Edwin Brumfield</a> dried the dishes<span class='line-break'> </span> to night.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-972">
<h3><a name="page-972">Thursday, August  7, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A day.  The men folks<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7894' title='pulling leaves'>pulled leaves</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7502' title='Edwin Brumfield'>Edwin Brumfield</a><span class='line-break'> </span> helped them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7365' title='John Baily'>John</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7519' title='Christinia Brumfield'>Christenia Brumfield</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George Blairs</a> this morning and <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lee Brumfields</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> She worked on <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> a <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/349' title='Minnie Owen'>Mrs. Owen</a> went to see <span class='line-break'> </span> her brother to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening I went to the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7363' title='corn field'>corn field</a> to see if there<span class='line-break'> </span> was any <a href='../subjects/7277' title='green beans'>snaps</a>.  I could not<span class='line-break'> </span> get any.  I think all concidered<span class='line-break'> </span> they have got the sorriest crop<span class='line-break'> </span> I ever saw.  I know they<span class='line-break'> </span> worke and tried but it is <span class='line-break'> </span> drowned.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a><span class='line-break'> </span> a few minutes.  <a href='../subjects/203' title='Alma Bennett'>Alma</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come while I was there.<span class='line-break'> </span> I feel age and infirmities<span class='line-break'> </span> so much and hear so much<span class='line-break'> </span> complaint a bout things that<span class='line-break'> </span> no one can help that I cant<span class='line-break'> </span> hardly stand it.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10:10 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-973">
<h3><a name="page-973">Friday, August  8, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The men folks<span class='line-break'> </span> finished <a href='../subjects/7894' title='pulling leaves'>pulling leaves</a> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7502' title='Edwin Brumfield'>Edwin</a> went <a href='../subjects/7476' title='squirrel hunting'>squirrel hunting</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  He killed two<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7235' title='squirrels'>squirrels</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> and finished <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Ednas</a> <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a> &amp; dressed Ednas<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7517' title='doll'>doll</a> very nicely.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/209' title='John Brumfield'>John</a> went with me <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fishing</a><span class='line-break'> </span> the first time and I expect <span class='line-break'> </span> it will be the last time.<span class='line-break'> </span> We came by <a href='../subjects/379' title='Jim Thompson'>Jim Thomsons</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and saw him and all of his<span class='line-break'> </span> family.  Jim gave us a nice<span class='line-break'> </span> basket of <a href='../subjects/7398' title='apples'>apples</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> We caught several little fish.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/424' title='Doris Brumfield'>Doris Brumfield</a> is here <span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.  She is visiting <a href='../subjects/7519' title='Christinia Brumfield'>Christenia<span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10: oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-974">
<h3><a name="page-974">Saturday, August  9, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/7365' title='John Baily'>John</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7519' title='Christinia Brumfield'>Christenia</a><span class='line-break'> </span> started home this morning on a <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/268' title='buggy'>buggy</a>.  <a href='../subjects/424' title='Doris Brumfield'>Doris</a> went with them<span class='line-break'> </span> as far as <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7502' title='Edwin Brumfield'>Edwin</a> staid<span class='line-break'> </span> here and helped <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> cover the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a>.  They did not get done.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> She baked a <a href='../subjects/240' title='cake'>cake</a> and to<span class='line-break'> </span> night she is <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a>.  I hope she<span class='line-break'> </span> may be better by morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  Did not stay<span class='line-break'> </span> but a few minutes.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> To night the men has <span class='line-break'> </span> all <a href='../subjects/7393' title='firing'>gone to the barn</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-975">
<h3><a name="page-975">Sunday, August 10, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/7393' title='firing'>fired</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> all day.  Quit at night.<span class='line-break'> </span> Has cured two <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>houses</a> of <a href='../subjects/7347' title='primings'>primings</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7502' title='Edwin Brumfield'>Edwin</a> staid here all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul Bennett</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7260' title='Lonnie Bennett'>Loney</a> come<span class='line-break'> </span> a little while this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> Paul got his <a href='../subjects/7520' title='hair cut'>hair cut</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  Ben and <span class='line-break'> </span> family went to <a href='../subjects/7240' title='Jim Power'>Jim Powers</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7276' title='Robert Hubbard'>Rob Hubards</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I <a href='../subjects/15' title='milking'>milked</a> &amp; got <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and Jim, Edwin, and I<span class='line-break'> </span> eat before they got home.<span class='line-break'> </span> I have not heard from <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Edwin finished reading<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7521' title='Philo Gubb'>Philo Gubb</a> to day &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> slept two hours.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I read some in the land<span class='line-break'> </span> mark &amp; [?].<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10:30 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-976">
<h3><a name="page-976">Monday, August 11, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7502' title='Edwin Brumfield'>Edwin</a><span class='line-break'> </span> finished covering the <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  They commenced to <a href='../subjects/7388' title='tobacco cutting'>cut</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> this evening.  They cut for<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr. Owen</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7365' title='John Baily'>John</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7519' title='Christinia Brumfield'>Christenia</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come back this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> and starched<span class='line-break'> </span> some clothes.  I cut some<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7250' title='cucumber'>cucumbers</a> and gathered <span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/250' title='tomatoes'>tomatoes</a>.  We <a href='../subjects/7371' title='canning'>canned</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> some tomatoes this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a><span class='line-break'> </span> was there.  I want to see Kate.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The boys are all gone to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a> tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10: oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-977">
<h3><a name="page-977">Tuesday, August 12, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rainy</a> day most of <span class='line-break'> </span> the time.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> finished <a href='../subjects/7388' title='tobacco cutting'>cutting</a> a <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>house</a><span class='line-break'> </span> of <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7365' title='John Baily'>John</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7502' title='Edwin Brumfield'>Edwin</a><span class='line-break'> </span> work on the <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> &amp; I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I <a href='../subjects/7371' title='canning'>can</a>ed<span class='line-break'> </span> a few <a href='../subjects/250' title='tomatoes'>tomatoes</a>.  I went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie Reynols</a> gave us<span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/7314' title='peaches'>peaches</a>.  <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul Bennett</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went after them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I helped <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> peel her<span class='line-break'> </span> fruit &amp; then helped <span class='line-break'> </span> Josie peel hers.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-978">
<h3><a name="page-978">Wednesday, August 13, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7331' title='suckering'>suckered</a> some <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a>.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a> and got<span class='line-break'> </span> some roofin.  <a href='../subjects/209' title='John Brumfield'>John</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7502' title='Edwin Brumfield'>Edwin</a><span class='line-break'> </span> finished covering the <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and helpe work in the<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco a while.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben carried Edwin &amp; <a href='../subjects/7386' title='Christine Reynolds'>Christenia</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7771' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield (b 1878)'>Henry</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> and I to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7206' title='White Falls, Virginia'>White Falls</a>.  The river was<span class='line-break'> </span> two full &amp; mudy.  So we <span class='line-break'> </span> soon come home.  I come by<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7408' title='Johnsons'>Johnsons</a>.  <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie</a> was makin<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7373' title='jelly'>grape jellie</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7361' title='Julia Brumfield'>Julia</a> was washin<span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/259' title='meal'>meal</a> that she had<span class='line-break'> </span> bought.  <a href='../subjects/369' title='Kate Reynolds'>Kate Hubbard</a> was<span class='line-break'> </span> taken <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a> today.  I hope <span class='line-break'> </span> she will soon be well a gain.<span class='line-break'> </span> I come by <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> She was pickin <a href='../subjects/7368' title='grapes'>grapes</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10:10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-979">
<h3><a name="page-979">Thursday, August 14, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good morning.  <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>Rain</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> <a href='../subjects/7331' title='suckering'>suckered</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> all day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a>.  <a href='../subjects/209' title='John Brumfield'>John</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7502' title='Edwin Brumfield'>Edwin</a> and <a href='../subjects/7519' title='Christinia Brumfield'>Christenia</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a>.  John gave <span class='line-break'> </span> them all <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> at the <a href='../subjects/7876' title='hotel'>hotel</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Kate &amp; Ben was in the rain<span class='line-break'> </span> comeing home.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> some.<span class='line-break'> </span> We both got dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> I <a href='../subjects/7371' title='canning'>caned</a> five <a href='../subjects/7371' title='canning'>cans</a> of <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/250' title='tomatoes'>tomatoes</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> and <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George Blairs</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie got uneasy a bout<span class='line-break'> </span> them, a fraid they would<span class='line-break'> </span> be in a hard cloud<span class='line-break'> </span> but they got home before<span class='line-break'> </span> it <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rained</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I thought that <a href='../subjects/7224' title='Julia Ferguson'>Julia<span class='line-break'> </span> Fergerson</a> would come but<span class='line-break'> </span> she did not.  Don't know<span class='line-break'> </span> what is the matter.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-980">
<h3><a name="page-980">Friday, August 15, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> worked on the <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> all day.  <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a><span class='line-break'> </span> has a <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a> full that they are<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7354' title='curing'>curing</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7240' title='Jim Power'>Jim Powers</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> with her.  <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> staid with me<span class='line-break'> </span> until <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  Then she went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> and staid all the evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I made a few <a href='../subjects/7457' title='pears'>pear</a> <a href='../subjects/251' title='preserves'>preserves</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/202' title='Prince'>Prince</a> the <a href='../subjects/133' title='horses'>horse</a> has been <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a><span class='line-break'> </span> all day.  He got to some <a href='../subjects/7263' title='wheat'>wheat</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and eat two much.  Heard that <span class='line-break'> </span> one of the <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lees</a> <a href='../subjects/133' title='horses'>horses</a> got its leg<span class='line-break'> </span> broke yesterday and they killed<span class='line-break'> </span> him.  I am very sorry a bout<span class='line-break'> </span> it.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie got <a href='../subjects/7314' title='peaches'>peaches</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7387' title='damsons'>damsons</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to preserve and <a href='../subjects/7371' title='canning'>can</a>. Guess<span class='line-break'> </span> we will be very busy<span class='line-break'> </span> tomorrow but we are that<span class='line-break'> </span> a most every day.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-981">
<h3><a name="page-981">Saturday, August 16, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good morning.  <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>Rain</a> tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> and <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7331' title='suckering'>suckered tobacco</a> all day except<span class='line-break'> </span> what time they worked over<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a> <a href='../subjects/133' title='horses'>horse</a>.  We hope he is<span class='line-break'> </span> some better tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I have bin very<span class='line-break'> </span> busy all day.  Josie made<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/251' title='preserves'>preserves</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7373' title='jelly'>jellie</a> of the <a href='../subjects/7387' title='damsons'>damsons</a><span class='line-break'> </span> that she got from <a href='../subjects/7240' title='Jim Power'>Powers</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> We made a pie of part of <span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/7314' title='peaches'>peaches</a> that she got yesterday<span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7371' title='canning'>caned</a> the rest of them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/51' title='Jack Harvey'>Jack Harvey</a> come over<span class='line-break'> </span> here a while to day.  While he<span class='line-break'> </span> was here <a href='../subjects/336' title='Alice Wooding'>Miss Alice Wooding</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7877' title='Annie Carter'>Miss Annie Carter</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come a few minutes.  We cut <span class='line-break'> </span> a fine <a href='../subjects/7324' title='watermelons'>water mellon</a> while they<span class='line-break'> </span> were here.  <a href='../subjects/7224' title='Julia Ferguson'>Julia Fergerson</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went back to <a href='../subjects/7216' title='Portsmouth, Virginia'>Portsmouth</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Julia did not come to see <span class='line-break'> </span> us while she was at home.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> and <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> went to the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7878' title='baptism'>baptizing</a> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-982">
<h3><a name="page-982">Sunday, August 17, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> went to look at a home in<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7879' title='Campbell County, Virginia'>Cambell county</a>.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a> with<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a>.  <a href='../subjects/153' title='Ren Worsham'>Ren Worshams</a> family<span class='line-break'> </span> was at <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  There was<span class='line-break'> </span> twenty three children at Marvins,<span class='line-break'> </span> all grand children except two.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> We all went to Marvins <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> All of us at home to night<span class='line-break'> </span> and all reasonable well.  For<span class='line-break'> </span> that I want to be thankful.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Marvin &amp; <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> has gone to<span class='line-break'> </span> Strait Stone to nigh to <a href='../subjects/7228' title='preaching'>preaching</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Rees</a> is takeing care of the<span class='line-break'> </span> little children.  <a href='../subjects/75' title='William Gilbert'>William Gilbert</a><span class='line-break'> </span> is at the <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a> close to the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7609' title='house'>house</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-983">
<h3><a name="page-983">Monday, August 18, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>Rain</a> at night.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> <a href='../subjects/7331' title='suckering'>suckered</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> until twelve oclock<span class='line-break'> </span> then Ben went to <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and got <a href='../subjects/7371' title='canning'>fruit jars and tops<span class='line-break'> </span> and rubbers</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Jim and Ben <a href='../subjects/7547' title='hauling wood'>hauled</a> a <span class='line-break'> </span> lot of olde boards to the <span class='line-break'> </span> wood pile.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I worked on <a href='../subjects/7368' title='grapes'>grapes</a><span class='line-break'> </span> most of the day.  This evening <span class='line-break'> </span> I picked a few dried<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/304' title='beans'>beans</a> and got some <a href='../subjects/7264' title='sweet potatoes'>sweet<span class='line-break'> </span> potatoes</a>, the first that we <span class='line-break'> </span> have had of this years<span class='line-break'> </span> crop.  Josie gathered some<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7277' title='green beans'>snaps</a> &amp; strung them and<span class='line-break'> </span> got <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>Irish potatoes</a> for <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>,<span class='line-break'> </span> tomorrows dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/202' title='Prince'>Prince</a> is much better than<span class='line-break'> </span> he was yesterday.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-984">
<h3><a name="page-984">Tuesday, August 19, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> saved [?] tobacco leaves.  <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul<span class='line-break'> </span> Bennett</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/75' title='William Gilbert'>William Gilbert</a><span class='line-break'> </span> helped and <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Rees Smith</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> two of the <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> boys <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> all <a href='../subjects/7344' title='handing'>handed</a> leaves.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7840' title='Tup Walker'>Mr Tup Walker</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie</a> &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7349' title='Evelyn Brumfield'>Evylin Brumfield</a> come to<span class='line-break'> </span> day.  This evening <a href='../subjects/59' title='Charles Harvey'>Charles</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1630' title='Virginia Harvey'>Virginia Harvey</a> come.  I was <span class='line-break'> </span> very glad to see them and<span class='line-break'> </span> Charles indeed as he had<span class='line-break'> </span> bin a way so long.<span class='line-break'> </span> Glad he was lookin so well.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The men folks is at the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a> yet and little Henry<span class='line-break'> </span> is with them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-985">
<h3><a name="page-985">Wednesday, August 20, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7388' title='tobacco cutting'>cut</a> a <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>house</a> of <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> for Jim.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  She had<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7277' title='green beans'>snaps</a> and <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chicken</a>, <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>potatoes</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie</a> made some <a href='../subjects/251' title='preserves'>preserves</a><span class='line-break'> </span> of <a href='../subjects/7387' title='damsons'>damson</a> that <a href='../subjects/348' title='Mrs Edmonds'>Mrs Edmons</a><span class='line-break'> </span> gave her.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening <a href='../subjects/7881' title='Miss Tredway'>Miss Tredway</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7882' title='Miss Creasy'>Miss Creasy</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7883' title='Tucker'>Tucker</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come to see <a href='../subjects/7349' title='Evelyn Brumfield'>Evylin</a>.  Did <span class='line-break'> </span> not stay but a few <span class='line-break'> </span> minutes.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Nellie &amp; Josie gathered<span class='line-break'> </span> snaps and <a href='../subjects/250' title='tomatoes'>tomatoes</a> for<span class='line-break'> </span> tomorrows dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7654' title='Eva Smith'>Carries baby</a> is <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a>.  I do <span class='line-break'> </span> hope that she will soon be well.<span class='line-break'> </span> Tonight <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went to the<span class='line-break'> </span> barn by him self after<span class='line-break'> </span> dark.  <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> has a bad<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>colde</a> tonight.  Hope she may<span class='line-break'> </span> soon get over it.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got a basket of <a href='../subjects/7264' title='sweet potatoes'>sweet<span class='line-break'> </span> potatoes</a> for <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a>. Brought<span class='line-break'> </span> them home &amp; washed them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7783' title='clocks'>Clock</a> not runing.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-986">
<h3><a name="page-986">Thursday, August 21, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The men folks<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7400' title='moving tobacco'>moved</a> some <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7388' title='tobacco cutting'>cut</a><span class='line-break'> </span> some for <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr. Owen</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> will stay at the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a> tonight.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> is with<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim now.  <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> is bad off with<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>colde</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7654' title='Eva Smith'>Carries baby</a> is <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>not well</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> with a little<span class='line-break'> </span> help.  <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie</a> <a href='../subjects/7371' title='canning'>caned</a> some <a href='../subjects/250' title='tomatoes'>tomatoes</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  This evening she<span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/168' title='Dick Wooding'>Mr. Woodings</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> got some <a href='../subjects/7368' title='grapes'>grapes</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7884' title='Willie Wooding'>Miss Willie<span class='line-break'> </span> Wooding</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7877' title='Annie Carter'>Miss Annie Carter</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come with her home on a <a href='../subjects/268' title='buggy'>buggy</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George Blairs</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/64' title='Lottie Craddock'>Lottie Craddock</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7727' title='Edith Ardena Craddock'>her little baby</a><span class='line-break'> </span> is over there.  <a href='../subjects/7885' title='Alice Hubbard'>Miss Alice <span class='line-break'> </span> Hubbard</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7535' title='Ada Hutcherson'>Ada Hutcherson</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7886' title='Susie Hutcherson'>Susie Hutcherson</a> was<span class='line-break'> </span> there.  They had <a href='../subjects/7324' title='watermelons'>water mellons</a> &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7314' title='peaches'>peaches</a> and grapes.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-987">
<h3><a name="page-987">Friday, August 22, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr<span class='line-break'> </span> Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/7388' title='tobacco cutting'>cut tobacco</a> all<span class='line-break'> </span> day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> staid at the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a>.  Jim &amp; Ben and <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went to the barn tonight<span class='line-break'> </span> to stay all night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie</a> made some <a href='../subjects/7373' title='jelly'>jellie</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7349' title='Evelyn Brumfield'>Evylin</a> come from <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harveys</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  <a href='../subjects/51' title='Jack Harvey'>Jack</a> was here<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  wanted a <a href='../subjects/133' title='horses'>horse</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Could not get one as they <span class='line-break'> </span> were at work.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Two <a href='../subjects/294' title='peddler'>pedlars</a> came by here <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie &amp; Nellie went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7654' title='Eva Smith'>Carries baby</a> is <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>not well</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> has<span class='line-break'> </span> bad <a href='../subjects/297' title='colds'>colds</a>.  Hope they will<span class='line-break'> </span> be well soon.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10: oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-988">
<h3><a name="page-988">Saturday, August 23, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> staid a round the <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barns</a><span class='line-break'> </span> most of the day.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr. Owen</a> went to the <a href='../subjects/44' title='mill'>mill</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Did not get his grinding.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7208' title='Altavista, Virginia'>Altavista</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> He went after <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owens</a> sister.<span class='line-break'> </span> While he was there he bought<span class='line-break'> </span> a little sack of <a href='../subjects/7523' title='flour'>flour</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7371' title='canning'>caned</a> some <a href='../subjects/7398' title='apples'>apples</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7349' title='Evelyn Brumfield'>Evylin</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and I went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7206' title='White Falls, Virginia'>White Falls</a> <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fishing</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> carried us and <span class='line-break'> </span> come after us.<span class='line-break'> </span> He had a <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>blow out</a> as<span class='line-break'> </span> he went over there.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Marvin went to <a href='../subjects/7228' title='preaching'>preaching</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10: oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-989">
<h3><a name="page-989">Sunday, August 24, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The men <span class='line-break'> </span> staid at home all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr. Owen</a> was <a href='../subjects/7354' title='curing'>fireing tobacco</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> helped him some.<span class='line-break'> </span> They are at the <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a> now.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7349' title='Evelyn Brumfield'>Evylin</a> and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7887' title='Ned Walker'>Mr Ned Walkers</a> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> &amp; the<span class='line-break'> </span> little children and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul<span class='line-break'> </span> Bennett</a> come a wile.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Edna is <a href='../subjects/81' title='complaining'>complaining</a> of <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/375' title='headache'>head ache</a> tonight.  I hope<span class='line-break'> </span> she may soon be well a gain.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went to <a href='../subjects/153' title='Ren Worsham'>Ren Worshams</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/150' title='Dr. Anderson Owen'>Dr Owens</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Heard today that <a href='../subjects/7889' title='Ann Layne'>Ann Layne</a><span class='line-break'> </span> is very <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10:30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-990">
<h3><a name="page-990">Monday, August 25, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7400' title='moving tobacco'>moved some tobacco</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  She baked <a href='../subjects/170' title='pies'>pies</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7349' title='Evelyn Brumfield'>Evylin</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> and I went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7461' title='Worsham&apos;s pond'>Worshams pond</a>.  Josie fixed<span class='line-break'> </span> our dinner.  We went on a <a href='../subjects/268' title='buggy'>buggy</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and drove <a href='../subjects/7414' title='Jake'>Jake</a>, <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Bens</a> <a href='../subjects/133' title='horses'>horse</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie</a> <a href='../subjects/7371' title='canning'>caned</a> some <a href='../subjects/250' title='tomatoes'>tomatoes</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate</a> come to see<span class='line-break'> </span> us this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I am sorry that I was<span class='line-break'> </span> not at home.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Nellie dug some <a href='../subjects/7264' title='sweet potatoes'>sweet <span class='line-break'> </span> potatoes</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-991">
<h3><a name="page-991">Tuesday, August 26, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> carried<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7349' title='Evelyn Brumfield'>Evylin</a> to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  He got back home at<span class='line-break'> </span> 10:20 oclock.  They have <a href='../subjects/7388' title='tobacco cutting'>cut<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewed</a> today.  She <span class='line-break'> </span> two gowns then gathered <span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/7277' title='green beans'>snaps</a> for <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a><span class='line-break'> </span> tomorrow.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> finished <a href='../subjects/7388' title='tobacco cutting'>cutting<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco</a> today.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> sent<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> some papers to <a href='../subjects/7626' title='reading'>read</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> He now has one reading.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am going to put out<span class='line-break'> </span> the light as he will have<span class='line-break'> </span> to work tomorrow.  Will need <span class='line-break'> </span> all the sleep he can get.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got a <a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a> from<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7636' title='Elsie East'>Elsie East</a> this evening.  Was<span class='line-break'> </span> glad to hear from her.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9:30 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-992">
<h3><a name="page-992">Wednesday, August 27, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The men folks<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7388' title='tobacco cutting'>cut tobacco</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> brought our <a href='../subjects/7523' title='flour'>flour</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> from the <a href='../subjects/44' title='mill'>mill</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie Reynols</a> come a few<span class='line-break'> </span> minutes this morning.  <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johnson</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went to see <a href='../subjects/7563' title='Mr Layne'>Mr Layne</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this  morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> We all staid at home all <span class='line-break'> </span> day.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> cut out some<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7569' title='garments'>garments</a> to mak soon.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I gathered &amp; strung some<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7277' title='green beans'>snaps</a> for tomorrows dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/349' title='Minnie Owen'>Mrs Owen</a> come this evening<span class='line-break'> </span> for <a href='../subjects/7286' title='milk'>milk</a>.  She picked up<span class='line-break'> </span> a bucket of <a href='../subjects/7398' title='apples'>apples</a> for<span class='line-break'> </span> us.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9:15 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-993">
<h3><a name="page-993">Thursday, August 28, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The men<span class='line-break'> </span> folk worked on <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a><span class='line-break'> </span> most of the day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr. Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/265' title='hog killing'>killed</a> his <a href='../subjects/986' title='dog'>dog</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  Though he was <a href='../subjects/447' title='rabies'>mad</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I worked a little.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese Smith</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to Whitefalls.<span class='line-break'> </span> We drove <a href='../subjects/7414' title='Jake'>Jake</a>, <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Bens</a> <a href='../subjects/289' title='colt'>colte</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Wel I am so near a <span class='line-break'> </span> sleep that I cant write.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-994">
<h3><a name="page-994">Friday, August 29, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p><a href='../subjects/187' title='cloudy'>Cloudy</a> most of the day but no<span class='line-break'> </span> rain.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/7400' title='moving tobacco'>moved tobacco</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this morning and <a href='../subjects/7388' title='tobacco cutting'>cut</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> staid at the <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a>.  Is <span class='line-break'> </span> there now.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewed</a> most all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening <a href='../subjects/335' title='Margaret Brumfield'>Mag Brumfield</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/424' title='Doris Brumfield'>Doris</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7651' title='Janie Brumfield'>Janie</a> and <a href='../subjects/7890' title='Charles Francis Brumfield, Jr.'>little<span class='line-break'> </span> Charley</a> come to see us.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Rees Smith</a> carried his<span class='line-break'> </span> mother to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got a <a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a> from<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7349' title='Evelyn Brumfield'>Evylin</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am always glad to hear<span class='line-break'> </span> from any of the kindsfolks.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-995">
<h3><a name="page-995">Saturday, August 30, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p><a href='../subjects/187' title='cloudy'>Cloudy</a> but no rain to speak of.<span class='line-break'> </span> We need rain.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> staid at the <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a> all day<span class='line-break'> </span> and is there yet.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> and the boys<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7388' title='tobacco cutting'>cut tobacco</a>.  They finished <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owens</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and Jims.  They are at the barn <span class='line-break'> </span> now <a href='../subjects/7891' title='stringing leaves'>stringing leaves</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening I went and got<span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/7264' title='sweet potatoes'>sweet potatoes</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> washed them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a little<span class='line-break'> </span> while late this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> was makeing <a href='../subjects/212' title='Roy Smith'>Roy</a> a<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7892' title='blouses'>blouse</a>.  I brought it home<span class='line-break'> </span> with me and have finished<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/91' title='button holes'>button holes</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewed</a> on the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/33' title='buttons'>buttons</a>.  Marvin had finished <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7357' title='tying'>tieing</a> <a href='../subjects/73' title='Hattie Gilbert'>Hatties</a> tobacco &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> commenced on <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul Bennetts</a>.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-996">
<h3><a name="page-996">Sunday, August 31, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p><a href='../subjects/187' title='cloudy'>Cloudy</a> most of the day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> staid at home.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to see my<span class='line-break'> </span> brother <a href='../subjects/7440' title='Letcher Craddock'>Letcher</a>.  He is <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> They think he is a little better <span class='line-break'> </span> now.  I do hope that he may <span class='line-break'> </span> get well soon.  <a href='../subjects/7893' title='Ellen'>Ellen</a> had<span class='line-break'> </span> a good dinner.  I am sorry<span class='line-break'> </span> for her.  She is so young to <span class='line-break'> </span> have the care of the house.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/153' title='Ren Worsham'>Ren Worsham</a> carried me.  I<span class='line-break'> </span> thank him for that.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> There was a crowd at <a href='../subjects/7440' title='Letcher Craddock'>Letchers</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/7231' title='Ethel Worsham'>Ethel</a> and all<span class='line-break'> </span> the children was on the <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am a fraid that they got<span class='line-break'> </span> wet before they got home.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> They got in and did not <span class='line-break'> </span> get wet.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-997">
<h3><a name="page-997">Monday, September  1, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7400' title='moving tobacco'>moved tobacco</a> all the morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening they pulled<span class='line-break'> </span> leaves in <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Bens</a> tobacco.<span class='line-break'> </span> Tonight they will stay with <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owens</a> tobacco.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> has bin<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7393' title='firing'>at the barns</a> all day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewed</a> some this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  This evening she <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  Today is<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/325' title='Paul Smith'>Paul Smiths</a> birthday.  <span class='line-break'> </span> He is seven years olde.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening I went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George Blairs</a>.  <a href='../subjects/204' title='Isla Blair'>Isla</a> &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/205' title='Cordie Blair'>Cordie</a> was at home.  <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia</a><span class='line-break'> </span> was at <a href='../subjects/153' title='Ren Worsham'>Ren Worshams</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/416' title='Beatrice Owen'>Beatris</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7751' title='Gladys Owen'>Gladis Owen</a> was<span class='line-break'> </span> there.  The girls gave us<span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/7314' title='peaches'>peaches</a> &amp; mellons.<span class='line-break'> </span> They were as nice to us<span class='line-break'> </span> as they could be.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Marvin was <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripping</a> tobacco<span class='line-break'> </span> but it dried out so he quit.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben &amp; Marvin has gone to Strait<span class='line-break'> </span> Stone to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-998">
<h3><a name="page-998">Tuesday, September  2, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> staid<span class='line-break'> </span> at the barns to day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> and <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul Bennett</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/75' title='William Gilbert'>William Gilbert (col)</a> all<span class='line-break'> </span> worked on <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Bens</a> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> <a href='../subjects/7894' title='pulling leaves'>pulling</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and hangin leaves.  I <a href='../subjects/7344' title='handing'>handed<span class='line-break'> </span> leaves</a> all day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
