<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Put out some <a href='../subjects/7398' title='apples'>apples</a> <a href='../subjects/7399' title='drying fruit'>to<span class='line-break'> </span> dry</a>.  The <a href='../subjects/109' title='teachers'>school teachers</a><span class='line-break'> </span> want to know what to depend<span class='line-break'> </span> on and worrie Ben lots.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/51' title='Jack Harvey'>Jack Harvey</a> come this evening<span class='line-break'> </span> and got <a href='../subjects/7414' title='Jake'>Jake</a> and the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/268' title='buggy'>buggy</a>.  I hope he will <span class='line-break'> </span> take care of them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7503' title='Jim Emerson'>Jim Emerson</a> passed here<span class='line-break'> </span> to day with ladies on the <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We had <a href='../subjects/355' title='peas'>peas</a> for dinner <span class='line-break'> </span> today.  They come from <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Blairs</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-999">
<h3><a name="page-999">Wednesday, September  3, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> finished<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7357' title='tying'>tieing leaves</a> to day.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7344' title='handing'>handed</a> some this morning<span class='line-break'> </span> then got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/51' title='Jack Harvey'>Jack Harvey</a> brought the <a href='../subjects/133' title='horses'>horse</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/268' title='buggy'>buggy</a> home this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning and staid and<span class='line-break'> </span> handed leaves until they<span class='line-break'> </span> finished tieing.  He eat<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner with Ben.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> carried <a href='../subjects/307' title='Grace Brumfield'>Grace</a> &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/41' title='Beulah Brumfield'>Beulah Brumfield</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> I to <a href='../subjects/7895' title='Jesse Worsham&apos;s pond'>Jessie Worshams<span class='line-break'> </span> pond</a>.  We <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fished</a>.  I caughed<span class='line-break'> </span> one nice fish.<span class='line-break'> </span> We c[om?]<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9:25 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1000">
<h3><a name="page-1000">Thursday, September  4, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> is at the <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a>.  They ground<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7398' title='apples'>apples</a> to day to <a href='../subjects/7896' title='cider making'>make cider</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening Ben went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7342' title='Cedar Forest'>Cedar Forest</a> to see some<span class='line-break'> </span> parties a bout a <a href='../subjects/194' title='school house'>school<span class='line-break'> </span> house</a>.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> I went two.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> While we were gone <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate<span class='line-break'> </span> Harvey</a> come.  Also <a href='../subjects/7897' title='Janie Gravely'>Janie<span class='line-break'> </span> Gravely</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7898' title='Evelyn Edmonds'>Evylin Edmons</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I would of bin glad to see<span class='line-break'> </span> them.  <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie Reynolds</a> come<span class='line-break'> </span> a little while before I went<span class='line-break'> </span> a way from home.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I washed<span class='line-break'> </span> the dishes after dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I have just finished working<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/91' title='button holes'>button holes</a> in <a href='../subjects/212' title='Roy Smith'>Roy Smiths</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/90' title='pants'>pants</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9:30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1001">
<h3><a name="page-1001">Friday, September  5, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> is at <span class='line-break'> </span> on [sic] the tobacco.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> to drive the <a href='../subjects/133' title='horses'>horses</a> up this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning and <a href='../subjects/7415' title='Pomp'>Pomp</a> kicked <span class='line-break'> </span> him.  Did not hurt him <span class='line-break'> </span> very bad.  We are all so glad<span class='line-break'> </span> it is no worse.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7211' title='Cedar Forest, Virginia'>Cedar Forest</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this morning a bout the <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a><span class='line-break'> </span> work.  Mrs Car come with<span class='line-break'> </span> him home.  I am glad that<span class='line-break'> </span> she came to see <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening Henry &amp; <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and I went to <a href='../subjects/7206' title='White Falls, Virginia'>White Falls</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and I <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fished</a>.  The children <span class='line-break'> </span> played.  Jim cut some <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> &amp; the children<span class='line-break'> </span> come down here a while<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/51' title='Jack Harvey'>Jack Harvey</a><span class='line-break'> </span> eat <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a> here tonight<span class='line-break'> </span> and will stay at the <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10: oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1002">
<h3><a name="page-1002">Saturday, September  6, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> is at work<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7354' title='curing'>curing</a> his last <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a>.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> went home this evening.  Ben carried<span class='line-break'> </span> him to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I went <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fishing</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went with me.<span class='line-break'> </span> We come by <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>Georg Blairs</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Heard to day that <a href='../subjects/7440' title='Letcher Craddock'>Letcher</a><span class='line-break'> </span> is worse off.  I am so sorry.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We fi[sh?]<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Jim went home this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> [?] Thomson sent us 20<span class='line-break'> </span> pounds of sugar to day.  <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr<span class='line-break'> </span> Owen</a> went after <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Bens</a> paint.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I am so near a sleep that<span class='line-break'> </span> I <a href='../subjects/7371' title='canning'>can</a>t write like it should<span class='line-break'> </span> be done.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9: oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1003">
<h3><a name="page-1003">Sunday, September  7, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> with <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs. Car</a> home at <a href='../subjects/7240' title='Jim Power'>Mr <span class='line-break'> </span> Powers</a>.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went with <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Uncle Marvin</a> to <a href='../subjects/391' title='Sunday school'>Sunday<span class='line-break'> </span> school</a> at <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a> church.<span class='line-break'> </span> He come home and we eat <span class='line-break'> </span> our <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  Then Henry went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/325' title='Paul Smith'>Paul Smith</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and Henry Brumfield went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/335' title='Margaret Brumfield'>Mag Brumfields</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to the sweet<span class='line-break'> </span> potatoe patch and dug a<span class='line-break'> </span> basket full of <a href='../subjects/7264' title='sweet potatoes'>sweet potatoes</a> &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> washed them this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a> and gathered<span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/7277' title='green beans'>snaps</a> &amp; strung them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to Marvins a while <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/67' title='Willie Mayhew'>Willie Mayhew</a><span class='line-break'> </span> was here this morning to<span class='line-break'> </span> look at <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Bens</a> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1004">
<h3><a name="page-1004">Monday, September  8, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> to meet <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> at <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  All the children<span class='line-break'> </span> went with him.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> To night <a href='../subjects/228' title='Clifton Reynolds'>Clifton</a> and <a href='../subjects/7333' title='Jane Reynolds'>Jane</a> and <a href='../subjects/406' title='Bruce Reynolds'>Bruce</a> &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Molie Reynols</a> was here to <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I was glad to have them.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/51' title='Jack Harvey'>Jack Harvey</a> commenced to <a href='../subjects/7899' title='painting'>paint</a><span class='line-break'> </span> the house top.  Quit and went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7900' title='Mr Moses'>Mr Moses</a>.  He had <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Bens</a> <a href='../subjects/133' title='horses'>horse</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/268' title='buggy'>buggy</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  She made a <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/240' title='cake'>cake</a>.  I killed two <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chickens</a><span class='line-break'> </span> for supper.  I washed two<span class='line-break'> </span> pair of <a href='../subjects/7902' title='blankets'>blankets</a> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Heard to night that <a href='../subjects/7440' title='Letcher Craddock'>my<span class='line-break'> </span> brother</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a><span class='line-break'> </span> Saturday and had some<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7545' title='dentistry'>teeth taken out</a>.  I do hope he<span class='line-break'> </span> may get well a gain.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Heard tonight that <a href='../subjects/7901' title='Hughes Walker'>Hughs<span class='line-break'> </span> Walker</a> <a href='../subjects/96' title='death'>died</a> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> I knew him when we were<span class='line-break'> </span> young.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 11 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1005">
<h3><a name="page-1005">Tuesday, September  9, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/51' title='Jack Harvey'>Jack Harvey</a> <a href='../subjects/7400' title='moving tobacco'>moved</a> some<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> this morning.  <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/120' title='falling'>fell</a> out of the <a href='../subjects/115' title='wagon'>waggon</a> in<span class='line-break'> </span> the wheel and got hurt right<span class='line-break'> </span> bad.  This evening Jim went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7206' title='White Falls, Virginia'>White Falls</a> to the <a href='../subjects/44' title='mill'>mill</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben &amp; Jack finished painting the <span class='line-break'> </span> roof of the <a href='../subjects/7609' title='house'>house</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed a good washing <span class='line-break'> </span> for her to do.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> and all the children<span class='line-break'> </span> but <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> come down here.<span class='line-break'> </span> I killed &amp; dressed a <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chicken</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and dug some <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>potatoes</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and went to the <a href='../subjects/7246' title='orchard'>orchard</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and got a basket of <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7398' title='apples'>apples</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I am counting on<span class='line-break'> </span> going <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fishing</a> in the  morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1006">
<h3><a name="page-1006">Wednesday, September 10, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day and very <a href='../subjects/159' title='warm'>warm</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/51' title='Jack Harvey'>Jack</a> painted the <a href='../subjects/7903' title='stable'>stable</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7904' title='buggy house'>buggy house</a> tops.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> to the <a href='../subjects/44' title='mill'>mill</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went with <a href='../subjects/67' title='Willie Mayhew'>Mr Willie<span class='line-break'> </span> Mayhew</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/8093' title='Melissa Mayhew'>wife</a> to <a href='../subjects/7203' title='Long Island, Virginia'>Long Island</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> We all <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fished</a> some.  We did<span class='line-break'> </span> not <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>catch any</a> thing.  I am so<span class='line-break'> </span> thankful that they would be<span class='line-break'> </span> troubled with me.  I eat dinner<span class='line-break'> </span> with them.  The whole trip did not<span class='line-break'> </span> cost me a penny.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7905' title='Jim Eades'>Jim Eades</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> got <a href='../subjects/7489' title='seed wheat'>seed wheat</a>.  He brought some<span class='line-break'> </span> for Ben.  Marvin went to Long<span class='line-break'> </span> Island and got a bed stead<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1007">
<h3><a name="page-1007">Thursday, September 11, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A little <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> but no<span class='line-break'> </span> rain to do any good.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> carried <a href='../subjects/1630' title='Virginia Harvey'>Virginia Harvey</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a> on her way to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/7357' title='tying'>tied tobacco</a> all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a> is working on tobacco<span class='line-break'> </span> two.  <a href='../subjects/51' title='Jack Harvey'>Jack Harvey</a> painted most<span class='line-break'> </span> all day.  Ben &amp; <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> helped <span class='line-break'> </span> some this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Two life <a href='../subjects/7906' title='insurance agents'>insurance agents</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come here to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got most of the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I baked a <a href='../subjects/170' title='pies'>peach<span class='line-break'> </span> pie</a> this evening.  I made some<span class='line-break'> </span> apple <a href='../subjects/7373' title='jelly'>jellie</a>.  Went to the <a href='../subjects/7246' title='orchard'>orchard</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and got a basket of <a href='../subjects/7398' title='apples'>apples</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a few<span class='line-break'> </span> minutes.  Come home and dressed<span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chicken</a> and <a href='../subjects/15' title='milking'>milked</a> the <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cows</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The men folks has gone a <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7907' title='possum hunting'>opossome hunting</a> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Jack Harvey went from here<span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9:30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>

<div id="page-1008">
<h3><a name="page-1008">Friday, September 12, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> carried<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> and I to <a href='../subjects/7461' title='Worsham&apos;s pond'>Worshams<span class='line-break'> </span> pond</a>.  We did not <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>catch anything</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> helped <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> fix up his<span class='line-break'> </span> shelter this evening.  Marvin <span class='line-break'> </span> come after us.  Met us at <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7909' title='Mrs Stork'>Mrs Storks</a>.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> &amp; the girls<span class='line-break'> </span> was with him.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben <a href='../subjects/7899' title='painting'>painted</a> at <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owens</a> this evening.  Come<span class='line-break'> </span> home &amp; washed and set down. <span class='line-break'> </span> His chair sliped and he <a href='../subjects/120' title='falling'>fell</a> &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> hurt him self right bad.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate</a> was here this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I did not see her.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>

<div id="page-1009">
<h3><a name="page-1009">Saturday, September 13, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/7899' title='painting'>painted</a> at <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/181' title='tenant house'>Owens house</a> to day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped tobacco</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening I went to <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George<span class='line-break'> </span> Blairs</a>.  Went by <a href='../subjects/7675' title='Charlie Hutcherson'>Charley<span class='line-break'> </span> Hutchersons</a> and bought<span class='line-break'> </span> a busel of <a href='../subjects/259' title='meal'>meal</a>.  <a href='../subjects/52' title='Irvin Harvey'>Irvin<span class='line-break'> </span> Harvey</a> brough it home for<span class='line-break'> </span> me.  I stopped at <a href='../subjects/7550' title='Jesse Hutcherson'>Jessie<span class='line-break'> </span> Hutchersons</a> a few minutes.<span class='line-break'> </span> All the young folks from<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Blairs</a> was gone to a <a href='../subjects/7912' title='parties'>lawn<span class='line-break'> </span> partie</a> at <a href='../subjects/7756' title='Edge Hill, Virginia'>Edge Hill</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben has gone to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait<span class='line-break'> </span> Stone</a> to night to the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/85' title='lodge'>lodge</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>

<div id="page-1010">
<h3><a name="page-1010">Sunday, September 14, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to look<span class='line-break'> </span> for Sl[??].  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> went to the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> was <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got a <a href='../subjects/7570' title='snack'>snack</a> for <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie &amp; Ben all the children<span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7240' title='Jim Power'>Jim Powers</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> and all the<span class='line-break'> </span> children and I went to <a href='../subjects/7916' title='John Emerson'>John<span class='line-break'> </span> Emersons</a> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/7672' title='Sarah Emerson'>Sarah</a> &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> the children was at home.<span class='line-break'> </span> They went for John.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7917' title='Mr &amp; Mrs ?asor'>Mr &amp; Mrs ?asor</a> come there.<span class='line-break'> </span> I was glad to see them.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am glad that John &amp; Sarah<span class='line-break'> </span> are doing as well as it seems<span class='line-break'> </span> that they are.  The children<span class='line-break'> </span> all seem to be nice &amp; polite.<span class='line-break'> </span> I certainly do wish them<span class='line-break'> </span> all well.  <a href='../subjects/7921' title='Fannie Emerson'>Fanny</a> is at <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9:10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1011">
<h3><a name="page-1011">Monday, September 15, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco</a>.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> worked on <a href='../subjects/419' title='Travis Dews'>Dews's</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a> this morning.  This evening<span class='line-break'> </span> he <a href='../subjects/7899' title='painting'>painted</a> on the <a href='../subjects/7918' title='cow shed'>cow shed</a> &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7919' title='hen house'>hen house</a> roofs.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7205' title='Effie Thornton Brumfield'>Effie</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/41' title='Beulah Brumfield'>Beaula Brumfield</a> come<span class='line-break'> </span> to see a bout getting <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>schools</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to <a href='../subjects/7461' title='Worsham&apos;s pond'>Worshams pond</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/204' title='Isla Blair'>Isla Blair</a> went with me.<span class='line-break'> </span> We did not <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>catch any</a> <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> We drove <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Bens</a> hores.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul Bennett</a> went from<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/195' title='Henry Blair'>Henry Blair</a> carried him<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1012">
<h3><a name="page-1012">Tuesday, September 16, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7469' title='cutting corn'>cut corn</a> all day.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> &amp; I peeled<span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/7314' title='peaches'>peaches</a> and made <a href='../subjects/251' title='preserves'>preserves</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> We had <a href='../subjects/7277' title='green beans'>snaps</a> for <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>, the last<span class='line-break'> </span> that we will get this year without<span class='line-break'> </span> it rains very soon.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewed</a> some this evening<span class='line-break'> </span> and gathered some <a href='../subjects/355' title='peas'>peas</a>.  We have<span class='line-break'> </span> finished shelling them tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went and dug some <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>potatoes</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; washed them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7365' title='John Baily'>Mr John Baily</a> and <a href='../subjects/7590' title='Miss Angle'>Miss Angle</a><span class='line-break'> </span> was here this evening.  They were<span class='line-break'> </span> going a round a bout the <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>schools</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> They did not see Ben.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> got my book &amp; <a href='../subjects/7920' title='pen'>pen</a> and <a href='../subjects/436' title='ink'>ink</a><span class='line-break'> </span> for me tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9:15 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1013">
<h3><a name="page-1013">Wednesday, September 17, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> finished <a href='../subjects/7469' title='cutting corn'>cutting corn</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> made <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> a <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> made some <a href='../subjects/7396' title='pickling'>pickel</a> of <a href='../subjects/7457' title='pears'>pears</a> that<span class='line-break'> </span> she brought from her mothers<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7246' title='orchard'>orchard</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> went to the <a href='../subjects/7552' title='saw mill'>saw mill</a><span class='line-break'> </span> twice today.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> washed<span class='line-break'> </span> some and <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a>. <a href='../subjects/75' title='William Gilbert'>William</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/73' title='Hattie Gilbert'>Hattie Gilbert</a> (col) picked<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/355' title='peas'>peas</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I <a href='../subjects/79' title='letter writing'>wrote</a> <a href='../subjects/7921' title='Fannie Emerson'>Fannie Emerson</a><span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a> today.  I went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Edna and <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> with me.  We came by the<span class='line-break'> </span> orchard and picked up<span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/7398' title='apples'>apples</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8:45 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1014">
<h3><a name="page-1014">Thursday, September 18, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a><span class='line-break'> </span> put <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> in the <a href='../subjects/232' title='pit'>pit</a> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening they covered the <a href='../subjects/7227' title='pigpen'>hog<span class='line-break'> </span> pen</a>.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went to <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning and to <a href='../subjects/7675' title='Charlie Hutcherson'>Charley Hutcherson</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  He paid for some<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/259' title='meal'>meal</a> that I bought and carried<span class='line-break'> </span> the sack home.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I got the <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie made <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> a pink <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> She is very glad of it.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/416' title='Beatrice Owen'>Beatrice Owen</a> come this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/325' title='Paul Smith'>Paul</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/212' title='Roy Smith'>Roy</a> and <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Rees</a> was<span class='line-break'> </span> here a little while to day.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/349' title='Minnie Owen'>Mrs. Owen</a> put in a <a href='../subjects/8' title='quilting'>quilt</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  She had <a href='../subjects/401' title='Virginia Dews'>Mrs Dews</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8' title='quilting'>quilting</a> frames.  I cant find<span class='line-break'> </span> two of mine.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9:30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1015">
<h3><a name="page-1015">Friday, September 19, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The men folks<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped tobacco</a> most of the<span class='line-break'> </span> day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to see<span class='line-break'> </span> some of the <a href='../subjects/109' title='teachers'>teachers</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> &amp; I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7922' title='Sam C?llens'>Old man Sam C[a?]llens</a><span class='line-break'> </span> was <a href='../subjects/118' title='burial'>buried</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> We have knowed him ever<span class='line-break'> </span> since we lived in this neighborhood.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> &amp; family went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> They had the childrens<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7266' title='photography'>pictures</a> made.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Heard that <a href='../subjects/7440' title='Letcher Craddock'>my brother</a> is<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/164' title='improving'>improving</a>.  Hope he may get <span class='line-break'> </span> well a gain.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/336' title='Alice Wooding'>Miss Alice Wooding</a> sent me<span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/363' title='seeds'>seed</a> <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a> by Ben this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  Hope I may live and<span class='line-break'> </span> be able to plant it.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9:10 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1016">
<h3><a name="page-1016">Saturday, September 20, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7923' title='hauling corn'>hauled up a little corn</a>.  Jim hauled<span class='line-break'> </span> some rails and made his <a href='../subjects/7227' title='pigpen'>hog pen</a><span class='line-break'> </span> larger, then they <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco</a>.  <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr. Owen</a> finished a <a href='../subjects/7354' title='curing'>cureing</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I commenced to<span class='line-break'> </span> wash.  Josie got <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a> and had<span class='line-break'> </span> to quit.  I finished.  They<span class='line-break'> </span> got dry.  Josie <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> some<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johnson Reynolds</a> passed<span class='line-break'> </span> here this evening at work<span class='line-break'> </span> on the <a href='../subjects/158' title='telephones'>phone</a> line.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1017">
<h3><a name="page-1017">Sunday, September 21, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  We all staid <span class='line-break'> </span> at home until after <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>,<span class='line-break'> </span> then <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> went sloes<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7631' title='hunting'>hunting</a>.  I went to <a href='../subjects/7924' title='Mr Edmonds'>Mr<span class='line-break'> </span> Edmons's</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7925' title='Mr. &amp; Mrs. Peak'>Mr. &amp; Mrs. Peak</a><span class='line-break'> </span> was there.  <a href='../subjects/336' title='Alice Wooding'>Miss Alice</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7884' title='Willie Wooding'>Miss Willie Wooding</a> come<span class='line-break'> </span> over there.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> They had plenty of <a href='../subjects/7368' title='grapes'>grapes</a><span class='line-break'> </span> at Edmons's.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> and <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> to see <a href='../subjects/7926' title='Dr Wiggonton'>Dr Wiggonton</a> &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/360' title='Pearl Harvey'>Pearl</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Rees</a> &amp; Smith &amp; [?] and<span class='line-break'> </span> Emet Brumfield come here<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/391' title='Sunday School'>Sunday School</a> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin carried them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim Brumfield</a> went with<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese Smith</a> home tonight<span class='line-break'> </span> to stay a little while.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1018">
<h3><a name="page-1018">Monday, September 22, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>Rain</a> tonight.  It is<span class='line-break'> </span> badly needed.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco</a> all day and they are at the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a> tonight <a href='../subjects/7357' title='tying'>tieing tobacco</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr. Owen</a> went to the island for<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/154' title='guano'>guano</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> eat dinner with us.<span class='line-break'> </span> I was glad to have her with us.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie walked with her as far as<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a> to day, the first day <span class='line-break'> </span> of this term.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/104' title='Tom Edmonds'>Tom Edmons</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7927' title='South Boston, Virginia'>South<span class='line-break'> </span> Boston</a> <a href='../subjects/128' title='tobacco sale'>with tobacco</a> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got a <a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a> from <a href='../subjects/7921' title='Fannie Emerson'>Fannie<span class='line-break'> </span> Emerson</a>.  Was glad to get it.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am always glad to hear from<span class='line-break'> </span> any of the folks that is a<span class='line-break'> </span> way from home.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8:30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1019">
<h3><a name="page-1019">Tuesday, September 23, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p><a href='../subjects/187' title='cloudy'>Cloudy</a> most of the day<span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>some rain</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped tobacco</a><span class='line-break'> </span> the most of the day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr. Owen</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7203' title='Long Island, Virginia'>the island</a><span class='line-break'> </span> for <a href='../subjects/154' title='guano'>guano</a>.  <a href='../subjects/75' title='William Gilbert'>William Gilbert</a> (col)<span class='line-break'> </span> went for <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harveys</a> guano<span class='line-break'> </span> with <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin Smiths</a> <a href='../subjects/133' title='horses'>team</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim B</a> is helpin <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> with<span class='line-break'> </span> his lessons.  Ben has gone<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7907' title='possum hunting'>possum hunting</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> made <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> some<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7928' title='underpants'>under pants</a> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went this evening and<span class='line-break'> </span> got some <a href='../subjects/7264' title='sweet potatoes'>sweet potatoes</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and washed them ready <span class='line-break'> </span> to cook.  I <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> some this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  Josie got most of<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben found <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>Mr. Owens cow</a><span class='line-break'> </span> with a little <a href='../subjects/87' title='calves'>calf</a> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8:30 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1020">
<h3><a name="page-1020">Wednesday, September 24, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/279' title='beautiful'>beautiful</a> day.  The men<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped tobacco</a> until <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a><span class='line-break'> </span> then they loaded the <a href='../subjects/115' title='wagon'>waggon</a><span class='line-break'> </span> ready to start to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a> in<span class='line-break'> </span> the morning.  <a href='../subjects/68' title='John Hutcherson'>John Hutcherson</a><span class='line-break'> </span> loaded his <a href='../subjects/219' title='truck'>truck</a> for <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> They are going to <a href='../subjects/973' title='Danville, Virginia'>Danville</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got the dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.  I <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> some this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning and <a href='../subjects/182' title='mending'>mended</a> some<span class='line-break'> </span> things this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> ask me to wake him<span class='line-break'> </span> at three in the morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1021">
<h3><a name="page-1021">Thursday, September 25, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a> <a href='../subjects/128' title='tobacco sale'>with the tobacco</a><span class='line-break'> </span> today.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to Gretna<span class='line-break'> </span> with the <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a>.  He bough<span class='line-break'> </span> roofing for the <a href='../subjects/7929' title='hen houses'>hen houses</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> spent the day with <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lee Brumfield</a> and I went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7281' title='the river'>the river</a>.  Lee caught one<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a>.  I did not <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>catch any</a><span class='line-break'> </span> thing.  I was glad to go <span class='line-break'> </span> with him.  I bought 10 pounds of<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/10661' title='sugar'>sugar</a> from <a href='../subjects/7931' title='Oscar Booker'>Oscar Booker</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I stopped at <a href='../subjects/7932' title='Mr Dillard'>Mr Dillards</a><span class='line-break'> </span> while Lee &amp; Dillard gathered<span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/7933' title='chinquapins'>chinquapins</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> went to <a href='../subjects/973' title='Danville, Virginia'>Danville</a><span class='line-break'> </span> today.  <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> went with him.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1022">
<h3><a name="page-1022">Friday, September 26, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/279' title='beautiful'>beautiful</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> is in<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a>.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> worked on <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a> most of the day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The children went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I washed some.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening Josie and I<span class='line-break'> </span> went to Marvins a while.<span class='line-break'> </span> Come home.  Josie g[ot] <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I <a href='../subjects/15' title='milking'>milked</a>.  The children<span class='line-break'> </span> got <a href='../subjects/36' title='wood'>wood</a> and <a href='../subjects/123' title='water'>water</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben has gone <a href='../subjects/7631' title='hunting'>hunting</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to night.  I <a href='../subjects/182' title='mending'>mended</a> <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1023">
<h3><a name="page-1023">Saturday, September 27, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> worked <span class='line-break'> </span> on his <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a> most of the day.<span class='line-break'> </span> I <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> some &amp; got a <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7570' title='snack'>snack</a> for <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> was <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Just at night to day<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/230' title='Lizzie Bennett'>Lizzie Bennett</a> and <a href='../subjects/7352' title='Faber Jefferson'>Faber</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/428' title='Ola Bennett Jefferson'>Ola Jefferson</a> come.<span class='line-break'> </span> They had bin to a <a href='../subjects/7934' title='picnic'>picknick</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> at <a href='../subjects/7259' title='Whittles Depot, Virginia'>Whittles</a>.  They brought<span class='line-break'> </span> enough things already<span class='line-break'> </span> cooked for our <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and even some of the things<span class='line-break'> </span> was for <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I made my supper of what <span class='line-break'> </span> they brought and did enjoy<span class='line-break'> </span> it.  Ben amd Faber went<span class='line-break'> </span> where they some one was<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7631' title='hunting'>hunting</a> but did not stay<span class='line-break'> </span> long.  I am so glad to<span class='line-break'> </span> hear that <a href='../subjects/7440' title='Letcher Craddock'>Brother Letcher</a> is<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/164' title='improving'>improving</a> some.  Hope he may <span class='line-break'> </span> get well a gain.  I am glad that<span class='line-break'> </span> Lizzie and the children come.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 11 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1024">
<h3><a name="page-1024">Sunday, September 28, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  We had company<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  <a href='../subjects/230' title='Lizzie Bennett'>Lizzie</a> and <a href='../subjects/428' title='Ola Bennett Jefferson'>Ola</a> &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7352' title='Faber Jefferson'>Faber</a> went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  I went<span class='line-break'> </span> with them.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> carried us.<span class='line-break'> </span> We went from there to <a href='../subjects/7408' title='Johnsons'>Johnsons</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> There we eat <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> and then<span class='line-break'> </span> we went to <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harveys</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We walked from Marvins to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Reynols</a> from there to Harveys.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin Smith</a> carried us from<span class='line-break'> </span> there to <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George Blairs</a> on his<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a>.  I walked from there home.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> There was <a href='../subjects/7228' title='preaching'>preaching</a> at <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  Some of the Odd Fellows<span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7213' title='Lynchburg, Virginia'>Lynch Burg</a> this morning<span class='line-break'> </span> and brought 19 girls from the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7935' title='Odd Fellows Home'>Odd Fellows Home</a> to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to preaching.  There was dinner on<span class='line-break'> </span> the ground.  Enough to <a href='../subjects/174' title='feed'>feed</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> them and some others.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went to <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lee Brumfields</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and went <a href='../subjects/7937' title='hazelnuts'>hazel nut hunting</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/349' title='Minnie Owen'>Mrs. Owen</a> got home from <a href='../subjects/7800' title='Roanoke, Virginia'>Roanoak</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8:45 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1025">
<h3><a name="page-1025">Monday, September 29, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/7547' title='hauling wood'>hauled</a><span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/36' title='wood'>wood</a> late in the evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> He went to <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a>.  He let all<span class='line-break'> </span> the children go with him.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie commenced her a <a href='../subjects/8' title='quilting'>quilt</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> for <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklins</a> bed.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> went to meet <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> at <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a>.  Jim got home<span class='line-break'> </span> a bout sundown.  I was glad <span class='line-break'> </span> to have him back.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a> today.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> gathered some <a href='../subjects/355' title='peas'>peas</a> for dinner<span class='line-break'> </span> tomorrows.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1026">
<h3><a name="page-1026">Tuesday, September 30, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> helped<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> on his <a href='../subjects/7903' title='stable'>stable</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The children went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I washed some.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> come a little while<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  She brought<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7654' title='Eva Smith'>Eva</a> with her.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> staid at <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a><span class='line-break'> </span> most of the day<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9:10 oclock</p>
</div>
