<br />
<div id="page-1027">
<h3><a name="page-1027">Wednesday, October  1, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> worked on <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a>'s <a href='../subjects/7903' title='stable'>stable</a><span class='line-break'> </span> all day.  Ben lost some<span class='line-break'> </span> time. <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> has been <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a><span class='line-break'> </span> all day.  She <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>has a little <span class='line-break'> </span> girl</a> born at 8 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.  <a href='../subjects/150' title='Dr. Anderson Owen'>Dr Owen</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> from here to <a href='../subjects/7938' title='Irvin Bennett'>Irvin Bennetts</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> The children all staid<span class='line-break'> </span> at <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I have done what work<span class='line-break'> </span> has bin done here to day.<span class='line-break'> </span> There is a light in<span class='line-break'> </span> the north tonight.  Dont<span class='line-break'> </span> know what caused it.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7939' title='fair'>The fair</a> is going on at <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7213' title='Lynchburg, Virginia'>Lynchburg</a><span class='line-break'> </span> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1028">
<h3><a name="page-1028">Thursday, October  2, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went for<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Car</a>.  She was in <a href='../subjects/7213' title='Lynchburg, Virginia'>Lynchburg</a><span class='line-break'> </span> then he went several places<span class='line-break'> </span> trying to find some one to help<span class='line-break'> </span> him with the work.  He could not<span class='line-break'> </span> find any one that would come.<span class='line-break'> </span>  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped tobacco</a> until <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a><span class='line-break'> </span> then he went to the <a href='../subjects/44' title='mill'>mill</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> He got home after dark<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> staid at <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> most<span class='line-break'> </span> of the day<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/73' title='Hattie Gilbert'>Hattie</a> worked some for <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening     <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9:00 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1029">
<h3><a name="page-1029">Friday, October  3, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day &amp; very<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/159' title='warm'>warm</a>  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> hauled <a href='../subjects/7940' title='rock'>a load<span class='line-break'> </span> of rock</a> this morning and<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> loaded up the olde <a href='../subjects/232' title='pit'>pit</a><span class='line-break'> </span> Ben went after <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Carr</a><span class='line-break'> </span> I was so glad for her to<span class='line-break'> </span> come  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate</a> came<span class='line-break'> </span> down a little while  this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening  <a href='../subjects/349' title='Minnie Owen'>Mrs Owen</a> came<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I had a <a href='../subjects/120' title='falling'>fall</a> tonight<span class='line-break'> </span> I had a bucket of <a href='../subjects/355' title='peas'>peas</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and a lighted lamp in<span class='line-break'> </span> my hands  The Lamp did<span class='line-break'> </span> not break or the chimney<span class='line-break'> </span> it hurt me a little<span class='line-break'> </span> I am glad it was no <span class='line-break'> </span> worse   9 o'clock<span class='line-break'> </span>  </p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1030">
<h3><a name="page-1030">Saturday, October  4, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>Partly <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> and a few drops <span class='line-break'> </span> of <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a> today <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> worked on the olde <a href='../subjects/232' title='pit'>pit</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/336' title='Alice Wooding'>Miss Alice Wooding</a> came<span class='line-break'> </span> to see <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a><span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> bathed <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> this evening<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> a few<span class='line-break'> </span> minutes this evening<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7208' title='Altavista, Virginia'>Altavista</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening he bought <span class='line-break'> </span> me some loaf <a href='../subjects/390' title='bread'>bread</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7433' title='cheese'>chees</a><span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9:10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1031">
<h3><a name="page-1031">Sunday, October  5, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day every body<span class='line-break'> </span> wishing it would rain that<span class='line-break'> </span> is every body that is olde <span class='line-break'> </span> enough to know how bad it<span class='line-break'> </span> is needed<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We all staid at home to<span class='line-break'> </span> day and no one came to see us<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> sent <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> a nice <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>  I cooked a <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chicken</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and squirrel <a href='../subjects/77' title='baking'>Baked</a> some<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>potatoe</a> <a href='../subjects/170' title='pies'>pies</a>  Would not <span class='line-break'> </span> write about what I done<span class='line-break'> </span> but have nothing else to<span class='line-break'> </span> write  every body is in<span class='line-break'> </span> bed but me and I will<span class='line-break'> </span> be prety soon if nothing <span class='line-break'> </span> happens              9 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1032">
<h3><a name="page-1032">Monday, October  6, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A fairly <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a>  We need <span class='line-break'> </span> rain so bad.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped tobacco</a> all<span class='line-break'> </span> day the children went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>  <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> staid at <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> most of the day<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia Blair</a> came to see us<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> came a<span class='line-break'> </span> few minutes this evening<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/150' title='Dr. Anderson Owen'>Dr Owen</a> called to see <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> this morning <span class='line-break'> </span> 8:30 clock<span class='line-break'> </span>          </p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1033">
<h3><a name="page-1033">Tuesday, October  7, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/279' title='beautiful'>beautiful</a> day.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped <span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco</a>.  <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> loaded some<span class='line-break'> </span> on <a href='../subjects/67' title='Willie Mayhew'>Mr Mayhews</a> <a href='../subjects/219' title='truck'>truck</a> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span> They are going to <a href='../subjects/446' title='South Boston'>South Boston</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie</a> and <a href='../subjects/7386' title='Christine Reynolds'>Christenia Reynolds</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come a little while to day.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/349' title='Minnie Owen'>Mrs Owen</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/401' title='Virginia Dews'>Mrs Dews</a> come<span class='line-break'> </span> a few minutes this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Car</a> washed dishes<span class='line-break'> </span> for me today and that was<span class='line-break'> </span> a big help.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I washed <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>the babys</a> flanels<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Jim &amp; Ben went to the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a> to nigh to tie tobacco.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I have <a href='../subjects/79' title='letter writing'>wrote a letter</a> to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7440' title='Letcher Craddock'>Letcher Craddock</a> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9:5 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1034">
<h3><a name="page-1034">Wednesday, October  8, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p><a href='../subjects/187' title='cloudy'>Cloudy</a> most of the day but no <span class='line-break'> </span> rain yet.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco</a> all day.  Ben went to the<span class='line-break'> </span> store just at night.  <a href='../subjects/59' title='Charles Harvey'>Charles <span class='line-break'> </span> Harvey</a> come and staid a while.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> solde his <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate</a> come this evening a few<span class='line-break'> </span> minutes.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> come and brought<span class='line-break'> </span> me some <a href='../subjects/355' title='peas'>peas</a>.  I <a href='../subjects/7355' title='shelling'>shelled</a> them<span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.  <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr. Owen</a> did not come <span class='line-break'> </span> home from <a href='../subjects/7927' title='South Boston, Virginia'>Boston</a> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lee Brumfield</a> went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/973' title='Danville, Virginia'>Danville</a> to day.  <a href='../subjects/7652' title='Effie Brumfield Cundiff'>Effie</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/41' title='Beulah Brumfield'>Beaulah</a><span class='line-break'> </span> commenced teaching <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9: oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1035">
<h3><a name="page-1035">Thursday, October  9, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day.  No rain to <span class='line-break'> </span> do any good.  The men worked on<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a>.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7945' title='Mr Bailis'>Mr Bailis</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  <a href='../subjects/7942' title='Jim Moon'>Jim Moon</a> carried<span class='line-break'> </span> him.  They went to see a bout<span class='line-break'> </span> getting a <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.  Also went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a> to see <a href='../subjects/128' title='tobacco sale'>tobacco<span class='line-break'> </span> solde</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a little<span class='line-break'> </span> while this evening.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> was<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/182' title='mending'>mending</a> overalls.  She was <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/81' title='complaining'>complaining</a> of <a href='../subjects/7629' title='rheumatism'>rheumatism</a><span class='line-break'> </span> in her knee.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Rees</a> brought me 10 <a href='../subjects/249' title='eggs'>eggs</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> staid at Marvins<span class='line-break'> </span> all day.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went <span class='line-break'> </span> to school.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben &amp; Jim went to the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a> to night and have not <span class='line-break'> </span> come back yet.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9:15 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1036">
<h3><a name="page-1036">Friday, October 10, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The men folks worked<span class='line-break'> </span> on <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a>.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and got some <a href='../subjects/7574' title='beef'>beef</a>.  He paid 25 cts<span class='line-break'> </span> a pound for it.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/349' title='Minnie Owen'>Mrs Owen</a> is <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The children went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a><span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> staid all day at <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I think I am getting on well<span class='line-break'> </span> with the work considering my age<span class='line-break'> </span> but I am so tired of staying<span class='line-break'> </span> here and being so confined<span class='line-break'> </span> but I cant help my self.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> To day is <a href='../subjects/209' title='John Brumfield'>John Brumfields</a><span class='line-break'> </span> birth day.  I had a <a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a> from<span class='line-break'> </span> him yesterday.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1037">
<h3><a name="page-1037">Saturday, October 11, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The men <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco</a> all day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7943' title='Mamie Hutcherson'>Mrs Mamie Hutcherson</a> come<span class='line-break'> </span> to see <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went with <a href='../subjects/63' title='Robert Reynolds'>Robert</a> &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7386' title='Christine Reynolds'>Christenia Reynolds</a> to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7203' title='Long Island, Virginia'>Long Island</a> to meet <a href='../subjects/7771' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield (b 1878)'>Henry<span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield</a>.  He is on a visit <span class='line-break'> </span> from <a href='../subjects/7218' title='Norfolk, Virginia'>Norfolk</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I stopped at <a href='../subjects/7944' title='Mr Thomsons store'>Mr Thomsons<span class='line-break'> </span> store</a> and bought a few<span class='line-break'> </span> things.  Robert brought me<span class='line-break'> </span> home.  I saw <a href='../subjects/195' title='Henry Blair'>Henry Blair</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> at <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a>.  He is lookin<span class='line-break'> </span> well.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> have gone to Strait Stone<span class='line-break'> </span> to night.  It is <a href='../subjects/85' title='lodge'>lodge</a> night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1038">
<h3><a name="page-1038">Sunday, October 12, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day and rain tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> It is badly needed.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We all staid at home all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lee</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/307' title='Grace Brumfield'>Grace Brumfield</a> come and<span class='line-break'> </span> spent the day with us.<span class='line-break'> </span> I was glad to have them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> caught a <a href='../subjects/7312' title='rabbits'>rabbit</a> in<span class='line-break'> </span> his trap this morning and<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/7698' title='dogs'>dogs</a> caught one this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I have not seen any of <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> people today.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> is <a href='../subjects/79' title='letter writing'>going to write</a> to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/209' title='John Brumfield'>John</a> tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8:25 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1039">
<h3><a name="page-1039">Monday, October 13, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p><a href='../subjects/187' title='cloudy'>Cloudy</a> most of the day.  <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>Rain</a><span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.  The men folks worked on<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> all day.  I worked a round<span class='line-break'> </span> from one thing to another.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Late this evening I went<span class='line-break'> </span> to see <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a>.  She was some<span class='line-break'> </span> better of her <a href='../subjects/7629' title='rheumatism'>rheumatism</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I hope she may soon be well.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/416' title='Beatrice Owen'>Beatris Owen</a> come in a few<span class='line-break'> </span> minutes to see <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>the little baby</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a> to day.  <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a><span class='line-break'> </span> staid at home all day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> solde his <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cow</a> today<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/136' title='John Smith'>Mr John Smith</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The boys went to <a href='../subjects/7357' title='tying'>tie tobacco</a><span class='line-break'> </span> tonight and have not come<span class='line-break'> </span> home yet.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8:30 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1040">
<h3><a name="page-1040">Tuesday, October 14, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p><a href='../subjects/187' title='cloudy'>Cloudy</a> but no rain today.<span class='line-break'> </span> They are still on <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> To night <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> is at the <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a><span class='line-break'> </span> by him self.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7972' title='Lucius Gravely'>Lucius Gravely</a> has<span class='line-break'> </span> gone a <a href='../subjects/7631' title='hunting'>hunting</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/252' title='Mrs Hutcherson'>Mrs Hutcherson</a> come to see <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a>.  I was glad that she<span class='line-break'> </span> come.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7771' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield (b 1878)'>Henry Brumfield</a> come to see<span class='line-break'> </span> us today.  He eat <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> with<span class='line-break'> </span> us.  I was glad that he come.<span class='line-break'> </span> He said that he would start <span class='line-break'> </span> home in the morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1041">
<h3><a name="page-1041">Wednesday, October 15, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> loaded their <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> on <a href='../subjects/67' title='Willie Mayhew'>Mr Mayhews</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/219' title='truck'>truck</a> ready for <a href='../subjects/973' title='Danville, Virginia'>Danville</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> come down to <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a <span class='line-break'> </span> little while this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7949' title='Mr McCray'>Mr McCray</a> come and was<span class='line-break'> </span> going to stay all night<span class='line-break'> </span> at Marvins.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/150' title='Dr. Anderson Owen'>Dr Owen</a> examined Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  He is going <span class='line-break'> </span> to take <a href='../subjects/7950' title='insurance'>insurance</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We heard to day that<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/68' title='John Hutcherson'>John Hutcherson</a> is very <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> We are all sorry to hear <span class='line-break'> </span> it.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I woun a tangled hart<span class='line-break'> </span> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 11:45 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1042">
<h3><a name="page-1042">Thursday, October 16, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Ben carried<span class='line-break'> </span> Lady cow to Odie Kellies<span class='line-break'> </span> the went to Cedar Forest<span class='line-break'> </span> to see [?] Patrick.<span class='line-break'> </span> He let me go with him<span class='line-break'> </span> and fish.  I caught several<span class='line-break'> </span> cat fish.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Willie Mayhew brought our<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco to Gretna from Danville.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got supper tonight<span class='line-break'> </span> after dark.  The children<span class='line-break'> </span> had made a fire and brought<span class='line-break'> </span> water.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8:30 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1043">
<h3><a name="page-1043">Friday, October 17, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p><a href='../subjects/187' title='cloudy'>Cloudy</a> all day.  <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>Rain</a> tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a>.  Went on<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/419' title='Travis Dews'>Mr Dews</a> <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a>.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> was at Gretna.<span class='line-break'> </span> They <a href='../subjects/128' title='tobacco sale'>solde tobacco</a> there today.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> and the little children<span class='line-break'> </span> come down here and eat<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> with us.  I am glad<span class='line-break'> </span> that they come.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a><span class='line-break'> </span> childrens <a href='../subjects/7266' title='photography'>pictures</a> come today.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben went to <a href='../subjects/7951' title='Kellies'>Kellies</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> brought the <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cow</a> home today.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Carrie sent us some <a href='../subjects/7574' title='beef'>beef</a><span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I washed a little this morning<span class='line-break'> </span> and part of the clothes is <span class='line-break'> </span> on the line takeing the rain.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1044">
<h3><a name="page-1044">Saturday, October 18, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p><a href='../subjects/187' title='cloudy'>Cloudy</a> but no rain.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped Henrys<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco</a> today.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben carried the children and<span class='line-break'> </span> I to <a href='../subjects/7206' title='White Falls, Virginia'>White Falls</a> <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fishing</a>.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a><span class='line-break'> </span> caught five.  I caught 14.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Car</a> helped me <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a> them.<span class='line-break'> </span> I was glad of help.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We had <a href='../subjects/7574' title='beef'>beef</a> for <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> gave it to us.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7952' title='Henry Patrick'>Henry Patrick</a> come here today<span class='line-break'> </span> to see Mrs Car on business.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben and <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> has gone<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7631' title='hunting'>hunting</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1045">
<h3><a name="page-1045">Sunday, October 19, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Some <a href='../subjects/7544' title='frost'>frost</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  We all staid at<span class='line-break'> </span> home except the children. <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johnson Reynolds's</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Uncle<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvins</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7550' title='Jesse Hutcherson'>Mr Hutcherson</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7535' title='Ada Hutcherson'>Ada</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went to see <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> come to see us<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7607' title='Mr Power'>Mr</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7953' title='Mrs Power'>Mrs Power</a> come to see<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  Had <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chicken</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7954' title='salmon'>salmon</a>, <a href='../subjects/7396' title='pickling'>pickle</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/251' title='preserves'>preserves</a>,<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/250' title='tomatoes'>tomatoes</a> and <a href='../subjects/170' title='pies'>pies</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I should not write such<span class='line-break'> </span> small things but have nothing<span class='line-break'> </span> else to write.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1046">
<h3><a name="page-1046">Monday, October 20, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/279' title='beautiful'>beautiful</a> day.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and I went to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  We met <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a>.  <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come with him.  Ben <a href='../subjects/128' title='tobacco sale'>solde</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henrys</a> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a>.  Ben had to put<span class='line-break'> </span> on a new tire before he come<span class='line-break'> </span> home.  We saw a <a href='../subjects/219' title='truck'>truck</a> that<span class='line-break'> </span> had turned over.  No one was<span class='line-break'> </span> seriously hurt.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Car</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a><span class='line-break'> </span> while we were gone.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a<span class='line-break'> </span> few minutes this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie Reynolds</a> was there.<span class='line-break'> </span> I was glad to see her.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The chlidren went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1047">
<h3><a name="page-1047">Tuesday, October 21, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day.  No rain to<span class='line-break'> </span> do any good.  The men folks <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> some.  They say the land is so<span class='line-break'> </span> hard that they cant get it in<span class='line-break'> </span> order.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Two men come here<span class='line-break'> </span> trying to sell shares in a mine.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7955' title='Mr Haynes'>Mr Haynes</a> come to look<span class='line-break'> </span> at the <a href='../subjects/7319' title='cattle'>cattle</a>.  He bought two.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7956' title='Dr Womack'>Dr Womack</a> come to see the<span class='line-break'> </span> boys.  He is <a href='../subjects/7546' title='election'>seeking office</a><span class='line-break'> </span> so they did not get much done.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lees</a> and got a <span class='line-break'> </span> few <a href='../subjects/7398' title='apples'>apples</a>.  <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie</a> made light<span class='line-break'> </span> rolls for <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.  <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Car</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went home tonight.  <a href='../subjects/7601' title='Fletcher Carr'>Fletcher <span class='line-break'> </span> Car</a> come to see her this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a <span class='line-break'> </span> few minutes this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> was working on<span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/7957' title='coats'>pretty coat</a> for me.<span class='line-break'> </span> I hate to be a trouble<span class='line-break'> </span> to any one but cant help my<span class='line-break'> </span> self.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1048">
<h3><a name="page-1048">Wednesday, October 22, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day <a href='../subjects/159' title='warm'>warm</a> and good.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> worked on the <a href='../subjects/7263' title='wheat'>wheat</a><span class='line-break'> </span> land.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> has not bin well.  He had<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/66' title='toothache'>tooth ache</a> and his jaw is<span class='line-break'> </span> swolen.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got the most of the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie</a> attended to <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>the <span class='line-break'> </span> baby</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> To day is my birth day.  I am 73<span class='line-break'> </span> years olde.  I got up at five oclock<span class='line-break'> </span> and got <a href='../subjects/26' title='breakfast'>breakfast</a>. Seven: milked<span class='line-break'> </span> two <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cows</a> then <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Washed 68 pieces and went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  Come home and <a href='../subjects/15' title='milking'>milked</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Nellie &amp; Josie got the <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I kept <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>the baby</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben said he would carrie me<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7281' title='the river'>the river</a>.  I had no one<span class='line-break'> </span> to go with me.  Thought I<span class='line-break'> </span> would wait and go some other<span class='line-break'> </span> day if I <a href='../subjects/7371' title='canning'>can</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I started <a href='../subjects/209' title='John Brumfield'>John</a> a <a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben has gone <a href='../subjects/7631' title='hunting'>hunting</a> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8:30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1049">
<h3><a name="page-1049">Thursday, October 23, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> all day.  We have<span class='line-break'> </span> had a <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>good rain</a> last night <span class='line-break'> </span> and to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The men folks <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped tobacco</a><span class='line-break'> </span> all day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> carried the children<span class='line-break'> </span> to the <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school house</a> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I cooked most of the <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie</a> brought the <a href='../subjects/123' title='water'>water</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> &amp; Nellie washed the dishes <span class='line-break'> </span> at dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie got <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We <a href='../subjects/7355' title='shelling'>shelled</a> some <a href='../subjects/304' title='beans'>beans</a> tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben has gone to <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a> to<span class='line-break'> </span> some sort of <a href='../subjects/7498' title='speaking'>public speakin</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> All of the ballance of the folks<span class='line-break'> </span> has gone to bed.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1050">
<h3><a name="page-1050">Friday, October 24, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day.  The men<span class='line-break'> </span> folks <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped tobacco</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie</a> brought<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/123' title='water'>water</a> that she used and<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/36' title='wood'>wood</a> was in the <a href='../subjects/7609' title='house'>house</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I washed some.  Did not put<span class='line-break'> </span> out the clothes.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George Blairs</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia</a> and the girls was<span class='line-break'> </span> cleaning the yards.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/205' title='Cordie Blair'>Cordie Blair</a> has some beautiful<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7958' title='flowers'>flowers</a>.  <a href='../subjects/204' title='Isla Blair'>Isla</a> has not come<span class='line-break'> </span> home yet.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Tonight <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> has<span class='line-break'> </span> gone <a href='../subjects/7631' title='hunting'>hunting</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1051">
<h3><a name="page-1051">Saturday, October 25, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day.<span class='line-break'> </span> The men <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped tobacco</a> to<span class='line-break'> </span> day.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.  <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie</a> brough the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/123' title='water'>water</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> carried<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and I to <a href='../subjects/7206' title='White Falls, Virginia'>White Falls</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>caught 30 fish</a>.  Henry<span class='line-break'> </span> caught five.  Ben <a href='../subjects/7476' title='squirrel hunting'>killed<span class='line-break'> </span> two squirrels</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got three <a href='../subjects/7959' title='letters'>letters</a> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span> One from <a href='../subjects/7205' title='Effie Thornton Brumfield'>Effie</a>, <a href='../subjects/209' title='John Brumfield'>John</a>, &amp; <a href='../subjects/7224' title='Julia Ferguson'>Julia<span class='line-break'> </span> Fergerson</a>.  I am always<span class='line-break'> </span> so glad to get letters.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I dug the bait to fish with.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> helped me get them.<span class='line-break'> </span> She is a good help when <span class='line-break'> </span> she will.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1052">
<h3><a name="page-1052">Sunday, October 26, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Very <a href='../subjects/159' title='warm'>warm</a> for<span class='line-break'> </span> the time of year.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> &amp; I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie</a> went home this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> carried her to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> and <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> went.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a few<span class='line-break'> </span> minutes.  <a href='../subjects/153' title='Ren Worsham'>Ren</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7231' title='Ethel Worsham'>Ethel</a> and all<span class='line-break'> </span> their children come a while<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  I was glad to see<span class='line-break'> </span> them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We agreed to take <a href='../subjects/7963' title='Bessie Callands'>a negro girl</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to help us.  She came this morning<span class='line-break'> </span> to see us.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7961' title='Lawson Emerson'>Lawson Emerson</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7962' title='Joe Edmonds'>Jo Edmons</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come this evening<span class='line-break'> </span> to see <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7650' title='Aubrey Brumfield'>Aubra</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7649' title='Emmett Brumfield'>Emet Brumfield</a><span class='line-break'> </span> was at Marvins this evening<span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/52' title='Irvin Harvey'>Irvin Harvey</a>.  They had a <span class='line-break'> </span> time <a href='../subjects/422' title='bicycle'>riding wheels</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1053">
<h3><a name="page-1053">Monday, October 27, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/279' title='beautiful'>beautiful</a> day.  Very <a href='../subjects/159' title='warm'>warm</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> got up some <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/15' title='milking'>milked</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> for me this morning and<span class='line-break'> </span> carried me to <a href='../subjects/7461' title='Worsham&apos;s pond'>Worshams pond</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/205' title='Cordie Blair'>Cordie Blair</a> went with<span class='line-break'> </span> me.  We did not <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>catch <span class='line-break'> </span> any</a> <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/348' title='Mrs Edmonds'>Mrs Edmonds</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie Smith</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come to see <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a>.  I would <span class='line-break'> </span> of liked to have seen them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben went to <a href='../subjects/7965' title='Graves Moses'>Graves Moses</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and got <a href='../subjects/986' title='dog'>dog</a>.  He brought<span class='line-break'> </span> her home on the <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7966' title='Mrs Booker'>Mrs Booker</a> come to the <a href='../subjects/7530' title='mail'>mail</a><span class='line-break'> </span> box &amp; Cordie and I was<span class='line-break'> </span> there.  I was glad to see<span class='line-break'> </span> her for a few minutes.  I<span class='line-break'> </span> regard her as one of the<span class='line-break'> </span> nob[l]est  women that I know.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1054">
<h3><a name="page-1054">Tuesday, October 28, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A very <a href='../subjects/159' title='warm'>warm</a> day for Oct.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> until <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> then Owen went to<span class='line-break'> </span> help <a href='../subjects/262' title='Tom Peak'>Tom Peak</a> <a href='../subjects/201' title='shucking corn'>shuck corn</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben &amp; Jim &amp; <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7631' title='hunting'>hunting</a> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I got dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a><span class='line-break'> </span> a few minutes.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The <a href='../subjects/7967' title='road machine'>road machine</a> worked<span class='line-break'> </span> in front of the house this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/59' title='Charles Harvey'>Charles Harvey</a> come this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8:30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1055">
<h3><a name="page-1055">Wednesday, October 29, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> all day.  <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7203' title='Long Island, Virginia'>Long Island</a>.  Carried<span class='line-break'> </span> his <a href='../subjects/87' title='calves'>calf</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7963' title='Bessie Callands'>Bessie Callands (col)</a> come here<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning to work.<span class='line-break'> </span> I hope she may stay and <span class='line-break'> </span> be some help to us.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got the <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I washed a little this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johnson Reynolds</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> While I was gone <a href='../subjects/62' title='Miss Smith'>Miss Smith</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7964' title='Miss Carter'>Miss Carter</a> and <a href='../subjects/7897' title='Janie Gravely'>Janey<span class='line-break'> </span> Gravely</a> stopped to see<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie and <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>the baby</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I would liked to have seen<span class='line-break'> </span> them but they did not<span class='line-break'> </span> come to see me.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Tonight Ben &amp; <a href='../subjects/67' title='Willie Mayhew'>Willie Mayhew</a><span class='line-break'> </span> has gone <a href='../subjects/7631' title='hunting'>hunting</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9:15 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>

<div id="page-1056">
<h3><a name="page-1056">Thursday, October 30, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a>.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> dug <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>potatoes</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got the <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  She cooked<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/304' title='beans'>dried beans</a>.  The first this fall.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harveys</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/59' title='Charles Harvey'>Charle</a> was at home fixin up<span class='line-break'> </span> a grind stone.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7968' title='Edwin Mayhew'>Edwin Mayhew</a> is boardin<span class='line-break'> </span> there.  I went in the store<span class='line-break'> </span> for the first time since<span class='line-break'> </span> Mayhew has bin there.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> &amp; the children was here<span class='line-break'> </span> a while this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben &amp; Jim has gone <a href='../subjects/7631' title='hunting'>hunting</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
