<div id="page-1057">
<h3><a name="page-1057">Friday, October 31, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr. Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/7484' title='sowing wheat'>sowed<span class='line-break'> </span> wheat</a>.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7972' title='Lucius Gravely'>Lucius Graveley</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went with them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I got a <a href='../subjects/7570' title='snack'>snack</a><span class='line-break'> </span> for <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and I went with<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7963' title='Bessie Callands'>Bessie Callan (col)</a> to <a href='../subjects/7969' title='Mr Stone'>Mr<span class='line-break'> </span> Stones</a> then went to <a href='../subjects/7206' title='White Falls, Virginia'>White<span class='line-break'> </span> Falls</a>.  We <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fished</a> a while.<span class='line-break'> </span> Caught 25 <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> swept the <a href='../subjects/324' title='yard'>yard</a><span class='line-break'> </span> some.  I helped her get up<span class='line-break'> </span> the leaves.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> &amp; the children<span class='line-break'> </span> come a while this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7970' title='Fred Stone'>Fred Stone</a> brought Bessie <span class='line-break'> </span> home.  I paid him a dollar <span class='line-break'> </span> for it.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1058">
<h3><a name="page-1058">Saturday, November  1, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/187' title='cloudy'>clody</a> day and it is <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>raining</a><span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> is in <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a>.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7378' title='sowing'>sowed</a> some <a href='../subjects/7263' title='wheat'>wheat</a> and <a href='../subjects/7292' title='oats'>oats</a> today.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr. Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped tobacco</a> today.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  We picked up<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>potatoes</a> this morning and Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> hauled them home this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7963' title='Bessie Callands'>Bessie Callens (col)</a> washed<span class='line-break'> </span> some &amp; <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7971' title='Anna Callands'>Anna Callens</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come to see a bout Bess being<span class='line-break'> </span> here.  She let her stay.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I had thought that I would<span class='line-break'> </span> start to <a href='../subjects/7212' title='Richmond, Virginia'>Richmond</a> in the morning<span class='line-break'> </span> but it is raining so that I<span class='line-break'> </span> doubt it now.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben &amp; <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7972' title='Lucius Gravely'>Lucious Gravely</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went <a href='../subjects/7631' title='hunting'>hunting</a> tonight.  Guess<span class='line-break'> </span> they will get wet.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> It is lightning &amp; thundering.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1059">
<h3><a name="page-1059">Sunday, November  2, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  I got <a href='../subjects/26' title='breakfast'>breakfast</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/15' title='milking'>milked</a> the <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cows</a> then <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> carried <a href='../subjects/205' title='Cordie Blair'>Cordie</a> and I to <a href='../subjects/7203' title='Long Island, Virginia'>Long Island</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> We come on the <a href='../subjects/7973' title='Virginian Railway'>Virginian R-R</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7974' title='Alberta, Virginia'>Alberta</a>.  The[re] we had to wait<span class='line-break'> </span> for a train until dark then we<span class='line-break'> </span> came to <a href='../subjects/7212' title='Richmond, Virginia'>Richmond</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7215' title='William Brumfield'>Willie</a> &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7361' title='Julia Brumfield'>Julia</a> met us at <a href='../subjects/7682' title='depot'>the depot</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> We come on a <a href='../subjects/464' title='street car'>street car</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7215' title='William Brumfield'>Willies</a> <a href='../subjects/7609' title='house'>house</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7205' title='Effie Thornton Brumfield'>Effie</a> had <span class='line-break'> </span> a good <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.  I am so glad <span class='line-break'> </span> that we got here ok.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1060">
<h3><a name="page-1060">Monday, November  3, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/7205' title='Effie Thornton Brumfield'>Effie</a>, <a href='../subjects/205' title='Cordie Blair'>Cordie</a>,<span class='line-break'> </span> and I went to see <a href='../subjects/203' title='Alma Bennett'>Alma Bennett</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> She is in the <a href='../subjects/7799' title='hospital'>hospitle</a> in <a href='../subjects/7212' title='Richmond, Virginia'>Richmond</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Found her feeling good considering<span class='line-break'> </span> that she cant walk a step.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I <a href='../subjects/79' title='letter writing'>wrote</a> to <a href='../subjects/230' title='Lizzie Bennett'>Lizzie Bennett</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  I went and looked <span class='line-break'> </span> at the pretty <a href='../subjects/7958' title='flowers'>flowers</a> at the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7975' title='greenhouses'>green houses</a>.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1061">
<h3><a name="page-1061">Tuesday, November  4, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Did not see <a href='../subjects/203' title='Alma Bennett'>Alma</a><span class='line-break'> </span> today.  <a href='../subjects/7205' title='Effie Thornton Brumfield'>Effie</a> had company to day,<span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/7976' title='Mrs Lavender'>Mrs Lavender</a>.  She had a nice<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  Served it in three<span class='line-break'> </span> courses.  <a href='../subjects/7410' title='William Brumfield, Jr.'>William</a> had a <a href='../subjects/375' title='headache'>head<span class='line-break'> </span> ache</a> last night and was<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a> this morning.  Could not go<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.  He was better this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  William, <a href='../subjects/205' title='Cordie Blair'>Cordie</a>, and <span class='line-break'> </span> I went to Windensburg [?] Pond.<span class='line-break'> </span> We saw the prettiest <a href='../subjects/7958' title='flowers'>flowers</a> over<span class='line-break'> </span> there.  Great beds of cannas in<span class='line-break'> </span> bloom.  We walked over there and<span class='line-break'> </span> come back on the <a href='../subjects/464' title='street car'>street car</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7215' title='William Brumfield'>Will</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/51' title='Jack Harvey'>Jack Harvey</a> are talking<span class='line-break'> </span> a bout their <a href='../subjects/7977' title='books'>dr books</a>.  It is dry stuff to me.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1062">
<h3><a name="page-1062">Wednesday, November  5, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/7205' title='Effie Thornton Brumfield'>Effie</a> has bin very<span class='line-break'> </span> busy all day.  We went to the store<span class='line-break'> </span> late this evening.  Effie treated us to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/55' title='ice cream'>ice cream</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We come home on <a href='../subjects/464' title='street car'>street car</a> so crowded<span class='line-break'> </span> that several had to stand up.<span class='line-break'> </span> We did not buy anything.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7410' title='William Brumfield, Jr.'>Will Brumfield</a> has blowed his<span class='line-break'> </span> horn most of the time until<span class='line-break'> </span> bedtime.  <a href='../subjects/7350' title='Thelma Brumfield'>Thelma</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/216' title='Mary Brumfield'>Mary</a><span class='line-break'> </span> has bin studieing to night.<span class='line-break'> </span> Effie has bin <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewing</a> tonight<span class='line-break'> </span> on babie [?] <a href='../subjects/90' title='pants'>pants</a>.  I think she<span class='line-break'> </span> is about finished them.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1063">
<h3><a name="page-1063">Thursday, November  6, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  We [are] at <a href='../subjects/7215' title='William Brumfield'>Willies</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> yet.  We <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> some this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening <a href='../subjects/7205' title='Effie Thornton Brumfield'>Effie</a> and <a href='../subjects/205' title='Cordie Blair'>Cordie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7978' title='Hollywood Cemetery'>Hollie wood Cimetry</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> It is the granest place I<span class='line-break'> </span> ever saw.  More beautiful monuments <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7638' title='tombstones'>tomb stones</a> than one could<span class='line-break'> </span> think a bout that never was at<span class='line-break'> </span> a place of the sort.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got two <a href='../subjects/7959' title='letters'>letters</a> to day<span class='line-break'> </span> from home.  Was glad to hear<span class='line-break'> </span> that all was well.  Hope to be<span class='line-break'> </span> with them soon.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1064">
<h3><a name="page-1064">Friday, November  7, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A little <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a> today.  <a href='../subjects/7205' title='Effie Thornton Brumfield'>Effie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/205' title='Cordie Blair'>Corrie</a> and I went to see<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/203' title='Alma Bennett'>Alma</a>.  She is getting on fine.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We went to the <a href='../subjects/7979' title='Confederate Museum'>Confederate<span class='line-break'> </span> Musieum</a>.  Saw lots of things that<span class='line-break'> </span> I never expected to see.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We was out most all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Eat <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> down town.  It was<span class='line-break'> </span> not so good.  Cost 50 cts.<span class='line-break'> </span> I bought <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> a <a href='../subjects/7517' title='doll'>doll</a> today.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1065">
<h3><a name="page-1065">Saturday, November  8, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  We staid at<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7215' title='William Brumfield'>Willies</a>.  <a href='../subjects/205' title='Cordie Blair'>Cordie</a> went to see the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/293' title='doctor'>Dr</a>. He said that she must have<span class='line-break'> </span> her eyes treated for two or three<span class='line-break'> </span> day so I have agreed to stay<span class='line-break'> </span> until Thursday.  To night <a href='../subjects/7205' title='Effie Thornton Brumfield'>Effie</a> &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7980' title='Lillian Shelhorse'>Miss Lillian Shelhorse</a> and Cordie<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7410' title='William Brumfield, Jr.'>William</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7412' title='a show'>a show</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Injoyed it very much.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 11 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1066">
<h3><a name="page-1066">Sunday, November  9, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  We are at Wills<span class='line-break'> </span> yet.  Guess they wonde what happened<span class='line-break'> </span> that we did not come home.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Wills children had company this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening. <a href='../subjects/7981' title='Miss Wood'>Miss Wood</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7982' title='Miss Thomas'>Miss Thomas</a>,<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7955' title='Mr Haynes'>Mr Haynes</a>, <a href='../subjects/7410' title='William Brumfield, Jr.'>Will</a> and <a href='../subjects/7361' title='Julia Brumfield'>Julia Brumfield</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7984' title='Emily Lyle Brumfield'>Emily</a> &amp; I went walkin this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> It was so dark that I could<span class='line-break'> </span> not see much.  <a href='../subjects/205' title='Cordie Blair'>Cordie</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7350' title='Thelma Brumfield'>Thelma</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went to see <a href='../subjects/203' title='Alma Bennett'>Alma Bennett</a><span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.  <a href='../subjects/7215' title='William Brumfield'>Willie Brumfield</a> &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/51' title='Jack Harvey'>Jack Harvey</a> left tonight, one<span class='line-break'> </span> for Bluefield &amp; one for <a href='../subjects/7983' title='Ashland, North Carolina'>Ashland,<span class='line-break'> </span> N C</a> to a doctors meeting.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7205' title='Effie Thornton Brumfield'>Effie</a> is washing dishes now.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8:30 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1067">
<h3><a name="page-1067">Monday, November 10, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/205' title='Cordie Blair'>Cordie</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> to see the <a href='../subjects/293' title='doctor'>Drs</a> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> I staid at <a href='../subjects/7215' title='William Brumfield'>Willies</a> all day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Cordie and I went to see the<span class='line-break'> </span> big <a href='../subjects/7486' title='warehouses'>ware houses</a>.  I was a fraid<span class='line-break'> </span> I might get lost but I did<span class='line-break'> </span> not.  <a href='../subjects/7205' title='Effie Thornton Brumfield'>Effie</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/216' title='Mary Brumfield'>Mary</a> both put<span class='line-break'> </span> new cuffs &amp; collars on their<span class='line-break'> </span> coats.  <a href='../subjects/7985' title='Miss Walker'>Miss Walker</a> come with<span class='line-break'> </span> Cordie home from down town.<span class='line-break'> </span> Effie is makeing her a hat<span class='line-break'> </span> to wear to the <a href='../subjects/7986' title='parade'>parade</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Now it is bed time.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9: oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1068">
<h3><a name="page-1068">Tuesday, November 11, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rainy</a> day.  We are still at<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7212' title='Richmond, Virginia'>Richmond</a>.  They expected to have<span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/7986' title='parade'>parade</a> here to day but it <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rained</a><span class='line-break'> </span> so they did not have it.  There is <span class='line-break'> </span> all sorts of side showes and<span class='line-break'> </span> merry go rounds in the city.  We<span class='line-break'> </span> that is <a href='../subjects/7205' title='Effie Thornton Brumfield'>Effie Brumfield</a> and all<span class='line-break'> </span> of her children, <a href='../subjects/205' title='Cordie Blair'>Cordie Blair</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; I went to the city.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We went to see <a href='../subjects/203' title='Alma Bennett'>Alma Bennett</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> She is in the best of spirits.<span class='line-break'> </span> They have taken off the cast<span class='line-break'> </span> that they had on her leg.  She<span class='line-break'> </span> has a room mate that has a <span class='line-break'> </span> baby.  Alma says that she likes<span class='line-break'> </span> her fine.  <a href='../subjects/7215' title='William Brumfield'>Willie</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/51' title='Jack Harvey'>Jack</a> are away<span class='line-break'> </span> yet.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1069">
<h3><a name="page-1069">Wednesday, November 12, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rainy</a> day.  We went<span class='line-break'> </span> down town.  Come home and eat<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7205' title='Effie Thornton Brumfield'>Effie</a> locked the doors and<span class='line-break'> </span> could not unlock them so she<span class='line-break'> </span> got a man to come and bring <span class='line-break'> </span> a ladder and climed up on<span class='line-break'> </span> the porch and went in at the<span class='line-break'> </span> window.  We have eaten <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and will go down town to night <span class='line-break'> </span> I guess.  Hope to be at home<span class='line-break'> </span> this time tomorrow and hope to<span class='line-break'> </span> find them all well.  <a href='../subjects/205' title='Cordie Blair'>Cordie</a> got<span class='line-break'> </span> her <a href='../subjects/7987' title='glasses'>glasses</a> today.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1070">
<h3><a name="page-1070">Thursday, November 13, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rainy</a> morning.  Clear<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  I come from<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7212' title='Richmond, Virginia'>Richmond</a> to day.  There was no<span class='line-break'> </span> one to meet us so a <a href='../subjects/7988' title='Mr Davis'>Mr Davis</a><span class='line-break'> </span> brought us to <a href='../subjects/7342' title='Cedar Forest'>Cedar Forest</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> brought us<span class='line-break'> </span> home.  Found them all well.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am glad that I am at<span class='line-break'> </span> home.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> is helping <span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripping<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco</a>.  I am talkin so much<span class='line-break'> </span> that I cant write like I<span class='line-break'> </span> ought.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1071">
<h3><a name="page-1071">Friday, November 14, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7736' title='hauling feed'>hauled</a> in some feed and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7547' title='hauling wood'>wood</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> &amp; the children has<span class='line-break'> </span> got bad <a href='../subjects/297' title='colds'>colds</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.  They come home<span class='line-break'> </span> at twelve.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> There was a <a href='../subjects/7543' title='killing frost'>killing frost</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this morning for the first<span class='line-break'> </span> one this year.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> It is colde<span class='line-break'> </span> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben and Josie keep talkin<span class='line-break'> </span> a bout killing a <a href='../subjects/7574' title='beef'>beef</a><span class='line-break'> </span> so that I cant waite.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1072">
<h3><a name="page-1072">Saturday, November 15, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> cut <a href='../subjects/174' title='feed'>feed</a> and <a href='../subjects/7531' title='sawing'>sawed wood</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am glad that they got it<span class='line-break'> </span> done.  Ben has gone <a href='../subjects/7631' title='hunting'>hunting</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.  Jim went to bed.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> went to <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> carried <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>her baby</a> the <span class='line-break'> </span> first time it was out <span class='line-break'> </span> of the house.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> has nursed her <a href='../subjects/7517' title='doll'>doll</a><span class='line-break'> </span> most of the day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> helped to cut feed<span class='line-break'> </span> and wood most of the day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1073">
<h3><a name="page-1073">Sunday, November 16, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A bright day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> carried<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs. Car</a> home this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> &amp; three of the children<span class='line-break'> </span> went two.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> and I went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> and eat <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went two after dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry &amp; <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> and <a href='../subjects/7656' title='Paul'>Paul</a> went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/153' title='Ren Worsham'>Ren Worshams</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Rees</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a><span class='line-break'> </span> on his <a href='../subjects/422' title='bicycle'>wheel</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Jim &amp; Marvin went to a crab<span class='line-break'> </span> apple tree.  Jim had the<span class='line-break'> </span> children bite them.  They<span class='line-break'> </span> thought it fun.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> All have gone to bed so<span class='line-break'> </span> I guess I had better go.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1074">
<h3><a name="page-1074">Monday, November 17, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7587' title='cattle killing'>killed a beef</a> this morning<span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped tobacco</a> this evening<span class='line-break'> </span> and to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening I went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George Blairs</a>. They were all<span class='line-break'> </span> busy.  <a href='../subjects/206' title='Nettie Blair'>Nettie</a> was fixin a <span class='line-break'> </span> box to take to the <a href='../subjects/194' title='school house'>school<span class='line-break'> </span> house</a>.  Some of them were<span class='line-break'> </span> strippin tobacco.  <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Reynolds</a> come while I was<span class='line-break'> </span> gone.  I was so sorry that<span class='line-break'> </span> I was not at home.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/308' title='Hugh Brumfield'>Hugh Brumfield</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Rees Smith</a><span class='line-break'> </span> are here tonight.  They are all<span class='line-break'> </span> playing Carom [?]<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I carried my <a href='../subjects/7920' title='pen'>pen</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/436' title='ink'>ink</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to the dineing room this morning<span class='line-break'> </span> and was two lazy to go after<span class='line-break'> </span> them to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9:15 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1075">
<h3><a name="page-1075">Tuesday, November 18, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped tobacco</a> all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7963' title='Bessie Callands'>Bessie the colored<span class='line-break'> </span> girl</a> washed.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> was washing.  She finished <span class='line-break'> </span> while I was there.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We heard to night over the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/158' title='telephones'>phone</a> that <a href='../subjects/7990' title='Ludia Barnett'>Ludia Barnett</a><span class='line-break'> </span> was <a href='../subjects/96' title='death'>killed</a> by a <a href='../subjects/7991' title='train'>train</a><span class='line-break'> </span> today.  That is so bad.  Her<span class='line-break'> </span> folks will miss her so much.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> made <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> a cap<span class='line-break'> </span> and a box.  Had good luck<span class='line-break'> </span> with both.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 7:30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1076">
<h3><a name="page-1076">Wednesday, November 19, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> <a href='../subjects/274' title='cool'>cool</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped tobacco</a>.  It was so<span class='line-break'> </span> dry they could not do much at it.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> made a<span class='line-break'> </span> box for <a href='../subjects/416' title='Beatrice Owen'>Beatrice Owen</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben and Josie went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a> a few minutes at<span class='line-break'> </span> twelve.  <a href='../subjects/7884' title='Willie Wooding'>Miss Willie Wooding</a> come<span class='line-break'> </span> a while this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie has had the <a href='../subjects/66' title='toothache'>tooth ache</a><span class='line-break'> </span> all the evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben &amp; Jim went to the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a> to night to <a href='../subjects/7357' title='tying'>tie some<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco</a> &amp; have not come<span class='line-break'> </span> to the house yet.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1077">
<h3><a name="page-1077">Thursday, November 20, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped tobacco</a> all day and until<span class='line-break'> </span> bed time tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> then I went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johnson Reynols</a>. <a href='../subjects/407' title='Clack Hubbard'>Clack</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/369' title='Kate Reynolds'>Kate Hubard</a> was there.<span class='line-break'> </span> Today was the first time<span class='line-break'> </span> that I ever saw <a href='../subjects/7992' title='Clack Hubbard, Jr.'>their baby</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> He is a fine baby.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Every body here has some<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/13' title='cold'>cold</a>.  I feel bad to night.<span class='line-break'> </span> I have made <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a><span class='line-break'> </span> a ball out of old <a href='../subjects/333' title='socks'>socks</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Just finished them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8:30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1078">
<h3><a name="page-1078">Friday, November 21, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped tobacco</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> baked a<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/240' title='cake'>cake</a> for to be solde at the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/194' title='school house'>school house</a>.  The cake brought<span class='line-break'> </span> a good sum.  The boxes all<span class='line-break'> </span> solde well.  There was a big<span class='line-break'> </span> crowd at the school<span class='line-break'> </span> house.  I was the oldest person<span class='line-break'> </span> there.  <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr. Owen</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7471' title='Luke'>Luke</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> went with Ben.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7994' title='Grace Wills'>Miss Grace Wills</a> got the<span class='line-break'> </span> cake for <a href='../subjects/7995' title='beauty contest'>being the prettyes girl</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim Brumfield</a> stripped tobacco<span class='line-break'> </span> while we went to the school<span class='line-break'> </span> house.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 11: oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Heard tonight that <a href='../subjects/7752' title='Lottie Kellie'>Lottie Kellie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> has a new boy.  Came this morning.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1079">
<h3><a name="page-1079">Saturday, November 22, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rainy</a> morning.  Clear<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> cut out<span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a> this morning &amp; hemed<span class='line-break'> </span> two sheets.  I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening I went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  Marvin went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a> to <a href='../subjects/7228' title='preaching'>preaching</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I come by the <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a> and <a href='../subjects/7357' title='tying'>tied</a><span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a>.  Josie had <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a><span class='line-break'> </span> a bout done when I come to the <a href='../subjects/7609' title='house'>house</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> has gone to <span class='line-break'> </span> Strait Stone to night to and<span class='line-break'> </span> Odd Fellows meeting.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got a <a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a> from <a href='../subjects/7205' title='Effie Thornton Brumfield'>Effie<span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield</a> today.  One from<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7921' title='Fannie Emerson'>Fanny Emerson</a> yesterday.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1080">
<h3><a name="page-1080">Sunday, November 23, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>Clear this morning.  Some <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a><span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> and <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> the children all staid at home<span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to see <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate<span class='line-break'> </span> Harvey</a> this morning.  I had not<span class='line-break'> </span> bin there long before they <a href='../subjects/158' title='telephones'>phoned</a><span class='line-break'> </span> me that <a href='../subjects/230' title='Lizzie Bennett'>Lizzie Bennett</a> had come.<span class='line-break'> </span> I started home.  I met Ben <span class='line-break'> </span> at <a href='../subjects/376' title='Posey Reynolds'>Posies</a> <a href='../subjects/7530' title='mail'>mail</a> box with the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a>.  Kate walked with me that <span class='line-break'> </span> far and then turned back.<span class='line-break'> </span> She would of come home with<span class='line-break'> </span> me but she was lookin for<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7795' title='Dr Wigginton'>Dr Wigginton</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/360' title='Pearl Harvey'>Pearl</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Lizzie went to <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George Blairs</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and I went with her.  I staid<span class='line-break'> </span> until 8 oclock.  <a href='../subjects/7855' title='George William Blair'>George Blair<span class='line-break'> </span> Junior</a> brought me home.  <a href='../subjects/204' title='Isla Blair'>Isla</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come with me &amp; went back<span class='line-break'> </span> with George.  I thank them <span class='line-break'> </span> for their kindness.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8:30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1081">
<h3><a name="page-1081">Monday, November 24, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco</a>.  <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr. Owen</a> and I<span class='line-break'> </span> helped.  Finished a while<span class='line-break'> </span> be fore night.  I went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a few minutes.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7963' title='Bessie Callands'>Bessie (col)</a> washed some.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/153' title='Ren Worsham'>Ren Worsham</a> come over.<span class='line-break'> </span> Got a few <a href='../subjects/7265' title='onions'>onions</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim &amp; Ben has gone <span class='line-break'> </span> to the <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1082">
<h3><a name="page-1082">Tuesday, November 25, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day.  We all <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco</a> all day.  <a href='../subjects/7963' title='Bessie Callands'>Bess (col)</a> washed.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7927' title='South Boston, Virginia'>Boston</a> with<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/128' title='tobacco sale'>his last tobacco</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7675' title='Charlie Hutcherson'>Charley Hutcherson</a><span class='line-break'> </span> carried it.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> has not come from<span class='line-break'> </span> the farm yet tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie is <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sowing</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I <a href='../subjects/79' title='letter writing'>wrote</a> <a href='../subjects/7921' title='Fannie Emerson'>Fannie Emerson</a> tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 7:30 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1083">
<h3><a name="page-1083">Wednesday, November 26, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day &amp; <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>some rain</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> We all <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped tobacco</a> most<span class='line-break'> </span> of the day and finished this <span class='line-break'> </span> years crop.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin Smith</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/128' title='tobacco sale'>solde</a> all of his crop today<span class='line-break'> </span> at <a href='../subjects/7927' title='South Boston, Virginia'>Boston</a>.  Was well pleased<span class='line-break'> </span> with the prices.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I went<span class='line-break'> </span> to see <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> a few minutes <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> has gone to <a href='../subjects/67' title='Willie Mayhew'>Willie<span class='line-break'> </span> Mayhews</a> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and probably to <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The teacher of Renan <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a><span class='line-break'> </span> has gone to <a href='../subjects/7212' title='Richmond, Virginia'>Richmond</a> to<span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/109' title='teachers'>teachers</a> meeting.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went to<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school house</a> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8:15 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1084">
<h3><a name="page-1084">Thursday, November 27, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/279' title='beautiful'>beautiful</a> <a href='../subjects/159' title='warm'>warm</a> morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> I would of given either of the<span class='line-break'> </span> boys five dollars to have taken<span class='line-break'> </span> me where I could of <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fished</a> some<span class='line-break'> </span> but did not say a word about<span class='line-break'> </span> it.  I was afraid they would deny<span class='line-break'> </span> me &amp; belitle me for being so foolish<span class='line-break'> </span> and it hurts so bad to be denied.<span class='line-break'> </span> In the place of <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fishing</a> I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and helped to clean the <a href='../subjects/324' title='yard'>yard</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and draped and covered two rows<span class='line-break'> </span> of <a href='../subjects/7265' title='onions'>onions</a> and went to <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a><span class='line-break'> </span> a few minutes.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> finished <span class='line-break'> </span> diggin Irish <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>potatoes</a> and put them<span class='line-break'> </span> in kiln in the <a href='../subjects/290' title='garden'>garden</a>.  Fixed the<span class='line-break'> </span> land to plant onions. <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Then <a href='../subjects/7721' title='hauling stalks'>hauled some stalks</a> to <a href='../subjects/174' title='feed'>feed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cows</a>.  To night Ben &amp; <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a>.  I stayed with<span class='line-break'> </span> the children.  Josie got a package<span class='line-break'> </span> from <a href='../subjects/7203' title='Long Island, Virginia'>the island</a> to day.  She gave<span class='line-break'> </span> me a nice <a href='../subjects/7403' title='sweater'>sweater</a>.  I am glad of <span class='line-break'> </span> it.  I am so near a sleep that I<span class='line-break'> </span> cant hardely write.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1085">
<h3><a name="page-1085">Friday, November 28, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> went to the <a href='../subjects/44' title='mill'>mill</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and I am glad.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7963' title='Bessie Callands'>Bess (col)</a> and the child[ren]<span class='line-break'> </span> worked on the <a href='../subjects/324' title='yard'>yard</a><span class='line-break'> </span> some.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> went to <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a><span class='line-break'> </span> a while.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> brought<span class='line-break'> </span> two bbls of <a href='../subjects/7523' title='flour'>flour</a> from<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> and the cradle.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewed</a> some.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I cant find my <a href='../subjects/7987' title='glasses'>glasses</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to nigh and I am<span class='line-break'> </span> mad.  We finished<span class='line-break'> </span> getting out a few [?]<span class='line-break'> </span> today.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1086">
<h3><a name="page-1086">Saturday, November 29, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p><a href='../subjects/187' title='cloudy'>Cloudy</a> this morning &amp; some<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/7547' title='hauling wood'>hauled some<span class='line-break'> </span> wood</a> this morning.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  I <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a> and stayed<span class='line-break'> </span> with <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>the baby</a>.  She did not cry<span class='line-break'> </span> while they were gone.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I went to <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George<span class='line-break'> </span> Blair</a>.  Got there as the men<span class='line-break'> </span> folks come from work.  <a href='../subjects/7998' title='Denny'>Denny</a><span class='line-break'> </span> was there.  He had bin <a href='../subjects/7631' title='hunting'>hunting</a><span class='line-break'> </span> all the morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia</a> and I went to see<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7999' title='Elizabeth Allen'>Mrs. Allen</a>.  She is <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>very feeble</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8000' title='Mrs. Kellie'>Mrs. Kellie</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/8001' title='Mrs. Strange'>Mrs. Strange</a> was there.<span class='line-break'> </span> The narce is a nice lookin<span class='line-break'> </span> lady.  They are having a time there then[?]<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1087">
<h3><a name="page-1087">Sunday, November 30, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> rambled a round all day.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I <a href='../subjects/7587' title='cattle killing'>killed</a> a <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chicken</a> &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> dressed it ready to cook.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to see <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/335' title='Margaret Brumfield'>Mag</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I eat dinner with Kate.  She<span class='line-break'> </span> was at home by her self.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening <a href='../subjects/7795' title='Dr Wigginton'>Dr</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/360' title='Pearl Harvey'>Pearl Wiggin</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/59' title='Charles Harvey'>Charles</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/52' title='Irvin Harvey'>Irvin Harvey</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come to <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kates</a>.  We were at<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/335' title='Margaret Brumfield'>Mags</a>.  I was glad to see the <span class='line-break'> </span> children.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I walked all the way home<span class='line-break'> </span> and nearly all the way there.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7689' title='Claude Edmonds'>Claude Edmons</a> carried me on<span class='line-break'> </span> their <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a> from our <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a> to<span class='line-break'> </span> the fork of the road at<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johnson Reynolds</a> barn.  I was<span class='line-break'> </span> mighty glad of that much help.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1630' title='Virginia Harvey'>Virginia Harvey</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> back to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9:30 ocl</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1088">
<h3><a name="page-1088">Monday, December  1, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A bright day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> loaded <a href='../subjects/67' title='Willie Mayhew'>Mr Mayhews</a> <a href='../subjects/219' title='truck'>truck</a> with<span class='line-break'> </span> their <a href='../subjects/128' title='tobacco sale'>tobacco</a> and they started<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7927' title='South Boston, Virginia'>Boston</a> this evening.  I do hope<span class='line-break'> </span> that they will get on OK.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> &amp; I <a href='../subjects/131' title='feeding'>fed</a> the <a href='../subjects/134' title='hogs'>hogs</a> tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie got <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7963' title='Bessie Callands'>Bessie (col)</a> did not come in<span class='line-break'> </span> until a bout night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I was at <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> a few<span class='line-break'> </span> minutes this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8:30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1089">
<h3><a name="page-1089">Tuesday, December  2, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/128' title='tobacco sale'>solde</a> the last of their <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a><span class='line-break'> </span> today.  They were not pleased<span class='line-break'> </span> with the sales.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/59' title='Charles Harvey'>Charles Harvey</a> come this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning and got the <a href='../subjects/133' title='horses'>team</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/115' title='wagon'>waggon</a> and said he was going<span class='line-break'> </span> to haul <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>his mother</a> some<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/36' title='wood'>wood</a>.  I was glad that he<span class='line-break'> </span> would get some wood for<span class='line-break'> </span> her.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a<span class='line-break'> </span> few minutes this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <sensitive>I feel so bad tonight<span class='line-break'> </span> that I cant help crying.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> am not sick but things <span class='line-break'> </span> has changed so much at <span class='line-break'> </span> [?]where once was a happy<span class='line-break'> </span> home to what it is now.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am one to my self.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> work like a servant but I<span class='line-break'> </span> am a mere nobody in every other<span class='line-break'> </span> way.  I guess I should not say<span class='line-break'> </span> any thing a bout it but I<span class='line-break'> </span> holde it and not say.  No one knows <span class='line-break'> </span> but my self.</sensitive><span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8:30 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1090">
<h3><a name="page-1090">Wednesday, December  3, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>colde</a> day.   <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> helped <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/265' title='hog killing'>kill hogs</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I washed some.  <a href='../subjects/7963' title='Bessie Callands'>Bess (col)</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> stayed with the children<span class='line-break'> </span> while Marvin &amp; <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7304' title='Riceville, Virginia'>Riceville</a> to see<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8003' title='Owen Smith'>Owen Smith</a> <a href='../subjects/7317' title='wedding'>married</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin come part of the way<span class='line-break'> </span> home.  Ben and <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> had not<span class='line-break'> </span> gone to bed when I got<span class='line-break'> </span> home.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10:30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1091">
<h3><a name="page-1091">Thursday, December  4, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day most of the <span class='line-break'> </span> time.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/265' title='hog killing'>killed hogs</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben had four &amp; Jim two.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin Smith</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Sam Owen</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/75' title='William Gilbert'>William Gilbert (col)</a> helped<span class='line-break'> </span> them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/8004' title='Betty Haley'>Betty Haley (col)</a> helped<span class='line-break'> </span> me.  We got on fine.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  She <a href='../subjects/8005' title='rendering lard'>dried out<span class='line-break'> </span> some of the fat</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Jim &amp; Ben went to <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The children are <a href='../subjects/8006' title='dominoes'>playing <span class='line-break'> </span> domminoes</a> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 7:30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1092">
<h3><a name="page-1092">Friday, December  5, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A day that all could work.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/7531' title='sawing'>sawed<span class='line-break'> </span> wood</a> then went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> cut some <a href='../subjects/174' title='feed'>feed</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  She made the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7622' title='sausage'>sausage</a> for Jim and her self.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8004' title='Betty Haley'>Bettie Haley (col)</a> helped to cut <span class='line-break'> </span> the fat up and grind the<span class='line-break'> </span> sausage.  I dried up the <a href='../subjects/7620' title='lard'>lard</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and strained it out.<span class='line-break'> </span> Bettie wshed the faces and feet.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Heard to day that Mrs<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/200' title='Richard Wooding'>Richard Wooding</a> has a son.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/393' title='Sallie Blair'>Sallie Blair</a> taught <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a><span class='line-break'> </span> in Miss Smiths room today.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Car</a> sent <a href='../subjects/7963' title='Bessie Callands'>Bessie Callans<span class='line-break'> </span> (col)</a> a ring.  She got it today.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Mr Owen went to the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/44' title='mill'>mill</a> today.  Brough me some<span class='line-break'> </span> brand.  Jim &amp; Ben &amp; Josie<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/946' title='playing cards'>played cards</a> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>

<div id="page-1093">
<h3><a name="page-1093">Saturday, December  6, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rainy</a> day most of<span class='line-break'> </span> the time.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a><span class='line-break'> </span> hauled some <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a>.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> to the store.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>

Bought<span class='line-break'> </span> it from <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Car</a>.  They paid<span class='line-break'> </span> $10 dollars per bbl.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a few<span class='line-break'> </span> minutes this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/104' title='Tom Edmonds'>Tom Edmons</a> was here awhile<span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.  <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> come in my<span class='line-break'> </span> room &amp; went to sleep in my lap.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We finished up after<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/265' title='hog killing'>killing hogs</a> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>

<p> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/212' title='Roy Smith'>Roy</a> and <a href='../subjects/222' title='Hazel Smith'>Hazel</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come down here a few<span class='line-break'> </span> minutes late this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> It is <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> tonight.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> am thinkin it will rain before<span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>

Guess they will<span class='line-break'> </span> have that to do now Bess is gone.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>

<h3><a name="page-1103">Tuesday, December 16, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7721' title='hauling stalks'>hauled some stalks</a> and <a href='../subjects/943' title='cutting feed'>cut<span class='line-break'> </span> feed</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed a gain today.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  Boiled <a href='../subjects/260' title='meat'>meat</a><span class='line-break'> </span> in the dineing room &amp; started<span class='line-break'> </span> to the <a href='../subjects/7382' title='kitchen'>cook room</a> and stumbled<span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/120' title='falling'>fell</a> and spilt some of<span class='line-break'> </span> the meat.  It did not hurt me.<span class='line-break'> </span> Burnt me a little.  I am glad <span class='line-break'> </span> it did not hurt me and I am<span class='line-break'> </span> very sorrie that it happened.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I hemed two little sheets<span class='line-break'> </span> for <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklins</a> bed.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia Blair</a> come this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I was very glad to see<span class='line-break'> </span> her.  I have not seen any of<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> folks this week.<span class='line-break'> </span> Hope that tomorrow will be <span class='line-break'> </span> good.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
