<div id="page-1105">
<h3><a name="page-1105">Thursday, December 18, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A very colde day.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/7667' title='burning plantbeds'>burnt a plant<span class='line-break'> </span> bed</a> to day. <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I kept <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>the baby</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> some this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/8012' title='S[eu?]la[r?] Hayley'>S[eu?]la[r?] Hayley</a> come and<span class='line-break'> </span> brought some <a href='../subjects/36' title='wood'>wood</a> to the<span class='line-break'> </span> porch and carried some up<span class='line-break'> </span> stairs.  Want to have some<span class='line-break'> </span> ready for Xmas.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Today is <a href='../subjects/222' title='Hazel Smith'>Hazel Smiths</a> birth day.<span class='line-break'> </span> I would of went up there<span class='line-break'> </span> but did have time and do <span class='line-break'> </span> the ironing.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8:30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1106">
<h3><a name="page-1106">Friday, December 19, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A bad day.  <a href='../subjects/147' title='hail'>Hailed</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/50' title='sleet'>sleet</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> put in some <a href='../subjects/7555' title='glazing'>window glass</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> attended to the stock.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.  <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> played and made<span class='line-break'> </span> all the nois that they could.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a> cried a lot.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I commenced a <a href='../subjects/8' title='quilting'>quilt</a> for Josie.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Jim &amp; Ben has gone to <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a><span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.  I think they will<span class='line-break'> </span> have a rough time.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1107">
<h3><a name="page-1107">Saturday, December 20, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> day.  The <a href='../subjects/3' title='ice'>ice</a> melted<span class='line-break'> </span> some.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> <a href='../subjects/8013' title='sledding'>rode on his sled</a><span class='line-break'> </span> a while this morning.  Tonight<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry &amp; <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> has <a href='../subjects/8014' title='coughing'>bad coughs</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> stayed a round<span class='line-break'> </span> home all day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/7531' title='sawing'>sawed wood</a> for <a href='../subjects/7924' title='Mr Edmonds'>Mr<span class='line-break'> </span> Edmons</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  Boiled the<span class='line-break'> </span> last <a href='../subjects/8015' title='hog feet'>hog feet</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> starched the cloths<span class='line-break'> </span> that she washed the first<span class='line-break'> </span> of the week.<span class='line-break'> </span> Tonight she washed up the<span class='line-break'> </span> diningroom floor.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1108">
<h3><a name="page-1108">Sunday, December 21, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> brought<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/134' title='hogs'>Bell</a> from <a href='../subjects/7563' title='Mr Layne'>Mr Laynes</a> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> &amp; I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/424' title='Doris Brumfield'>Doris</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7651' title='Janie Brumfield'>Janie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7650' title='Aubrey Brumfield'>Aubra Brumfield</a> come here<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening. <a href='../subjects/52' title='Irvin Harvey'>Irvin Harvey</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/325' title='Paul Smith'>Paul<span class='line-break'> </span> Smith</a> come a while. I went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a few minutes.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie got <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I put on a pair of bed room<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7630' title='slippers'>slippers</a> that Josie gave me. I like<span class='line-break'> </span> them fine.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1109">
<h3><a name="page-1109">Monday, December 22, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> home.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7208' title='Altavista, Virginia'>Altavista</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> baked some <a href='../subjects/37' title='cakes'>cakes</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; washed some.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/7531' title='sawing'>sawed wood</a> for <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lee</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Two col girls washed <span class='line-break'> </span> for Josie.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I kept <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>the baby</a> most<span class='line-break'> </span> of the day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1110">
<h3><a name="page-1110">Tuesday, December 23, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/7531' title='sawing'>sawed<span class='line-break'> </span> wood</a> at <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lee Brumfields</a>.  Got<span class='line-break'> </span> home at dark.  He went over<span class='line-break'> </span> to the <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school house</a>.  <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> with him.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> was over there.<span class='line-break'> </span> They got home at 10 oclock.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> nearly all day and until<span class='line-break'> </span> 9 oclock to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I made <a href='../subjects/7278' title='scrapple'>scrappel</a> and press<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/260' title='meat'>meat</a>.  I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and got a boiler to cook in.<span class='line-break'> </span> To night I worked some button<span class='line-break'> </span> holes and hemed a table<span class='line-break'> </span> cloth.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10:30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1111">
<h3><a name="page-1111">Wednesday, December 24, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Colde tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; I went to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait<span class='line-break'> </span> Stone</a> and bought several<span class='line-break'> </span> things.  <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Sam Owen</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> to the <a href='../subjects/44' title='mill'>mill</a>.  Carried some<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a> for us.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> baked some <a href='../subjects/37' title='cakes'>cakes</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Give <a href='../subjects/75' title='William Gilbert'>William Gilbert</a> one.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/153' title='Ren Worsham'>Ren</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7231' title='Ethel Worsham'>Ethel Worsham</a> sent<span class='line-break'> </span> me a nice <a href='../subjects/7403' title='sweater'>sweater</a> for a Xmas<span class='line-break'> </span> gift.  Josie and I had a <a href='../subjects/7696' title='postcard'>card</a><span class='line-break'> </span> from <a href='../subjects/8016' title='Irene Dyer'>Irene Dyer</a>. This evening<span class='line-break'> </span> I had one from <a href='../subjects/7224' title='Julia Ferguson'>Julia Fergerson</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Guess she is at <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>her fathers</a> tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> <a href='../subjects/265' title='hog killing'>killed</a> two <a href='../subjects/7833' title='ducks'>ducks</a> today<span class='line-break'> </span> and I dressed them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I don't think that Henry can<span class='line-break'> </span> go to sleep tonight for wanting to<span class='line-break'> </span> know what Santy will bring.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Well I may never see another<span class='line-break'> </span> Xmas.  We have bin well all<span class='line-break'> </span> the year.  Have not missed a night<span class='line-break'> </span> waiting on account of <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sickness</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8:30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1112">
<h3><a name="page-1112">Thursday, December 25, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/279' title='beautiful'>beautiful</a> day.  We was all <span class='line-break'> </span> at home at <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/7631' title='hunting'>hunted</a> a little.<span class='line-break'> </span> He killed a <a href='../subjects/7312' title='rabbits'>rabbit</a> and a bird.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got dinner.  We had <a href='../subjects/8017' title='spare ribs'>sparribs</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/236' title='cabbage'>cabbage</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chicken</a> and <a href='../subjects/37' title='cakes'>cakes</a>.  We had no company.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> children come a while this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> Carries and <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Bens</a> children gave me<span class='line-break'> </span> some nice <a href='../subjects/7633' title='presents'>presents</a>.  I was invited to dinner<span class='line-break'> </span> at <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lee Brumfields</a> but I did not go.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> straitened up things some but <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>the<span class='line-break'> </span> baby</a> cried so much that she could<span class='line-break'> </span> not do anything much.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The children spent the day playing<span class='line-break'> </span> with the toys that they got this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1113">
<h3><a name="page-1113">Friday, December 26, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/7631' title='hunting'>hunted</a><span class='line-break'> </span> some this morning.  <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> come a while today.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> and eat<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <a href='../subjects/241' title='Mr Padget'>Mr Padget</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/8018' title='Dr Smith'>Dr Smith</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/8019' title='Mrs Smith'>Mrs Smith</a> was there.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> had a nice dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> Had a <a href='../subjects/140' title='turkey'>turkey</a> and <a href='../subjects/248' title='ham'>ham</a> &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/37' title='cakes'>cakes</a> of different sorts<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8020' title='cranberry sauce'>cranberrie sauce</a> and <a href='../subjects/54' title='custard'>custard</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7350' title='Thelma Brumfield'>Thelma</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/216' title='Mary Brumfield'>Mary Brumfield</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/51' title='Jack Harvey'>Jack Harvey</a> come from<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7212' title='Richmond, Virginia'>Richmond</a> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben went to <a href='../subjects/7203' title='Long Island, Virginia'>Long Island</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> for them.  <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a> had a <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/19' title='dance'>dance</a> tonight.  Had one at <a href='../subjects/218' title='George Hutcherson'>George<span class='line-break'> </span> Hutchersons</a> tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben &amp; Jack and <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> Thelma &amp; Mary and <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went up there and staid<span class='line-break'> </span> a while.  Thelm &amp; Mary brought<span class='line-break'> </span> me <a href='../subjects/7632' title='diary'>a book for 1920</a>.  Also a<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7920' title='pen'>founing pen</a> &amp; some <a href='../subjects/42' title='candy'>candy</a>.  I am<span class='line-break'> </span> glad of them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 11 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1114">
<h3><a name="page-1114">Saturday, December 27, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7631' title='hunting'>hunted</a> some.  <a href='../subjects/406' title='Bruce Reynolds'>Bruce Reynolds</a> come<span class='line-break'> </span> to see <a href='../subjects/7350' title='Thelma Brumfield'>Thelma</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/216' title='Mary Brumfield'>Mary</a>.  They went<span class='line-break'> </span> with him home and staid a while.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> &amp; I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  We had two<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7833' title='ducks'>ducks</a> for dinner.  They were fine.<span class='line-break'> </span> I killed and dressed a <a href='../subjects/140' title='turkey'>turkey</a><span class='line-break'> </span> today.  Ben &amp; Thelma &amp; Mary<span class='line-break'> </span> has gone to <a href='../subjects/7283' title='Bob Starkey'>Bob Starkeys</a> to a <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/48' title='party'>party</a> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/406' title='Bruce Reynolds'>Bruce</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/228' title='Clifton Reynolds'>Clifton</a> and <a href='../subjects/7333' title='Jane Reynolds'>Jane<span class='line-break'> </span> Reynolds</a> went to <a href='../subjects/8440' title='Mrs. Gravely'>Mrs Gravelys</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8:30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1115">
<h3><a name="page-1115">Sunday, December 28, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; family <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7350' title='Thelma Brumfield'>Thelma</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/216' title='Mary Brumfield'>Mary</a> went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7240' title='Jim Power'>Jim Powers</a> and spent <span class='line-break'> </span> the day.  <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Car</a> gave them<span class='line-break'> </span> several new <a href='../subjects/7633' title='presents'>presents</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I staid at home all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Swept the floors, <a href='../subjects/131' title='feeding'>fed</a> the <a href='../subjects/370' title='pigs'>pigs</a>,<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/15' title='milking'>milked</a> the <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cows</a>, got in wood,<span class='line-break'> </span> fixed a little <a href='../subjects/54' title='custard'>custard</a>, and eat <span class='line-break'> </span> by myself.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I guess I would of went to<span class='line-break'> </span> some of their homes but thought<span class='line-break'> </span> I might be in the way.  They<span class='line-break'> </span> might be going some where<span class='line-break'> </span> and I would be a bother.<span class='line-break'> </span> Be sides I did not feel like <span class='line-break'> </span> walkin far.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7897' title='Janie Gravely'>Miss Janie Gravely</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/8021' title='Aubrey Hendricks'>Mr Aubra<span class='line-break'> </span> Hendricks</a> come here tonight to<span class='line-break'> </span> see Thelma &amp; Mary.  They were<span class='line-break'> </span> gone to <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lee Brumfields</a>.  <a href='../subjects/51' title='Jack Harvey'>Jack<span class='line-break'> </span> Harvey</a> come after them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1116">
<h3><a name="page-1116">Monday, December 29, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> morning &amp; a little<span class='line-break'> </span> snow.  Clear this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7350' title='Thelma Brumfield'>Thelma</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/216' title='Mary Brumfield'>Mary</a> and I went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/335' title='Margaret Brumfield'>Mag Brumfields</a> and spent the day.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> carried us and come after<span class='line-break'> </span> us.  Mag had as nice a <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a><span class='line-break'> </span> as I ever set down to.  <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Rees</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7656' title='Paul'>Paul</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7390' title='Smith'>Smith</a> and <a href='../subjects/308' title='Hugh Brumfield'>Hugh Brumfield</a><span class='line-break'> </span> was there.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> staid at home with the<span class='line-break'> </span> children.  <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>The baby</a> is so cross<span class='line-break'> </span> that there is no doing anything with<span class='line-break'> </span> her.  I am sorry for her &amp; Josie<span class='line-break'> </span> two.  Josie looks worn and tiered.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/59' title='Charles Harvey'>Charles Harvey</a> was home today.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/1630' title='Virginia Harvey'>Virginia Harvey</a> come to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/335' title='Margaret Brumfield'>Mags</a> a few minutes this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Tonight Ben &amp; Thelma &amp; Mary <span class='line-break'> </span> has gone to <a href='../subjects/7965' title='Graves Moses'>Graves Moses</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> They are haveing a <a href='../subjects/48' title='party'>party</a><span class='line-break'> </span> there tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1117">
<h3><a name="page-1117">Tuesday, December 30, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A very <a href='../subjects/61' title='wind'>windy</a> morning but<span class='line-break'> </span> a good evening.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7349' title='Evelyn Brumfield'>Evylin Brumfield</a> came last night<span class='line-break'> </span> a bout nine oclock.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; the<span class='line-break'> </span> girls come home this morning<span class='line-break'> </span> at half passed four<span class='line-break'> </span> We were all at home at <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a><span class='line-break'> </span> Today we had a nice <a href='../subjects/140' title='turkey'>turkey</a><span class='line-break'> </span> for dinner it was <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josies</a><span class='line-break'> </span> turkey.  And <a href='../subjects/8022' title='mince pie'>mince pie</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/37' title='cakes'>cakes</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/54' title='custard'>custard</a><span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening Jim <a href='../subjects/7631' title='hunting'>hunted</a><span class='line-break'> </span> with <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> a while then<span class='line-break'> </span> they <a href='../subjects/7667' title='burning plantbeds'>set a plant bed on<span class='line-break'> </span> fire</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben &amp; <a href='../subjects/7349' title='Evelyn Brumfield'>Evylin</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7350' title='Thelma Brumfield'>Thelma</a> &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/216' title='Mary Brumfield'>Mary</a> and <a href='../subjects/59' title='Charles Harvey'>Charley</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/1630' title='Virginia Harvey'>Virginia<span class='line-break'> </span> Harvey</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7240' title='Jim Power'>Jim Powers</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to a <a href='../subjects/19' title='dance'>dance</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> did not<span class='line-break'> </span> go on account of <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>the little baby</a><span class='line-break'> </span> The baby has bin better<span class='line-break'> </span> today than she was yesterday<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim has gone to the store tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1118">
<h3><a name="page-1118">Wednesday, December 31, 1919</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7631' title='hunting'>hunting</a>.  A lot of the grand<span class='line-break'> </span> children come to night and a<span class='line-break'> </span> few others.  <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate</a> and <a href='../subjects/52' title='Irvin Harvey'>Irvin</a> walked<span class='line-break'> </span> down here.  The children played <span class='line-break'> </span> until midnight.  They all<span class='line-break'> </span> said that they had a good<span class='line-break'> </span> time.  I did not have anything<span class='line-break'> </span> to do with the askin them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I am glad that the Xmas<span class='line-break'> </span> is gone.  Every day is preshious<span class='line-break'> </span> but the excuse for doing<span class='line-break'> </span> nothing is gone.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We have had good wood <span class='line-break'> </span> and have had good <a href='../subjects/14' title='fire'>fires</a><span class='line-break'> </span> for which I want to be <span class='line-break'> </span> thankful.  I have not bin<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a> a day so that I could<span class='line-break'> </span> not go a bout.<span class='line-break'> </span> I feel sad to think <span class='line-break'> </span> of this being the last<span class='line-break'> </span> time that I will <span class='line-break'> </span> write in <a href='../subjects/7632' title='diary'>this book</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> one oclock 1920</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1119">
<h3><a name="page-1119">Memoranda (i)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>November the 24 1919<span class='line-break'> </span> I paid <a href='../subjects/7971' title='Anna Callands'>Anna Callans</a><span class='line-break'> </span> $5 00 Dollars on <a href='../subjects/7963' title='Bessie Callands'>Bessie</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> wages</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1120">
<h3><a name="page-1120">Memoranda (ii)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>April the 4 I let <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Sam<span class='line-break'> </span> Owen</a> have $50 dollars to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> May the 23rd let <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> have<span class='line-break'> </span> three dollars to pay Sam <span class='line-break'> </span> Owens <a href='../subjects/8024' title='taxes'>taxes</a></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1121">
<h3><a name="page-1121">Memoranda (iii)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p><a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/128' title='tobacco sale'>solde</a> a load of <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a><span class='line-break'> </span> in <a href='../subjects/973' title='Danville, Virginia'>Danville</a> Febuary the 14th 1919<span class='line-break'> </span> for $3:86 dollars.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> February the 19th 1919<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin Smith</a> solde a curing<span class='line-break'> </span> of tobacco for Ben for<span class='line-break'> </span> $2:19 dollars.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/8025' title='Belle (sow)'>Bells</a> <a href='../subjects/370' title='pigs'>pigs</a> came June the 2nd 1918.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/8026' title='Lucy (cow)'>Lucys</a> calf came December <span class='line-break'> </span> the 2nd 1919.</p>
</div>
